Yesu kawapetela wanhu mbuli yake kwa masimwe yamwenga fana ino, kawalongela viya viwodaha kuvimanya.
Ivo Yesu kalonga, “Vinhu va Kaisali mwing'heni Kaisali, vinhu va Mulungu mwing'heni Mulungu.” Nawo wamwazanya ng'hani.
Mafalisayo wamwenga weza kwa Yesu, wandusa kuibishila na Yesu. Wakala wolonda kumgeza, ivo wamulonda yatende chilaguso cha mauzauza kulawa kwa Mulungu.
Nowalongela kweli, sizakung'wa kaidi divai ya nzabibu mbaka siku ija vondaniing'we divai ya sambi muna Ufalume wa Mulungu.”
Wanhu iwadanganike vondawazilibuke, hawezasola wala kusoligwa, wezakuwa fana wasenga wa kuulanga.
Wamwenga wandusa kumtemela mate, wamgubika yameso, na wamtowa na kumulongela, “Lagula, yelihi yakutowile!” Iviya wakalizi wamsola na kumtowa mang'huwa.
Wakulu wa nhambiko na wafundiza Malagilizo vawahulike yayo, wandusa kulonda nzila ya kumkoma Yesu. Mbali wakala wamdumba kwaviya lung'husesa lose lukanganyika kwa mafundizo yake.
Na ung'hali uhelelo haunafika, Mbuli Inogile yolondeka kupetigwa kwa ziisi zose.
Mbali waja wenevale wezakuwa wohawapetigwa, na waja wohawapetigwa wezakuwa wenevale.”
Wawawona wanahina wake wamwenga woja ndiya kuno makono hayanawigwe, hawanawile makono fana Mafalisayo viwolonda wanhu wanawe.
Viwakalile mwiinzila, waiting'hana na munhu imwe yatangigwe Saimoni, munhu wa isi ya Chilene, tati yawo Alekizanda na Lufo. Munhu iyo kakala kolawa kumgunda koita kudibululu. Wakalizi wamshulutiza yausole msalaba wa Yesu.
Wafika mudibululu da Besisaida, wanhu wemwenga wamgalila Yesu munhu chipofu na wamulamba yandalise.
Lusita ulo Yesu viyakalile kolonga, wanhu wamwenga weza kulawa ukaye kwa Yailo, ija mkulu wa kaye ya kutosela na wamulongela, “Mndele wako kadanganika. Habali kogendelela kumgaza mfundiza?”
Yesu viyaonile lung'husesa lwa wanhu wokongezeka kuulongozi kumwake, kambwakila chinyamkela ija, “Weye chinyamkela wa ububu na unziwi, nokulongela mulawe imwana ino, sekeumwingile kaidi!”
Kamulamba ng'hani Yesu sekeyawawinge kunze mwa isi ija.
“Kolonda uchitende choni, weye Yesu wa Nazaleti? Vino kwiza kuchikomeleza? Nokumanya weye iyo Yelile wa Mulungu!”
Wamuyawala chiwalo cha langi ya zambalau, na waluka kombelo da mfalume dodilukigwe na miwa, wadika muna iditwi da Yesu.
Bahobaho mndele ija kenuka na kandusa kugenda. Mndele iyo kakala na miyaka longo na midi. Chinhu icho vichilawilile, wanhu wazanywa ng'hani.
Wanahina wake hawavimanyile bule mbuli iyo, mbali wadumba kumuuza.
Yesu kambwakila chinyamkela ija, “Nyamala! Lawa kwa munhu ino!”
Bahobaho tata wa mwana ija kalonga kwa dizi kulu, “Nohuwila mbali uhuwilo wangu mdodo. Nitaze niwe na uhuwilo mkulu!”
Na wanhu wose wa dibululu waiting'hana hana ulwivi lwa ikaye.

Yesu kakala kuchisogo mwiingalawa, kagona na kadika ditwi jake mumto. Wanahina wamulamusa, wamulongela, “Mfundiza, hugesa cheye vichidanganika?”
Yesu viyakalile kokwela mwiingalawa, munhu ija yoyakalile na vinyamkela kamulamba wahite wose.
Yesu kakala hasi, kawalanga waja wanahina wake longo na waidi na kuwalongela, “Munhu yoyose yoyolonda kuwa wa mwanduso, kolondeka yawe wa kuuhelelo, na yawe mtumwa wa wose.”
Viyalulekile ulung'husesa lwa wanhu, kengila mnyumba, wanahina wake wamulongela yawafambulile simwe diya.

Maabaho Yesu kasegela, baho kahita mwiisi yili habehi na dibulu da Tilo. Uko kengila mnyumba na halondile munhu yoyose yavimanye kuwa kahaja, mbali hadahile bule kuifisa.

Maabaho kabwela kaidi, kawafika wanahina wake wagona, meso yawo yakala vuwevuwe. Nawo hawavimanyile bule da kumulongela.
Goza chimulole iyo Chilisito, Mfalume wa Isilaeli! Yahulumuke sambi mu msalaba, na cheye chizamuhuwila!” Na hata waja wanhu waidi wawambigwe mu misalaba hamwe nayo wamuliga.
Bahobaho Yesu kavimanya kuwa udahi umulawa. Basi kaluhindukila lung'husesa lwa wanhu na kuluuza, “Yelihi yoyadalise walo jangu?”
Yesu kawalongela wanhu wakale hasi. Kayasola yaja yamagate saba, kamwing'ha Mulungu hewela. Maabaho kayamogola yamagate yaja na kuweng'ha wanahina wake waweng'he wanhu, na wawo watenda ivo.
Mbali wawo hawamwidike kwaviya muinzila wakala woibishila yelihi yeli mkulu mgati yawo.
Kawawona wanahina wake wogayagaya kutowa zing'hafi, kwaviya beho kulu dikala dowabweleza kuwalawile. Nzogolo zikwika, Yesu kawahitila kuno kogenda mchanyha ya mazi. Kalonda kuwafosa,
Maabaho wamuwamba mu msalaba na wayigolela viwalo vake kwa kutowa mhiya kulamula yelihi yapate chilihi.
Ulinga na mbeyu ya haladali yili ndodo kufosa mbeyu zose zili mwiisi.
Na dilagizo da kaidi kwa ukulu ijo dino, ‘Mulonde miyago fana vowiilonda mwenyewo.’ Habule lagilizo kulu kufosa yano maidi.”
Beho kulu dilawilila na kutibula mazi, mawimbi yandusa kwingila mwiingalawa na mbaka ilonda kumema mazi.
Yesu na wanahina wake wabaguka muulwanda lwa Galilaya, wanhu wamsondelela. Walawa mwi izisi za Galilaya, Yudeya,
Kwaviya chinhu chochose chochifisigwe chizawoneka, na chinhu chochose chochigubikigwe chizagubuligwa.
Mbali munhu imwe mwa iwaja wemile haja kalava mwele wake, kamtowa mtumwa wa mkulu wa nhambiko na kumkanha gutwi jake.
Hamwande Yesu kawalawilila wanahina longo na imwe viwakalile woja. Kawabwakila kwaviya wakala wabule uhuwilo, na kwaviya wakala wadala kuwatogola wanhu waja wowamuonile viyamalile ya kuzilibuka.
Maabaho mami yake Yesu na wandugu zake weza Wema hanze, wamtuma munhu yakamtange Yesu.
Yesu kamulongela, “Habali kolonga uhadaha! Niye nokulongela, yose yodahika kumwake yoyohuwila.”
Kawalongela, “Ino iyo damu yangu ya lagano ikwitika kwa ichimu cha wanhu wengi.
Maabaho Yesu kayasola yaja yamagate matano na somba waidi, kalola kuchanyha kuulanga na kumwing'ha Mulungu hewela. Maabaho kayamogola yamagate yaja, kaweng'ha wanahina wake wawagolele wanhu. Viyaviya kawagolela wose waja somba waidi.
Na wanhu wadile wakala wafosa magana malongo mane. Yesu kawalaga wanhu.
Wanhu wakalile ofosa mwiinzila watingisa matwi yawo na kumuliga Yesu, walonga, “Mwee! Weye mwene kuibena Kaye ya Mulungu na kuizenga kwa siku nhatu!
Na habule munhu yoguma divai ya sambi mwii mifuko ya mbende ya umwaka. Kwaviya yahatenda ivo, divai ya sambi izaitula mbende, na divai izakwitika na mifuko izabanangika. Mbali divai ya sambi igumigwa mwii mbende ya sambi.”
Mbali Yesu kawagomesa kumulongela munhu yoyose kuwa yeye yalihi.
Ichigulogulo vichifikile, wanhu wamgalila Yesu watamu wawo na wose wowakalile na vinyamkela.
Wafundiza Malagilzo wamwenga wakalile Mafalisayo viwamuwonile koja na “weli na uhasanyi” na wasola kodi, wawauza wanahina wake, “Habali koja na wanhu fana wano?”
Wanhu wengi wezakwiza na kulonga, niye niiyo! Na wezawavwizila wengi.
Yesu kakala uko Besaniya mwii kaye ya Saimoni, munhu yoyakalile na dikulu umwaka. Na viyakalile koja, mwanamke imwe yakalile na nyhupa ya mavuta yonung'hila ya bei ng'hulu ng'hani keza. Kaifungula na kangidila Yesu mavuta yayo nditwi.
Ivo fana ufalume wa Lufyende wahaigola wenyewo, uzagwa na kufika hauhelelo.
Wafika Yelusalemu, Yesu kengila mwii Kaye ya Mulungu. Maabaho kandusa kuwawinga wanhu wakalile wochuuza na kugula vinhu umo. Kavihindula ivilingo va wanhu wakalile wovunja hela, na vigoda va wanhu wakalile wochuuza nziwa.
Wakulu wa nhambiko wamsitaka Yesu kwa mbuli nyingi.
Yelusalemu, na Idumeya, na umwambu wa Yolodani, na banzi za Tilo na Sidoni. Wose wawo weza kwa Yesu kwaviya wahulika mbuli zayatendile Yesu.
Siku izo, Yesu keza kulawa mudibululu da Nazaleti, mwiisi ya Galilaya, na kabatizigwa na Yohana muna ulwanda wa Yolodani.
Muna siku za mkulu wa nhambiko Abiyasali, Daudi kengila mwii Kaye ya Mulungu na kuyaja yamagate yoyalavigwe kwa Mulungu. Yamagate yayo yalondeka kudigwa na walava nhambiko muhala. Mbali Daudi kayaja na maabaho kaweng'ha wayage.”
Mbali Yesu kanyamala hupi, halongile mbuli yoyose. Mkulu wa nhambiko kamuuza kaidi, “Vino weye iyo Chilisito, Mwana wa Mulungu yotemiligwa mate?”
Kalonga ivo kwaviya Yesu kamulongela, “Chinyamkela mulawe munhu ino!”
Mbali zuwa vidilawile, diisoma minoga, na kwaviya haikalile na mizizi, inyala.
Mumuhulika vayamuligile Mulungu! Mweye mwonaze?” Wose wamtagusa yakomigwe.
Meso munayo mbali hamuwona? Magutwi munayo mbali hamuhulika? Wala hamukumbuka?
Na mudizuwa da kenda imisi, Yesu kalila kwa dizi kulu, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabakitani?” Fambulo jake ni, “Mulungu wangu, Mulungu wangu, habali kunileka?”
Iviya umulonde Mulungu kwa moyo wako wose na kwa hakili zako zose na kwa nguvu zako zose, na kumulonda miyago fana vouwilonda mwenyewo vinoga kufosa kumulavila zabihu Mulungu.”
Maabaho keka ditwi ijo muna ichano, kamgalila mndele ija, nayo kamwing'ha mami yake.
Wandika vitala vake vino, “Mfalume wa Wayahudi”.
One Mndewa sigambe yahunguze siku izo, habule munhu yonda yahone. Mbali kwa ichimu cha wanhu waja Mndewa woyawasagule, kayahunguza zisiku izo.
“Mnhegeleze, Hakala na munhu yoyohanda kahita kumiza mbeyu.
Yesu viyakalile kofundiza mwii Kaye ya Mulungu, kawauza, “Habali wafundiza Malagilizo wolonga Chilisito ni mwana wa Daudi?
Nowalongela kweli, munhu yoyose yonda yaweng'he nhungo ya mazi ya kung'wa kwaviya mweye mwa wanhu wa Chilisito, kezahokela gweko jake.
Yesu kamulola kamulonda na kamulongela kuhungukilwa na mbuli imwe. Hita ukagule vose vuuli navo, uweng'he hela ngayengaye, na weye kwizakuwa na ngama uko kuulanga. Maabaho wize unisondelele.
Mndewa kachitenda chinhu chino, na chiwa chinhu cha mwazanyo ng'hani kumwetu.’ ”
Petili viyakalile yang'hali muluhelengo, mwanamke imwe yakalile msang'hani wa mkulu wa nhambiko keza.
Maabaho Yuda Isikaliyoti, imwe wa waja longo na waidi, kahita kwa wakulu wa nhambiko muladi yamuhinduke Yesu kumwawo.
Kawauza kaidi, “Na vinimogole yaja yamagate saba na kuweng'ha wanhu magana malongo mane, mudondola vigelo vingahi va masigavu?” Wamwidika, “Chidondola vigelo saba.”
Viwamalile kumkeweza, wamvula viwalo va langi ya zambalau, wamuyawala viwalo vake. Amalabaho wamulava kunze muladi wamuwambe mu msalaba.
Mbali Yesu kahinduka, kawalola wanahina wake na kumbwakila Petili, “Segela kuchisogo changu, Lufyende! Kwaviya magesa yako siyo ya Mulungu, ila ya chiunhu!”
Yesu kawedika, “Mami yangu yalihi? Na wandugu zangu walihi?”
“Na mweye muyilole. Mwizagwiligwa na kugaligwa kwiichitala. Mwizatowigwa mwii zikaye za kutosela. Mwizagaligwa haulongozi ha watawala na wafalume kwa ichimu changu, muladi muwalongele Mbuli Inogile.
Yesu kawalongela, “Mweye wose mwizakimbila na kundeka, fana Maandiko Yelile viyolonga, ‘Nizamtowa imdimi, na ng'hondolo wezapwililika.’
Kawalongela vose kwa masimwe mbali kakala yaidumwe na wanahina kawalongela chila chinhu funhufunhu.
Yuda ija imuhinduka, kakala kalwing'ha chilaguso lung'huse ulwo kuwa, “Ija yondanimnonele iyo iyo mgwileni, mumgale na mumkalize sekeyasulupuke.”
Maabaho Yesu kawagomesa kumulongela munhu yoyose mbuli ino. Mbali vayagendelele kuwagomesa, niivo vawagendelele kuipwililisa mbuli iyo.
Viyamhile walo da Yesu, bahobaho damu ileka kumulawa, nayo kaihulika kuwa kahona.
‘Kwa ichimu icho mulume keza muleka tati yake na mami yake, nayo kezailumba na muke wake,
Nawo wawalongela fana Yesu vayawalongele, na wanhu waja wawaleka wahite.
Yesu kamulongela yahite na kumgomesa ng'hani,
na Yuda Isikaliyoti, yoyamuhinduke Yesu.
Wafundiza Malagilizo wamwenga wakalile baho wandusa kuyiuza wenyewo,
Wanahina waja wahita na kumuwona mwana chihongwe kafungigwa hana ulwivi wa kaye. Vawakalile womfungula,
Yesu kapata usungu muumoyo, kalonga, “Mbona wanhu wa ulelwa uno wolonda vilaguso? Nowalongelani kweli, habule chilaguso chonda weng'higwe.”
Yesu kamulongela munhu yahololile mkono, “Izo hano haulongozi.”
Wanahina wa Yohana Mbatizi na wanahina wa Mafalisayo wakala wofunga kuja. Wanhu wamwenga wamwitila Yesu na kumuuza, “Habali wanahina wa Yohana na wanahina wa Mafalisayo wofunga kuja, mbali wanahina wako hawafunga kuja?”
Ivo wamwidika Yesu, “Cheye hachivimanya.” Yesu kawalongela, “Na niye iviya siwalongela bule kwa udahi wa yelihi notenda yano yose.”
Pilato kawauza, “Vino mwolonda nimulekele mfalume wa Wayahudi?”
Petili kakala komsondelela Yesu kwa kutali, kengila muluhelengo lwa kaye ya mkulu wa nhambiko. Kakala hamwe na wakalizi, kokotela moto.
Mbali muvimanye vino, Mwana wa Munhu kana udahi wa kusegeza uhasanyi mwiisi.” Maabaho kamulongela munhu yahololile,
Udongo wenyewo wozitenda mbeyu kukula goya na kwima matunda, teng'hu diyani maabaho mada, na kuuhelelo uhemba wokung'hunha.
Ivo vinyamkela wamulamba Yesu, “Uchigale kuzinguluwe, na uchilekelele chiwengile wawo.”
Bahobaho Yesu kawalagiliza wanahina wake wakwele mwiingalawa wahite Besisaida. Yeye kakala kolulaga lung'husesa lwa wanhu wasegele.
Yesu kawauza, “Munayo magate mengahi?” Wamwidika, “Chinayo saba.”
Yesu kawedika, “Hamusomile chiya Daudi chayatendile na wayage vawakalile na nzala?
Baho kukala na mwanamke imwe yoyakalile na utamu wa kulawa damu kwa miyaka longo na midi.
Wanahina wazanywa ng'hani, wandusa kwiiuza, “Vino yelihi yonda yadahe kulopoligwa?”
Yesu kalonga kaidi, “Vino Ufalume wa Mulungu chiulinganyize na choni? Simwe dilihi donda nisang'hanile kuufambula?
“Vondamuwone ‘Wihi wa ubananzi’ wima hanhu si hake (munhu yosoma yavimanye), waja weli mwii isi ya Yudeya wakimbilile kumilima.
Mbali chipindi chizakwiza munhu yoyosola vondayasegezigwe kumwawo. Baho wezafunga kuja.
Valeni vilatu, mbali sekemsole viwalo vimwenga.
Ndugu kezamuhinduka ndugu yake yakomigwe, na tata kezamuhinduka mwanage yakomigwe. Wana wezawalema na kuwakoma tati zawo na mami zawo.
Ndugu wose saba wamsola muke iyo mbali hawalekile wana bule. Kuuhelelo, muke ija iviya kadanganika.
Yesu viyengile mnyumba, wanahina wake wamuuza viyakalile yaidumwe, “Habali cheye hachidahile bule kumulava chinyamkela?”
Yesu kengila mnyumba na kuwalongela, “Habali motenda tibwilitibwili na kulila? Mndele hadanganike bule, kagona tu!”
Wamgala mwana chihongwe iyo kwa Yesu, wavitandika viwalo vawo mchanyha yake, na Yesu kakala mchanyha ya mwana chihongwe iyo.
Kukala na wanhu wengi wowakalile wokwiza na kusegela, mbaka Yesu na wanahina wake hawapatile bule nyafasi ya kuja ndiya. Ivo kawalongela, “Chiteni chiidumwe hanhu helibule wanhu muladi mukahumule chidogo.”
Ivo wakala mwiivibumbila va wanhu gana-gana na va wanhu malongo matano-matano.
Wamwenga walinga fana mbeyu zihandigwe muna yamabwe. Wahahulika mbuli, bahobaho woihokela kwa deng'ho.
Ivo chiya chayalumbilize Mulungu, munhu sekeyachigole.”
Chipindi icho, kukala na munhu yotangigwa Balaba. Iyo kakala kafungigwa hamwe na wanhu wamwega kwa kutenda usonga magida na kuwakoma wanhu vikukalile na magodogodo.
Mbali yahahandigwa, yokula na kuwa biki kulu kufosa mibiki yose. Dokwika matambi makulu ng'hani, mbaka ndege weli kuulanga wodaha kuzenga mvulu zawo muna yamatambi yake.”
Wanhu wamwenga wakala wolonda chimu cha kumgwila Yesu. Ivo wamulola fana kezamuhonya mwii Isiku ya Mhumulo.
Mwanamke iyo kakala Muyunani, yalekigwe mudibululu da Silofoinike uko Siliya. Kampula Yesu yamulave mndele wake chinyamkela.
Ivo vimuibena mbuli ya Mulungu kwa mafundizo yomuihokeleza. Iviya motenda vinhu vingi vifanile na ivo.”
Mulonde Mndewa Mulungu wako kwa moyo wako wose, na kwa muhe wako wose, na kwa hakili zako zose, na kwa nguvu zako zose.’
Kahita kuulongozi chidogo, kayibwanha hasi na katosa, one ihadahika sekeyafosele lusita luja lwa manhesa.
Chilochilo, wakulu wa nhambiko waiting'hana na walala na wafundiza Malagilizo na balaza jose, waitogolela kumgala Yesu kwa Pilato. Ivo wandaza wangala na kumwing'ha Pilato.
Maabaho keza munhu imwe mkulu wa kaye ya kutosela zina jake Yailo. Viyamuwonile Yesu, kaibwanha hasi muyamagulu yake,
Imwe wa wafundiza Malagilizo kafika na kuhulika Yesu koisosokanya na Masadukayo. Viyaonile Yesu kawedika goya, kamuuza, “Muna yamalagilizo yose, lagilizo dilihi dikulu kufosa yose?”
Vizifosile siku sita, Yesu kawasola Petili, Yakobo na Yohana, kahita nawo hachanyha muumulima mtali waidumwe. Baho lukuli lwa Yesu lugaluka haulongozi hawo.
Mbali Yesu kaumanya udelenya wawo. Kawauza, “Mbona mwonigeza? Ngalileni hela niilole.”
Maabaho viwakomeleze kwimba wila, wahita kumulima wa Mizaituni.
Maabaho wanhu wezaniona niye, Mwana wa Munhu naheza mmawingu kwa udahi mkulu na utunhizo.
Miyanza mingi chinyamkela kageza kungwisa muumoto hebu munayamazi muladi yamkome. One uhadaha, uchiwonele ubazi na uchitaze!”
Munawo ngaengae siku zose, na mwodaha kuwataza lusita lolose lumulonda. Mbali hamwizakuwa hamwe na niye siku zose.
Yesu kawedika, “Kweli Eliya kezakwiza teng'hu na kusasala chila chinhu goya. Mbali, habali yandikigwa Mwana wa Munhu kezagazigwa ng'hani na kulemigwa?
Kawalongela, “Hiteni mwiisi yose mkapetele Mbuli Inogile kwa wanhu wose.
Mbali Yesu kawalongela, “Chihite mwii vibululu vimwenga vili mmabehi na hano. Uko nako nolondeka kuwapetela wanhu Mbuli Inogile, kwaviya icho niicho chinizile.”
Yesu kamulongela, “Nokulongela kweli, ichilo cha diyelo, yang'hali nzogolo hanakwika miyanza midi, kwizanibela miyanza mitatu.”
Wanhu wamtegeleze wazanywa ng'hani kwa mafundizo yake, kwaviya hafundize fana wafundiza Malagilizo, mbali kakala yofundiza fana munhu yana udahi.
Wanhu wengi wambwakila na wamulongela yanyamale. Mbali yeye kagendelela kutanga kwa dizi kulu, “Mwana wa Daudi, niwonele ubazi!”
Vino vose vihile volawa mgati muumoyo wa munhu, navo niivo mwambula mwiko munhu.”
Wanhu wazanywa ng'hani, walonga, “Katenda yose vinogile. Kawatenda vinziwi wahulike na mabubu walonge!”
Wafika kaidi Yelusalemu. Yesu viyakalile yoita mwii Kaye ya Mulungu, wakulu wa nhambiko na wafundiza Malagilizo na walala wamwitila.
Kwaviya hachingila muumoyo mbali chokwingila mmunda, maabaho cholawa kunze ya lukuli.” Viyalongile ivo, Yesu kazitogola ndiya zose kudigwa.
Kwaviya muumoyo wa munhu molawa magesa yehile na ugoni na ubavi na kukoma na kuigona na wihi
Niye nowabatiza kwa mazi, mbali yeye kezawabatiza kwa Muhe Yelile.”
Yesu kawedika, “Mweye mwing'higwa kuzimanya mbuli zifisigwe za Ufalume wa Mulungu. Mbali waja weli kunze wozihulika mbuli izo kwa masimwe,
Fana munhu yahambonela chinyala niye na mbuli zangu muna ulelwa uno wa uzinzi na uhasanyi, niye, Mwana wa Munhu nizamuwonela chinyala munhu iyo vondanize muna utunhizo wa Tati yangu, hamwe na wasenga wa kuulanga welile.
Mwanamke ija kedika, “Mndewa, mbali hata zimbwa zozikalile hasi ha imeza zoja ndiya za wana zozisigale!”
Nayo kawasagula wanhu longo dimwe na waidi, kawalanga watumigwa. Kawalongela, “Niwasagula mweye mukale na niye. Maabaho nizawatuma mkawapetele wanhu.
Bunu ni bwambilo bhwe misango jo bhwana eja Yesu Kristo, omwana wa Nyamuanga.
Lwa kutyo jandikilwe no mulagi Isaya, “Lola, enimutuma omukosi wani imbele yao, oumwi unu kajo okuchuma-chuma injila yao.
Obhulaka bhwo munu unu kabhilikila ibhala, “Ichumwe kisi injila ya Lata bhugenyi; Jigololwe kisi jinjila jae”.
Yohana ejile, nabhatija ibhala no kusimula obhubhatijo bhwo kuta no kwiswalililwa ebhikayo.
Echalo chona echa Yudea na abhanu bhona abha Yerusalemu bhagendele ewae. Bhaliga nibhabhatija nage mu mugela gwa Yordani, nibhegamba ebhibhibhi bhyebhwe.
Yohana aliga nafwala echifwalo bhwo bhufufi bhwa Ingamia na lifwata lyo lwai muchibhunu chae, na aliga nalya jinsige no bhuki bhwe mwila.
Asimuye no kwaika, “Alio umwi unu kajokuja inyuma yani unu ankilile kula amanaga anye, nitana chibhalo nolwo okwinama emwalo no kusulumula jingoye je bhilato byae.
Anye nabhabhatijishe mu maji, mbe nawe omwene kabhabhatija emwe mu Mwoyo Mwelu.”
Munaku ejo jabhonekene ati Yesu ejile okusoka Nazareti ya Galilaya, mbe nabhatijibhwa na Yohana mu mugela gwa Yordani.
Mu mwanya Yesu ejile enamuka okusoka mu maji, alolele olwile nilugabhanyika nabha abhwelu na Mwoyo namwikila namujako ali uti njibha.
No bhulaka nibhusoka mu lwile, “Awe uli mwana wani omwendwa. Enikondelelwa muno nawe.”
Okumala ao nao Mwoyo namusinyilisha okuja ibhala.
Abheeyo ibhala naku makumi gana, nasakwa na Shetani. Aliga ali na jityanyi je mwila jindulu, na Bhamalaika nibhamufulubhendela.
Oli ejile Yohana agwatibhwa, Yesu ejile Galilaya nalasha omusango gwo bhwana ogwa Nyamuanga,
Naika,”Omwanya gwakumila, no bhukama bhwa Nyamuanga bhwelila ayei. Mute no kwikilisha mu musango gwo bhwana.”
Anu aliga nalabha kunjejekela ya Galilaya, amulolele Simoni na Andrea owabho Simoni nibhatega emitego jebhwe mu nyanja, kwo kubha bhaliga bhategi.
Yesu abhabhwiliye, “Muje, mundubhe, ne enibhakola kubha bhategi bha bhanu.”
Ao nao nibhajisiga emitego nibhamulibha.
Mu mwanya Yesu ejile alibhatao kula kutoto, amulolele Yakobho omwana wa Jebhedayo na Yohana omumula wabho; bhaliga mu bhwato nibhasobhola emitego.
Okwiya nabhabhilikila na bhene nibhamusiga esemwene webhwe Jebhedayo mu bhwato na bhakosi bhanu bhaliga bhaliga bho kuliywa, nibhamulubha.
Mbe bhejile bhakinga Kaperinaumu, mu lunaku olwa isabhato, Yesu engie mulikofyanyisho no kwiigisha.
Eliigisho lyae lyabhatang'ang'anyishe, lwa kutyo aliga nabheigisha lwo munu unu ali no bhutulo na atali lwa abhandiki.
Mu mwanya ogwo ogwo aliga alio omunu mulikofyanyisho lyebhwe unu aliga no musambhwa mujabhi, aliga nakunga,
naika, “Chili na chinuki echokukola nawe, Yesu owa Nanjareti? Wijile okuchisimagisha? Enikumenya awe nawega. Awe nu Mulengelesi enyele owa Nyamuanga!”
Yesu naligonya lisambwa elyo no kwaika, “Jibila na umusokemo!”
Mbe lisambwa lijabhi elyo nilimugwisha ansi mu mwanya ogwo namusokako nalila kwo bhulaka bhwa ingulu.
Mbe abhanu bhone nibhatang'ang'ala, kwibhyo nibhabhushanya bhuli umwi, “Chinu Niki? Eliigisho eyaya elyo bhutulo? Kalagilila amasambwa amajabhi ona agamuyana echibhalo!”
Emisango jo kulubhana no mwene nijitalala bhuli ebhala mu musi gwona ogwa Galilaya.
Na bhwangu wejile auluka mulikofyanyisho, bhengie mu nyumba ya Simoni na Andrea bhali Yakobho na Yohana.
Mbe woli nyabhuko Simoni aliga amamile ali mulwae wo muswija, bhwangu nibhamubhwila Yesu emisango jae.
Kwibhyo ejile, amugwatile no kubhoko, no kumwinamusha ingulu; Omuswija nigumusokako na namba okubhafulubhendela.
Kegolo eyo omwanya gwa lisubha lyalagae, bhamuletee ewae bhona bhanu bhaliga bhalwae, amwi na bhanu bhaliga bhaungilwe amasambwa.
Omusi gwona bhekofyanyishe amwi mu mulyango.
Abheulisishe bhwafu bhanu bhaliga bhalwae abha malwala ga bhuli mbaga no kusoshako amasambwa mafu, nawe atekilisishe amasambwa okwaika ku nsonga bhamumenyele.
Emukile katondo mumachelelesha, chichali chisute; asokeleo no kuja ebhala lyo bhiibhise no kusabhwa eyo.
Simoni na bhona bhanu bhaliga bhali amwi nage nibhamulubha.
Nibhamubhona mbe nibamubhwila, “Bhuli umwi kakuiga”.
Abhabhwiliye, “Chigende ebhala lindi, anja mu misi jinu jiindile, koleleki eyo one nitule okusimula. Niyo insonga nijile anu.”
Agendelee nalabha mu Galilaya Yona, nasimula mu mekofyanyisho gebhwe no kugonya amasambwa.
Omugege umwi namujako ku mwene. aliga namwilembeleja; Nafukama no kumubhwila, “Alabha owenda, outula okukola nibhe muanga.”
Nasindikwa ne chigogo, Yesu nagolola okubhoko kwae no kumukunyako,”Namubhwila, “Enenda. ubhe muanga.”
Ao nao ebhigege nibhimusokako, na eulisibhwe nabha muanga.
Yesu namukomelesha muno namubhwila agende bwangu,
Amubhwilie, “komelesha ati utakutula kwaika musango ku wona wona, mbe nawe genda, uje okwiyelesha ku mugabhisi, na usoshe echogo kulwo kwela ku bhinu Musa alagilie, kuti bhubhambasi ku bhene.”
Mbe nawe agendele no kwamba okumubhwila Bhuli umwi no kulasha muno omusango nolwo Yesu atatulile lindi okwingila mu musi gwo abhwelu bhwelu. Kwibyo enyanjile enyelela na bhanu nibhamujako ku mwene okusoka bhuli ebhala.
Ejile asubha Kaperinaumu jejile jatulao naku ntoto, nijungwibhwa ati aliga ali mu nyumba.
Abhanu bhafu muno bhaliga bhekofyanyishe alya na gwaliga gutalio mwanya lindi, nolwo ilya eya ku mulyango, Yesu naika omusango ku bhwene.
Okumala abhanu abhandi nibhamujako bhanu bhamuletele omunu unu aliga afue omubhili; Bhanu bhana bhaliga bhamubhatue.
Mu mwanya bhejile bhasingwa okumukingako kulwa insonga yo bhwafu bhwa bhanu, bhafumue olusala kwi bhala linu aliga ali. Bhejile bhamala okufumulao omwanya ngubhao, nibhesha obhulili bhunu omulwae ulya aliga amamileko.
Ejile alola elikilisha lyebhwe, Yesu namubhwila omufue wo mubhili ulya (omukombolike ulya), “Mwana wani, ebhikayo bhyao bhyeswalililwa.”
Mbe nawe abhandiki abhandi bhalya bhanu bhaliga bhenyajile alya bhebhusilisishe mu mioyo jebhwe,
Katula-atiki omunu unu okwaika kutya? Kafuma Nyamuanga! Niga unu katula okwiswalilila ebhikayo akabha atali Nyamuanga -la enyele?”
Okumala Yesu namenya mu mwoyo gwae chinu bhaliga nibheganilisha agati-gati yebhwe abhenela. Abhabhwilie, “kulwaki omwiganilisha kutya mu myoyo jemwe?
Echangu ni chiya kukila okwaika ku munu unu aliga afuye omubhili, 'Ebhikayo bhyao bhyeswalililwa' amwi okwaika 'Imelegulu, ugege obhulili bhwao, na ulibhate?'
Mbe nawe koleleki bhabhone okumenya ati Omwana wo munu ali no bhutulo bhwo kwiswalilila ebhikayo mu Chalo, amubhwiliye ulya unu aliga afue omubhili,
“Enikubhwila awe, imuka, gega echilago chao na ugende ika ewao.”
Nemelegulu ao nao nagega echilago chae, nalibhata naja anja ya inyumba imbele ya bhuli munu, kwibhyo bhona nibhatang'ang'ala no kumuyana Nyamuanga likusho, na nibhaika “Kata, chichaliga kubhona ebhisango bhyejabho bhinu.”
Agendele lindi kunjejekela yo mwalo, na liijo lyona lya bhanu bhejile kumwene, na bheigisha.
Anu aliganatula amulolele Lawi amwana wa Alfayo eyanjile ku lubhala lunu bhakumanyaga ligoti namubhwila,”Ndubha.” Emeleguyu no kumulubha.
No omwanya ogwo Yesu aliga na bhona ebhilyo mu nyumba ya Lawi, abhakumanya bha ligoti bhafu na bhanu bhebhikayo bhaliga ni bhalya na Yesu nabheigisibhwa bhae, kwo kubha bhaliga bhafu nabho bhamulubhile.
Omwanya abhandiki, abho bhaliga Masadukayo, bhejile bhalola ati Yesu aliga nalya na bhanu bhebhikayo na bhakumanya bha likodi, bhabhabhwilie abheigisibhwa bhae,”Kubhaki kalya na bhakumanya bha likodi na bhanu bhebhikayo bhikayo?”
Omwanya Yesu ejile ongwa kutyo abhabhwilie, “abhanu abho bhali no bhujima mu mubhili bhatakumweda omulagusi; ni bhanu bhalwae bhenyele nibho abhamukena. Nitejile kubhabhilikila bhanu bhalengelesi, nawe bhanu bhebhikayo.”
Abheigisibhwa bha Yohana na bhafarisayo bhaliga ne chisibho. Na bhanu abhandi bhejile kumwene no kumubhwila,” ku bhaki abheigsibhwa bha Yohana na bhafarisayo bhabhaga ne chisibho, nawe abheigisibhwa bhao bhatali na chisibho?
Yesu abhabhwilie,” Ati bhanu bhakalibhisibhwe mubhulegesi abhatula okubha nechisibho omwanya omutwasi bho bhulegesi achali amwi nabho? Anu bhachalindiliye no mutwasi wo bhwega achali amwi nabho nabho bhatakutula kubha ne chisibho.”
Mbe nawe jisiku ejija omwanya omutwasi wo bhulegesi akasosibhwao ku bhwene, na mu siku ejo abhwene abhabhaga ne chisibho.
Atalio Omunu unu kabhalila akabhala kayaya akaigubho kugubho ikokolo, kwibyo echilapa echibhanduka okusoka mwilyo echiyaya okubhanduka okusoka mu chikokolo no kubhao obhutemuke bhunene.
Atalio munu unu katula amanji go mujabibu omuyaya mu bhilibha bhikokolo, kefula natamo amaji go mujabibu ngabyata ebhiliba byona bhibhili amaji go mujabibu ne bhiliba ebhibhula. okumala kwae, tula amanji go mujabibu omuyaya mu bhilibha bhiyaya.”
Mu lunaku olwa isabhato Yesu alabhile mu masambu agandi, abheigisibhwa bhae bhambile okugega ebhyangala bhya ingano.
Mbe abhafarisayo nibhamubhwila, “Lola, kulwaki abhakola echinu chinu chitasikene ne chilagilo echa mulunaku olwa isabhato?”
Nabhabhwila, “Mutasomele chilya Daudi akolele anu aliga ali no bhukene no mweko-mwenene amwi na bhanu bhanu aliga ali amwi nage?
Lwakutyo agendele mu nyumba ya Nyamuanga mu mwanya gwa Abhiathali anu aliga ali Mugabhisi mukulu nalya omukate gunu gwaliga guteywe imbele- na lwa kutyo bhyaliga bhitasikene ne bhilagilo bhyo munu wona wona ati kalya atali abhagabhisi- nabhayana nolwo abhandi bhalya bhanu bhaliga amwi nage?”
Yesu aikile, “isabhato yakolelwe kulwa ingulu yo mwana munu, atali omwana munu kulwa ingulu ya isabhato.
kulwejo, Omwana wo munu ni Latabhugenyi, nolwo kulwa isabhato.”
Lindi engie mulikofyanyisho na mulya aliga alimo Omunu unu aliga ali no kubhoko kufuye.
Abhanu abhandi bhaliga nibhamulubhilila kwa ayei bhalole alabha katula okumwiulisha ku lunaku olwa isabhato koleleki ati bhamusitake.
Yesu amubhwilie omunu wo kubhoko kufuye, “Imuka na wimelegulu agati-gati ya liijo linu.”
Okumala nabhabhwila abhanu, “angu nijakisi okukola echikolwa che kisi mu lunaku olwa isabhato amwi okukola ganu gatali go bhulengelesi; Okukisha obhulame, amwi okwita?” Mbe nawe bhajibhiye jibhi.
Nabhalolelela kwe bhinyiga, nasulumbala kwa insonga yo bhukomee bhwe mioyo jebhwe, mbe namubhwila omunu ulya, “Golola okubhoko kwao”. Nakugolola Yesu namwiulisha okubhoko kwao.
Amafarisayo nibhaja anja no kwiya nibhakola jinjila amwi na bhaerode ingulu yae koleleki bhamwite.
Okumala Yesu, amwi na bheigisibhwa bhae, bhagendele ku mwalo, na liijo enene lya bhanu nilibhalubha nilisokelela Galilaya na bhuyaudi
no kusoka Yerusalemu na Idumaya na imbele ya Yordani no bhwikashanya bhwa Tiro na Sidoni, eijo enene, bhejile bhongwa bhuli chinu chinu aliga nakola, nibhamujako.
Mbe nabhabhwila abheigisibhwa bhae okwilabha obhwato bhutoto ingulu yo mwene ku nsonga ya liijo, koleleki ati bhasiga mukinda.
Kulwo kubha eulisishe bhafu, koleleki bhuli munu unu aliga ali na jinyako aliga nenda okumukingako koleleki amukunieko.
Ona ona emioyo ja masambwa amajabhi anu gamulolaga, gagwaga ansi imbele yae no kulila, na nibhaika, “Awe uli Mwana wa Nyamuanga”.
Abhalagilie kwo kumasha ati bhasiga kukola amenyekane
Agendele kwibhanga ingulu, nabhabhilikila bhanu aliga endele, okumala nibhaja ewae.
Nabhasola ekumi na bhabhili (bhanu abhilikie jintumwa), koleleki ati bhabhe amwi nage koleleki atule okubhatuma bhaje okusimula,
no kubha no bhuinga bhwo kusoshako amasambwa.
Mbe nabhasola ekumi na bhabhili: Simoni, unu ayanilwe lisina lya Petro,
Yakobho omwana wa Jebhedayo, na Yohana owabho Yakobho, unu ayanilwe lisina lya Bonagesi, abho ni, bhana bha libhaluka,
na Andrea, Filipo, Bartholomayo, Mathayo, Tomaso, Yakobho omwana wa Alfayo, Thadayo, Simoni Mkananayo,
na Yuda Iskariote, unu amulomee iniku.
Okumala agendelee ika, na liijo lya bhanu nibhaja amwi lindi, nolwo bhatakutula kulya nolwo mukate.
Imbaga yae yejile yongwa emisango ejo, nibhagenda okumugwata, kulwo kubha bhaikile ati, “amasala”
Abhandiki bhanu bhejile okusoka Yerusalemu bhaikile ati, “agwatibwa amasambwa Bhelijebhuli,” na “kwo mutungi wa masambwa kasoshako amasambwa”.
Yesu nabhabhilikila ewae no kwaika nabho kwe bhijejekanyo, “Ni kutiki Shetani katula okumusoshako Shetani?
Alabha obhukama bhukagabhanyika obhwenela, obhukama obhwo bhutakutula kusimbagilila.
Alabha inyumba ikagabhanyika yenyelela, inyumba eyo itakutula kusimbagilila.
Nolwo Shetani akemuka atasikene omwene kwo mwenela no kugabhanyika, atakutula kusimbagilila, na kabha akingile kubhutelo bhwae.
Mbe nawe atalio nolwo umwi unu katula okwingila mu nyumba yo munu unu ana managa no kwibha ebhinu bhyae obhutamubhoya owa manage kwamba, no kumala naola bhyona bhinu bhilimo mu nyumba.
Echimali enibhabhwila, ebhikayo bhone ebhya bhana bha bhanu bhiliswalililwa, amwi no kufuma kunu abhaika,
Mbe nawe wona wona unu alimufuma Mwoyo Mwelu atalisasilwa chimwi, nawe ana intambala ye chikayo cha kajanende”.
Yesu agwaikile gunu kwa insonga bhaliga nibhaika, “Ano mwoyo mujabhi”.
Okumala nyilamwene na bhabho bhejile no kwimelegulu anja. Nibhamutuma omunu, okumubhililkila.
Na liijo lya bhanu linu lyaliga linyanjile ayei nage nibhamubhwila, “nyokomwana na bhanyu bhali anja, abhakuiga awe”.
Abhasubhishe, “Mai wani niga na bhana bhasu?
Nabhalolelela bhanu bhaliga bhenyajile kenu bhamusingie, naika, “Lola, bhanu ni bhamai bhani na bhana bhasu!
wona wona unu kakola okwenda kwa Nyamuanga, omunu oyo niwo owasu, na muyala wasu na Mai wani”.
Ambile okwiigisha lindi ku njenjekela ya kumwalo. Na liijo lyafu nilikofyanya limusingie, nengila mu bhwato bhuli munyanja, no kwinyanja. Liijo lyona lyaliga liliku njenjekela ya kumwalo mulufuka.
Mbe nabheigisha masango mafu kwe bhijejekanyo, naika nabho kwa meigisho gae.
Mutegeleshe, omubhibhi ajie okubhibha.
Anu aliga nabhibha, jimbegu ejindi janguye ku njila, na jinyonyi nijija nijijilya.
Jimbegu ejindi janguye kwitale, anu galiga gatalio mayalu mafu. Okumala nijinywagala kwa insonga jaliga jitana mayalu go kwiya.
Mbe nawe lisubha lyejile lyauluka, janywagae, kulwo kubha jaliga jitana misi, nijuma.
Jimbegu ejindi jaguye agati-gati ya mawa. Amawa nigakula nigajiiganya, jitateyeko matwasyo gona gona
Jimbibho ejindi jaguye ku mayalu ge kisi na nijitwasha amatwasho kenu nijikula no kwiyongesha, nejindi nijitwasha kukila makumi gasatu, ne jindi makumi mukaga, nejindi egana”.
Na naika ati, wona wona unu Ali na matwi go kungwa, nongwe”.
Yesu anu aliga Ali enyelela, bhanu bhaliga ayei nage na bhalya ekumi na bhabhili bhamubhusishe okulubhana ne bhijejekanyo.
Naika ku bhene, “Kwimwe muyanilwe jibhisike jo bhukama bhwa Nyamuanga. Mbe nawe ku bhanu bhali anja bhuli chinu ni chijejekanyo,
koleleki bhakalola, ni chimali abhalola, mbe nawe bhatakulola, kulwejo ugwa bhakongwa ni chimali abhongwa, mbe nawe bhatakusombokelwa, labha jitali kutyo bhakaindukile na Nyamuanga akabheswalilie”.
Naika nabho, “Angu mutakuchimenya echijejekanyo chinu? Omutula atiki okumenya echijejekanyo ebhindi?
Omubhibhi abhibhile omusango.
Abhandi ni bhalya bhanu bhalagae ku mbali ya injila, Anu omusango gwabhibhilwe. Mbe bhejile bhagungwa, Shetani naja no kugugega omusango gunu gwabhibhilwe mu moyo jebhwe.
Na bhandi ni bhalya bhanu bhabhibhilwe kwi tale, bhanu, ungwa bhakagungwa omusango, kwo bhwangu nibhagulamila kwo bhukondeleywe.
Kulwo kubha bhatana misi jona jona mu myoyo jebhwe, nawe abhegumilisha kwa mwanya mufui. jikabhonekana jinyako no kunyasibwa ungwa bhikaja kulwa insonga yo musango, ao nao nibhekujula.
Na bhandi ni bhalya bhanu bhabhibhilwe mu mawa. abhagungwa omusango,
mbe nawe amaangaiko ge Chalo, no bhujigijigi bhwo ebhinu, bhyo bhunibhi no bhuligisi bhwe misango ejindi, nibhibhengila no kuguiganya omusango, no kusigwa okutwasha amatwasho.
Okumala bhalio bhanu bhabhibhilwe ku mayalu ge kisi. Nibhongwa omusango no kugulamila no kutwasha amatwasho: abhandi makumi gasatu na bhandi makumi mukaga, na bhandi egana limwi”.
Yesu nabhabhwila, “Angu ungwa ukaleta itala munyumba oita emwalo ye chitukulu, amwi mwifufu lwo bhulili? Oileta munju no kuita ingulu ye chigango.
Kwokubha chitalio chona chona chinu chiselekele chinu chitalimenyekana abhwelu.
Akabha alio owa matwi go kungwa, mbe nongwe”.
Nabhabhwila, “Mubhe bhekomelesha mu chinu omungwa, kwo kubha indengo inu omulengelamo niyo one mulilengelwamo, na eyongesibhwa kwimwe.
Ku nsonga ati unu alinacho, kalamila bhyafu, na ulya unu atanacho, ukusoka ku mwene bhiligengwa nolwo bhilya bhinu alinabhyo”.
Mbe naika, “Obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga obhususanyibhwa no munu unu kabhibha jinjuma ku mayalu ge kisi.
Ejile amama mugeta no kwimuka katondo, nasanga jaletele emitenga no kukula, nolwo kutyo atakumenya kutyo jabhonekene.
Echalo echisosha jinjuma echenela; okwamba amabhabhi, okumala echangala, okumala jinjuma jinu jikomee.
Mbe mu mwanya gunu injuma ikaya okumala nusila omwolo, ku nsonga ligesa lyakingile”.
Mbe naika, “chibhususanyishe Obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga na chinu ki, amwi chelesha chijejekanyoki echo kwelesha?
Nilwa injuma ya haradali, yejile yayambwa yaliga noto muno kukila jinjuma jone muchalo.
Nolwo, mu mwanya gwo kuyambwa, eikula nibha Nene kukila emikubhi jona eja mwisambu, na eikola amatabhi manene nolwo jinyonyi ja mulwile ejitula okutamo obhunsuli bhwajo mu mbeo yalyo”.
Mu bhijejekanyo bhyafu abeigisishe omusango, lwa kutyo bhatulaga okumenya,
na ataikaga nabho atali mu bhijejekanyo. Mbe nawe mu mwanya gunu aliga Ali enyele-la, abhelesishe bhuli chinu abheigisibhwa bhae.
Mu lunaku olwo, mu mwanya gwa kegolo gwejile gwakinga, nabhabhwila, “Chigende ku lubhala lwa kabhili”.
kulwejo nibhalisiga liijo, nibhamugega Yesu, mu mwanya ogwo aliga engie mubhwato. Amato agandi galiga amwi nage.
Mbe omuyaga mwafu ogwe chiule na amakonjo galiga nigengisha amaji mu bhwato no bhwato mbubha bhwejue.
Mbe nawe Yesu omwene aliga ali kuseji, amamile ali ku musagulo. Nibhamulafya, nibhaika, “Mwiigisha, awe utakuchikukwa eswe chikafwa?”
Nemuka, nagugonya omuyaga na naibhwila inyanja, “'Cholela, omulembe”. Omuyaga nigutemekela, na nilibha etole enene.
Nabhabhusha ati, kulwaki omubhaya? Angu mutali no kwikilisha kutiki?
Nibhengilwa no bhubha bhwafu mu myoyo jebhwe nibhaikana abhene kwa bhene, unu niga lindi, kunsoga nolwo omuyaga na inyaja ebhimubhaya?”.
Bhejile nibhakinga kwi bhala elindi elya inyanja, mu Chalo cha abhagerasi.
Bhwangu ejile ashoka mu bhwato, omunu wa masabwa majabhi amwijileko nasoka mubhitulo.
Omunu unu agekae mu bhitulo. Atalio unu amuganyishe muno, atalio nolwo kwe bhibhoelo bhye chuma.
Aliga nabhoywa mwanya mwafu kwa masega ne bhibhoyelo bhye chuma. Mbe nawe aliga nagatemya amasega ne bhibhoyelo bhye chuma no kujibhutula-bhutula. Aliga atalio nolwo umwi unu aliga na amanaga go kumuiga.
Mugeta na mu mwisi aliga ali mubhitulo na mumabhanga, aliga nalila no kwitema-omwenela kwa amabhui go bhugi.
Ejile amulola Yesu kulao, namubhilimila no kumwinamusha(okumulamya).
Nalila kwo bhulaka bhwa ingulu, “0wenda nikukoleleki, Yesu, omwana wa Nyamuanga unu ali ingulu muno? Enikulembelesha ku Nyamuanga omwene, wasiga kunyasha.”
Kulwo kubha aliga amubhwiliye ati, “Musokemo omunu unu, awe musambwa mujabhi.”
Mwenene namubhusha, “Lisina lyao nawe-ga?” Namusubhya ati, “Lisina lyani ni Legion, kulwo kubha chili bhafu.”
Namulembelesha lindi na lindi asiga kubhasila anja ye Chalo.
Oli liijo linene lya jingulubhe lyaliga nililebhwa ingulu ye chima,
Nabho nibhamwilembeleja, nibhaika,” Nuchitume ku ngulubhe; chingile munda yebhwe.”
Kwibyo abhekilisisishe mwoyo omujabhi bhabhasokeleko no kwingila munda ya njingulubhe, nabho bhabhilimie ansi yechimali okinga kwigobhelo, na fogelela jingulubhe bhiumbi bhibhili bhatubhie kwigobhwelo.
Na bhalya bhaliga nibhalebha njingulubhe bhabhilimie no kusosha obhubhambasi bhwecho chabhonekene mu musi na mu Chalo. Nio abhanu bhanfu bhemukile okugenda okulola echo chabhonekene.
Nio bhejile ku Yesu ni bhamulola omunu oyo aungilwe ne misabhwa- oyo aligaali na bhalisi- eyanjile ansi, afwae, abhee no bhwege bhwae bhwekisi, nabho bhobhaile.
Bhalya bhaliga bhalolele chinu chabhonekene ku bhanu Oyo aliga aungilwe ne misambwa bhabhabhwilie echo chabhonekene ku mwene na ona kulubhana na jingulubhe.
Nabho bhambile okumlembeleja agende mu Chalo chebhwe.
Ao aliga nibhwengila munda yo bhwato, omunu oyo aliga aungwilwe emisambwa amulembelejishe ati agende amwi nage.
Mbe nawe atamwilebejishe, nawe amubwilie,” Genda ika ewao na ku bhanu bhao na ubhabhwile ejo akukolee Latabhugenyi, lwakutyo akufwilie echigogo.”
Kutyo agendele na ambile okulasha emisago mikulu ejo Yesu akola kumwene mu Dekapoli, na bhuli umwi alugulile.
No mwanya ogwo Yesu ejile ambuka lindi lubhala lundi, munda yo bhwato, liijo enene lwekumanyishe okumusingila, ao aligaali kujejekela yo mwalo.
No umwi wa bhatagasha bhe likofyanyisho, oyo aliga nabhilikilwa Yairo, ejile, na ejile amulola, ague mumagulu gae.
Namulembeleja kafu kafu, omuyalakaji wani omulela ali ayei no kufwa. Enikwilembeleja, uje na uteko amabhoko gao ingulu yae koleleki ati atule okubhona obhuwanga bho kulama.”
Kutyo agendelee amwi nage, na liijo enene lyamulubhile nabho nibhamuiganyaiganya ayei nibhamusingilisha.
Aliga alio omugasi unu amanyiga gae galiga nigamusokamo kwa miyaka ekumi nebhili.
Anyakile kutyo jiile emwalo ya bhafumu bhafu bhanu bhagegele bhuli chinu chinu aliga anacho. Nolwo kutyo atasakiwe chona chona, nawe okumala iyali yae niiyogesha-la okubha mbhibhi.
Nongwa emisango ejo kulubhana na Yesu. Kwibhyo ejile inyuma yae mu mwanya ogwo aliga nalibhata mwiijo, mwenene nachikunyako echifwalo chae.
Kulwo kubha aikile, “Nikabhikunyako-ela ebhifwalo bhyae-la, niniulila.”
Ejile amukunyako-la, okusoka kwa manyiga galya nikutemekela, neyungwa ku mubhili gwae ati eulila okusoka munyako jae.
Ao nao Yesu nemenya omwenela ati amanaga gamusokamo. Nekebhukila enu nenu mwiijo lya abhanu no kubhusha, “Niga unu akunyako echifwalo chàni?”
Abheigisibhwa bhae nibhamubhwila ati, “Oulola liijo linu kutyo likuiganyishe likusingie, mbe awe nuwaika ati, 'Niga unu akunyako?”'
Nawe Yesu namagamaga amulolele unu aliga akoleleelyo.
Omugasi, namenya chinu chabhonekene ku mwene, nobhaya no kuyalala. Ejile nokufukama imbhele yae no kumubhwila echimali chona.
Namubhwila, “muyasha, elikilisha lyao lyakokola kubha muanga. Libhata kwe likilisha na wiulisibhwe okusoka ku bhulwae bhwao”.
Anu aliga naika, abhanu abhandi bhejile okusoka ku mutangasha we likofyanyisho, nibhaika, “Omuyansha wao afue. Kulwaki kugendelela okumunyasha omwiigisha?”
Mbe nawe Yesu ejile ongwa chinu bhaikile, amubhwiliye omutangasha we likofyanyisho, Wasiga kubhaya. Ikilisha-la.”
Atamwikilisishe wona wona okutangashanya nage, atali Petro, Yakobho, na Yohana owabho Yakobho.
Bhejile ika ewo mutangasha we likofyanyisho nawe mwenene one alolele injogele, eyo kulila no kulila jimamu.
Ejile engila muju, nabhabhwila, “kulwaki musulumbae na kulwaki omulila? Omwana achali kufwa nawe amamile-la.”
Nibhamuseka, nawe mwenene, nabhaulusha anja, nabhagega abhebhusi bho mwana oyo na bhalya bhanu bhaliga bhaliga amwi nage, nengila muju munu aliga ali omwana.
Akugegele okubhoko kwo mwana mbe namubhwila, “Talitha koum,” gunu ogwelesha okwaika, Omuyansha mutoto, enikubhwila, nulafye.”
Ao nao omwana ulya nemuka no kulibhata (kulwo kubha aliga ali na miaka ekumi nebhili). Ao nao nibhagatwa ne chitang'ang'alo chinene.
Nabhalagilila kwa managa ati atalio wona wona unu jimwiile okumenya okulubhana na linu. Na nabhabhwila bhamuyane omuyansha ulya ebhilyo.
Nasokao ao no kuja mumusi gwabho, na abheigisibhwa bhwae nibhamulubha.
Isabhatho yejile yakinga, ambhile okwiingisha mu likofyanyisho. Abhanu bhafu nibhamungwa na mbatang'ang'asibhwa. Nibhaika, “Amagabhonaki ameigisho ganu? Ka ni bhwenge ki bhunu ayanilwe?” Angu kakola atiki ebhilugulo bhinu kwa amabhoko gae?”
Angu unu tiwe ulya omubhuya, omwana wa Mariamu no mumula wabho Yakobho, Yose, Yuda na Simoni? Na bhayala bhabho bhatekae anu amwi neswe?” Mbe bhatakondelesibhwe na Yesu.
Yesu nabhabhwila, “Omulagi atakubhulwa chibhalo, atali munsi yabho na muluganda lwabho na munyumba yae.”
Atatulile kukola bhilugulo ao, nawe abhatuliyeko amabhoko abhalwae bhatoto-ela nabheulisha.
Atang'ang'asibhwe muno kunsonga yo kulema okwikilisha kwebhwe. Okumala alibhatie emisi ja kuluguyo neigisha.
Abhabhilikiye abheigisibhwa bhalya ekumi na bhabhili namba okubhatuma bhabhili bhabhili. Abhayanile obhutulo ingulu ye misambwa mijabhi,
no kubhalagilila bhasige okugega chinu chona chona bhakagenda atali isimbo ela. Bhasiga gega omukate, nolwo efwata nolwo jimpilya jo bhwiseleke;
Mbe nawe bhafwale ebhilato, nolwo bhasiga kubha na kanju ebhili.
Na bhabhwila,”Inyumba yona yonà eyo mulengilamo, mwinyanje awo okinga awo mulagendela.
No musi gwona gwona gukalema okubhalamila nolwo okubhategelesha, musokeo kubhene, mukukumule oluteli lwa magulu gemwe, koleleki bhubhe obhubhambasi kubhene.”
Nabho nibhagenda nibhalasha abhanu bhate no kusiga ebhikayo byebhwe.
Bhabhilimishe emisambwa myafu, nabhabhambaga amafuta abhalwàye ni bheulisibhwa.
Omukama Herode ejile ongwa ago, kwo kubha lisina lya Yesu lyaliga lyamenyekene muno. Abhandi bhaikile,”Yohana omubhatija asukile na kusonga eyo, nikwo kutyo amanaga obhuinga obhukola emilimu munda yae.”
Abhandi bhebhwe nibhaika,” unu ni Eliya,” Bhachali ao abhandi ni bhaika,”unu ni mulagi, ati ni umwi wa bhalagi bhalya abhainyuma.”
Mbe nawe Herode ejile ongwa ganu naika,” Yohana, unu natemeleko omutwe asukile.”
Kunsoga Herode omwene amulagilie Yohana agwatwe na mubhoyele mwibhoyelo kusonga ya Herodia (omugasi wa mutabhaniwabho Filipo) Ku songa omwene aliga amutwae.
Kusonga Yohana amubhwiliye Herode,”Itali kisi okumutwala omugasi wa mutabhaniwanyu.”
Mbe nawe ambile okumubhiililwa aliga nenda okumwita, nawe atatulile,
Kusonga Herode amubhaile Yohana; amenyele ati ni mulegelesi munu mwelu, na àmusigile kwo mulembe. Ejile agendelela omutegelesha asulumbae munu, nawe akondelewe okumutegelesa.
Mbe gwejile gwakingila omwanya ogwo gwaliga gwaikilwe nilufogela olunaku lyo kwibhulwa Herode nabhatelao amalya nabhatekela ebhilyo abhakulubhae, na bhàkuru bhe Chalo cha Galilaya.
Nio omuyansha wa Herodia nengila no kubhina imbele yebhwe, namukondelesha Herode na bhagenyi bhanu bhaliga bheyanjile omwanya gwe bhilyo bya kegolo. Nio omukama na mubhwila omuyansha,”niusabhwe chona chona chinu owenda anyone enikuyana.”
Na mulailila no kwaika, chona chona echo ulasabhwa, enikuyana, nolwo libhala elyo bhukama bhwani.”
Nasoka anja namubhusha nyilamwene “Nisabhwe chiya?” Naika, “omutwe gwa Yohana omubhatija.”
Na ao nao negila kumukama namba okwaika,” Enenda unanile Munda ya isaani, omutwe gwa Yohana omubhatijaji.”
Omukama nasulumbala muno, nawe ku songa ye chilailo chae kusonga ya bhagenyi atatulile kumulemelela lisabhwa lyae.
Kwibyo, omukama natuma omusilikale okusoka kubhalisi bhae no kubhalagilila okugenda bhamuletele omutwe gwa Yohana. Omulisi agendele okumubhutula omutwe ali mwibhoyelo.
Naguleta omutwe gwae ku saani no kumuyana omuyansha, no omuyansha namuyana nyilamwene.
Na bhweigisibhwa bhae, bhejile bhogwa ago bhagendele okugega omubhili gwae nibhageda okugusika muchitulo.
Na jitumwa, nijikofyanya amwi imbele ya Yesu, nibhamubhwila gona ago bhakolele nago bheigisishe.
Omwene nabhabhwila ati, “Muje emwe abhene-la mwibhala lyobhwitebhe na chiumule kwo mwanya. “Abhanu bhafu bhaliga nibhaja no kugenda, nolwo bhatabhwene omwanya gwo kulya.
Kutyo nibhalinya obhwato nibhagenda mulubhala lwo bhwitebhe omwene-la.
Mbe nawe bhabhalolele nibhagenda na bhafu bhabhamenyele, kwa amwi bhabhilimile kwa magulu okusoka mu misi jona, nabho nibhakinga nibhabhatanga abhene.
Bhejile bhakinga ku njejekela, abhwene liijo enene na bhafwilwa echigogo, ku songa bhaliga bhali lwà jinyabhalega ejo jitali na mulefi. Nibhamba okubheigisha emisango myafu.
Omwanya gwejile gwageda muno, abheigisibhwa nibhamujako nibhamubhwila,” Anu nilubhala lwo bhwitebhe no mwanya gwa gendelee
Nu bhalage bhagende mumisi Jo luguyo jinu jisijene koleleki bhegulile ebhyokulya.”
Mbe nawe nabhasubya naika, “Mubhayane emwe echokulya. “Nibhamubhwila,” Echitula okugenda no kugula emikate Jo bhugusi bhwa jimpilya magana ghabhili no kubhayana bhalye?”
Nabhabhwila,” Muli ne mikate elinga? Mugende mulole.” Bhejile bhabhona nibhamubhwila,”emikate etanu na jinswi ebhili.”
Nabhalagilila abhanu bheyanje mu mekofyanyisho ingulu ya manyasi mabhisi.
Nabheyanja mu bhise bhya magana na mu ghatanu.
Okumala nagega emikate etanu na jinswi ebhili, na kulola ingulu kulwile, nabhisabhwilwa okumala nabhayana abheigisibhwa bhatule imbele ya liijo. No kumala nagabha jinswi ebhili ku bhanu bhona.
Bhalie bhona nibheguta.
Nibhakumanya ebhibhala bye mikate ebyo byasigae nibhijula bhikapo ekumi na bhibhili, ne bhibhala bya jinswi one.
Na bhaliga bhalume bhiumbi bhitanu abho bhalie emikate.
Ao nao nabhabhwila bhalinye mubhwato bhagende lubhala olundi, okukinga Bethasaida, Omwanya ogwo omwene nabhalaga amekofyanyisho.
Bhejile bhakamala okugenda, nagenda kuchima okusabhwa.
Yejile yakinga kegoro, no bhwato bhwebhwe mu mwanya ogwo bhuli agatigati ya inyanja, omwene aligali enyele kuchalo echumu.
Na abhalolaga nibhanyaka okufuga jingai kusonga yo muyaga gwabhaganyishe. Yejile yalebhelela okukinga katondo nabhalubha, nalibhata ingulu ya manji, na aliga nenda okubhalabhako.
Mbe nawe bhejile bhamulola nalibhata ingulu ya manji nibhabha no bhubha bhaliga nibhetogela ati ni sambhwa nibhamba injongele.”
Ku songa bhejile bhamulolele nibhejusibhwa no bhubha. Ao nao naika nabho nabhabhwila, “Mubhe bhakomee! nanye! Mutabha no bhubha.”
Nengila Munda yo bhwato, no muyanga nigusiga okuyemba, nabho nibhalugula muno.
Kutyo bhaliga bhachali kumenya isonga ye mikate ilya. Kusonga obhwenge bhwebhwe bhwaliga no bhwengeso bhutoto.
Nabho bhejile bhambuka echigobho, nibhakinga kuchalo chumu cha Genesareti obhwato nibhalasa lisikyo.
Bhejile bhauluka anja yo bhwato, ao nao nibhamumenya.
Nibhabhilima okulasha mu chalo chona no kwamba okubhaleta abhalwae ku malili ga abhalwae bhuli eyo bhongwaga ati kaja.
Wona wona ao aliga nengila mu luguyo, amwi mu misi amwi mu chalo, bhabhatee abhalwae mulubhala lwa ligulilo, nibhamwilembeleja abhabhwile bhakunyeko lifwata lye chifalo chae. Na bhona abho bhamukunisheko bhaolele.
Mafarisayo na bhandi abhandiki abho bhaliga bhasokele Yerusalemu nibhekofyanya okumusingila omwene.
Na bhalolele ati abheigisibhwa bhae abhandi bhalie omukate kwa mabhoko majabhi; Ago gatesabhile
(Ku Mafarisayo na Bhayaudi bhona bhatakulya kukinga bhoshe okwamba amabhoko gebhwe kisi; Bhagwatilie echimila cha bhakaluka. Omwanya
Abhafarisayo bhakasubha okusoka kulubhala lwa ligulilo, bhatakulya bhachali kwonga okwamba. Na bhilio ebhilagilo ebhindi ebyo abhalubha chimali, ikabha ni amwi no kwosha ebhikombe, amafulila, ebhinu bhye chuma, nolwo bhitebhe ebyo abheyanjako omwanya gwo kulya.)
Mafarisayo nabhandiki bhamubhusishe Yesu kubhaki abheigisibhwa bhao bhatakwikala okulubhana nechimila cha bhakaluka, kubhaki abhalya omukate bhatesabhile mabhoko?”
Mbe nawe omwene abhabhwiliye ati, “Isaya alangile kisi okulubhana nemwe abho lulimi, andikile, 'Abhanu bhanu abhanana echibhalo kwe mimwa jebhwe, nawe emitima jebhwe jili kula nanye.
Abhakolela lisabhwa elyo litali lyekisi, abheigisha ebhilagilo bya bhana bhanu kutyo bhalamie abhene.'
Mwabhisigile ebhilagilo bha Nyamuanga no kugwatilila kwo bhwangu jimila ja bhana bhanu.”
Na naika kubhene, “Nimuchilema echilagilo cha Nyamuanga kwo bhwangu koleleki ati mubhike jimila jemwe
Kwo kubha Musa aikile ati, “Numwende esomwana wao na nyokomwana wao,' no mwene oyo kaika amabhibhi ingulu ye esemwene wae amwi nyilamwene wae chimali kafwa.'
Mbe nawe omwaika ati, “Alabha omunu akaika kwi semwene wae amwi nyilamwene, “Obhusakisi bhwona bhwona obhwo mwakalamie okusoka kwanye ni chiyanwa cha mwiekalu,”'(Echo ni kwaika ati,'chasosibhwa ku Nyamuanga
Kutyo utakulagilila kukola musango gwona ngwona ingulu ye semwene amwi nyilamwene wae.”
Omubhikola ebhilagilo bya Nyamuanga okubha kutye-la kwo kuleta echimila chemwe. Nemisango myafu jakutyo-ela ejo omukola.”
Alibhilikiye elikofyanyo lindi no kubhabhwila ati, “Munyungwe anye, emwe bhona, no kunsombokelwa.
Chitalio chona chona okusoka anja yo munu chinu echitula okumujabhyasha omunu chinu echimwingila. Nawe ni chilya chinu echimusokamo omunu nicho echimujabhiasha.
(“komelesha: olugobho lunu, “Alabha omunu wona wona ali na matwi go kungwa, nongwe” Lutalimo mu maandiko ga kala).
Yesu ejile alisiga elikofyanyo no kwingila mu nyumba, abheigisibhwa bhwae nibhamubhusha okulubhana ne echijejekanyo echo.
Yesu naika, “Emwe one muchali kwelelwa? Mutakulola ati chona chona chinu echimwingila omunu chitakutula kumujabhiasha,
Kunsonga chitakutula kuja ku mutima gwae, nawe echingila Munda yae okumala nichilabhamo nichija mu choloni “Ku melesho ganu Yesu abhikolele ebhilyo bhyona kubha bhyelu.
Aikile, “Ni chilya chinu echimusokamo omunu nicho echimujabhiasha.
Kulwo kubha echisoka Munda yo munu, anja yo mutima agasokamo ameganilisho mabhibhi, obhusengi, no bhwifi, no bhwiti,
no obhulomesi, inamba mbhibhi, no bhubhibhi, no bhujigijigi, no bhulangilangi, na lifuwa, no kufuma, ne chigundu, no bhumumu.
Ebhibhibhi bhinu bhyona ebhisoka Munda, nibhyo ebhimujabhiasha omunu.”
Emukile okusoka alya no kwimuka okugenda mu muluguyo lwa Tiro na sidoni. Engie Munda na atendele munu wona wona amenye ati aliga aliao, nawe itatulikene okumuseleka.
Mbe nawe ao nao omugasi, Oyo omwana wae aliga no mwoyo mujabhi, onguwe emisango jaye, naja nagwa mumagulu gae.
Omugasi Oyo aliga Muyunani, wo luganda lwe kifoeniki. Amwilembejishe omwene abhilimye lisambwa okusoka mu muyansha wae.
Yesu namubhwila omugasi, “bhasige abhana bhalisibhwe okwamba, kwo kubha jitali ja kisi okugugega omukate gwa bhana no kujilasila jimbwa.”
Mbe nawe omugasi namusubhya no kwaika, “Nikwo kutyo Latabungenyi, nolwo jimbwa ejilya ebhilyo bhinu ebhisigala ebhya abhana emwalo ya lmeja.
Namubhwila, “Kwokubha waika kutya, owikilisibhwa okugenda. Lisambwa lyamusokeleko omuyansha wao.”
Omugasi nasubha ika ewae no kumusanga omuyansha wae amamile kubhulili, na lisambwa nasanga lyamusokeleko.
Yesu nasoka lindi anja ye chalo cha Tilo no kulabha Sidoni nalebhelela ku nyanja ya Galilaya kukinga mu Chalo cha Dikapolisi.
Nibhamuletela omusibhi wa amatwi na aga atakutula okwaika kisi, nibhamulembeleja Yesu amuteleko amabhoko ingulu yae.
Amusosishe anja ye likofyanyisho kwo bhwitebhe natula ebhyala bhyae mu matwi gae, na ejile afubhula amachwanta, namukuniako ku lulimi lwae.
Nalola ingulu mu lwile, nasabhwa naika no kumubhwila ati, “Efata,” ejo ni kwaika ati “Iguka!”
No mwanya gulya gulya amatwi nigeguka, necho chaliga chiganyishe olulimi chanyamuywe natula okwaika kisi.
Nabhakomelesha bhasiga kumubhwila munu wona wona. Nawe lwa kutyo abhakomelesishe, Nikwo kutyo bhalasishe emisango ejo kwo bhwafu.
Ni chimali nibhatang'ang'asibhwa, (nibhalugusibhwa) no kwaika, “Akola bhyona kisi kegula abhegale bha amatwi na abhatita okwaika.”
Mu naku ejo, lyaliga lilio liijo elindi enene, na bhaliga bhatali na bhilyo. Yesu nabhabhilikila abheigisibhwa bhae nabhabhwila,
“Enilisasila liijo linu, abhagendelela okubha nanye kwa naku esatu na bhatali na bhilyo.
Nikabhanyalaganya bhasubhe mumisi jebhwe bhachali kulya abhatula okukabha munjila ku songa ya injala. Na bhandi bhebhwe bhasokele kula muno.”
Abheigisibhwa bhae nibhamusubhya, “Echibhona aki emikate ejokwiya okulisha abhanu bhanu mwibhala linu lisigilwe?”
Nabhabhusha, mulina bhibhala bhilinga ebhye mikate?” Nibhaika, “Musanju”.
Nalilagilila liijo bhenyanje ansi. Nagega mikate musanju, namusima Nyamuanga, no kujibhutula. Nabhayana abheigisibhwa bhae bhajite imbele yebhwe, na bhene nibhajita imbele ya liijo.
One bhaliga bhali na jinswi notwela jitali nyafu, bhejile bhamala okusima, nabhalagilila abheigisibhwa bhae bhabhagabhile bhinu one.
Bhalie nibheguta. Nibhakofya ebhibhala bhinu bhyasagile, ebhikapo bhinene musanju.
Bhaliga nibhalebhelela bhanu bhiumbi bhina. Mbe nabhasiga bhagende.
Okwiya nashabhala mubhwato na abheigisibhwa bhae, mbe nibhagenda mu mabhala ga Dalmanuta.
Okumala Abhafarisayo nibhauluka anja na nibhamba okubhambashanya nage. Bhaliga nibhenda abhayane echibhalikisho okusoka mu lwile, kwo kumulegeja.
Neganilisha muno mu mwoyo gwae naika, “Kulwaki olwibhulo lunu oluyenja echibhalikisho? Enibhabhwila emwe chimali chitalio chibhalikisho chinu echisosibhwa ku lwibhulo lunu.”
Okumala nabhasiga, nashabhala lindi mubhwato, nasokao naja ebhala lindi.
Mu mwanya ogwo abheisibhwa bhalabhiywe okugega emikate. Bhaliga bhatana mikate nolwo kabhala na kamwi kukila kanu kaliga mubhwato.
Nabhakomelesha no kwaika ati, “Mukabhuke na mwikenge ingulu ye chifwimbya cha bhafarisayo ne chifwimbya cha Herode.
Abheigisibhwa nibhaika abhene kwa bhene, “Kusonga chitana mikate.”
Yesu alimenyele linu, nabhabhwila, “Kulwaki omwaikana okulubhana no okulema okubha ne mikate? Muchali kumenya? Muchali kusombokelwa? Emitima jemwe jabhee miyangu? (mikomee)?
Muli na meso, mutakulola? Muna amatwi, mutakungwa? Mutakwichuka?
Anu najigabhanyishe emikate ku bhanu bhiumbi bhitanu, mwagegele bhikapo bhiliga bhinu bhyaliga bhijue bhibhala bhye mikate?” Nibhamusubhya ati, “Ekumi na bhibhili.”
Na nejile najigabhanyishe mikate musanju ku bhanu bhiumbi bhina, mwagegele bhikapo bhilinga?”
Nibhaika ati, “Musanju.” Muchali kusombokelwa?”
Nibhaja Bethsaida. Abhanu abho nibhamuleta ku Yesu omunu muofu na nibhamulembelesha Yesu amukunieko.
Yesu namugwata no kubhoko omuofu ulya, no kumutangasha anja yo musi. Namufubhulila amachwanta ku meso gae nokugolola amabhoko gae ingulu ya meso gae, namubhusha ati, “Oulola chona chona?”
Alalamie ingulu no kwaika, “Enilola abhanu na bhene abhabhonekana uti mati agalibhata.”
Nio nagolola lindi amabhoko gae ingulu ya meso gae, omunu ulya neguka ameso gae, nalola lindi, mbe nalola bhuli chinu kisi.
Yesu namusiga agende ika na namubhwila, “Wasiga kwingila mu musi.”
Yesu nagenda na bheigisibhwa bhae naja mu misi eja Kaiseria ya Filipi. Anu bhaliga bhali munjila nabhabhusha abheigisibhwa, Abhanu abhanyaika ati anye nanyega?”
Nibhamusubhya nibhaika ati, Yohana omubhatijaji. Abhandi abhaika ati, 'Eliya' na abhandi, ni umwi wa Abhalagi.”
Nabhabhusha, “Nawe emwe omwaika ati anye nanyega? “Petro namubhwila, “Awe uli Kristo.” (Masihi).”
Yesu nabhakomelesha bhasiga kubhwila munu wona wona ejo kulubhana no mwene.
Namba okubheigisha ati Omwana wo munu kumwiile anyake kwe misango miyafu, na kajo okulemwa na bhatangasha na abhagabhisi abhakulu, na abhandiki, na kajo kwitwa, na kulunaku lwa kasatu kasuluka.
Aikile ganu abhwelu. Niwo Petro namugega namusubhya kumbali namba okumugonya.
Mbe nawe Yesu ekebhukie no kubhalola abheigisibhwa bhae no okumugonya Petro no kwaika, “Subha inyuma yani Shetani! Utakukukwa emisango ja Nyamuanga, atali emisango eja abhanu.”
Okumala nabhilikila liijo amwi na abheigisibhwa bhae, no kubhabhwila, “Alabha alio omunu unu Kenda okundubha eganye omwene-la, agege omusalabha gwae, na andubhe.
Kulwo kubha wona wona unu Kenda okukisha obhulame bhae, kabhubhusha, na wona wona unu kenda okubhusha ubhulame ingulu yani na ingulu yo omusango gwo bhwana, kabhukisha.
Omunu ejimusakila-ki, akabhona Echalo chona, no kumala nafwilwamo obhulame bhwae?
Omunu katula okusosha-ki chinu chitambene no bhulame bhwae?
Wona wona unu kandolela jinswalo ne misango Jani mu lwibhulo lunu olwo bhulomesi no lwibhulo lwa abhebhibhi, Omwana wo munu one alimulolela nswalo alibha aja mu bhukama obhwa esemwene amwi na Bhamalaika abhelu.
Nabhabwila, “Echimali enibhabhwila emwe, bhaliwo abhanu abhobhemeleguyu anu, bhatakuloja olufu bhachali okubhulola obhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga nibhuja kwa managa.
Baada yansiku mukaga yesu abhagegele Petero, Yakobo, na Yohana nibhaja mwibhanga bhenyele. Niwo ambile oyinduka imbele yebhwe.
Jingubho jaye nijamba okwengelela muno, nijibha jimwela muno kukila bhinu bhyone muchalo.
Niwo Elya bhali na Musa nibhabhonekana imbele yebhwe, bhaliga nibhaloma na Yesu.
Petro namubhwila yesu “Mwiigisha nibhwakisi eswe okubha anu, Chumbake bhiyumba bhisatu, echimwi chilichao, echimwi chilicha Musa nechindi chilicha Eliya.”
Atalomele lyone lyone, nibhobhaya bhone.
Elile lyejile nilibhaswikila. Niwo lilaka nilisokelela mumele nilyaika, “Unu niwomwana wani mwendwa. mumutegeleshe omwene.”
Niwo bhaliga wachelolela, bhatamulolele wona wona oundi tali Yesu.
Bhaliga nibhasubha okusoka mwibhanga, abhabhwiliye mutaja kubhwila munu wonewone ago goone mwagalola, mpaka Omwana womunu akasuluka okusoka mukabhuli.
Niwo bhagabhikile amagambo ago bhenekili. Tali bhebhusishe bhenekili insonga “yokusuluka mukabhuli”
Nibhamubhusha Yesu, “Kubhaki abhandiki abhaika Eliya niwo alija okwamba?” Nabhabhwila “Chimali Eliya alija okwamba okusakila ebhinu bhyone.
Kubhaki yandikilwe Omwana womunu kabhona inyanko nyanfu nabhamubhiililwa?
Tali enibhabhwila Eliya alejile, bhamukolelo kutyo bhendele, lwakutyo ligambo elyaika kumwene.
Bhejile bhakasubha kubhanafunzi, bhalolele likumo lyabhanu libhasingiliye Amasadukayo bhaliga nibhabhambashanya nabho.
Bhejile bhakamulola likumo lyone nililugula nilimulubha okumukesha.
Nabhabhusha abhanafunzi bhaye, “Omubhambashana nabho chinuki?”
Umwi webhwe naika, “Mwiigisha, Namuleta Omwana wani kwawe; anemisambwa ajimukola atakuloma,
ejimukola okuyalala nomugwisha ansi, nokusosha amafilo mukanwa kanyaka muno. Nabhasabhwa abhanafunzi bhao okumusosha amasambwa tali bhasingwa.
Nabhabhwila olwibhulo olwo lutakwikilisha, enibhanemwe katunguki? enibhanemwe katungukii? Mulete kwani.”
Wamuletele Omwana waye. Emisambwa jejile jikamulola Yesu, nijimukola nayalala.
Omusigaji aguye ansi nasosha lifilo mukanwa. Yesu namubhusha esemwene omwana, “alwaye kutya alinakatunguki?” achali mulela
Lugendo kagwa mumulilo namumanja, nigendo omwita. labha utula okukola chona chona chisaslile uchikolele.
Yesu namubhwila, labha wendele? bhulichinu echikolekana kuwonawona oya kekilisha.
Niwo esemwene omwana nalilia naika, “Nekilisha! Nsakila okulema okwikilisha kwani.”
Akatungu Yesu ejile akalola likumo lyabhanu nilija kwebhwe, namusabhila emisambwa neulila.
Alilile kwa managa nijimunyansha omwana emisambwa nijisokako. Omwana obhonekene kuti afuye,
niwo bhone nibhaika, “Afuye,” tali Yesu amugwatile namwimusha, omwa nemuka.
Akatungu Yesu nengila munyumba, abhanafunzi bhaye nibhamubhusha, “Kubhaki chasingilwe okumusosha?”
Nabhabhwila, kwokukola kutyo jitakusokako tali kwokusabhwa.
Bhasokele aliya nibhalabha Galilaya. Atendele munu wonawona amenye awo bhali, kulwokubha aliga neigisha abhanafunzi bhaye.
Nabhabhwila omwana wo Munu abhamukingya mumabhoko gabhanu, abhamwita. Akabha afuye, akabha afuye lunaku lwakasatu kasuluka.
Tali bhatamenyele amagambo ago nibhobhaya okumubhusha.
Nibhakinga Karperinaumu. akatungu aliga alimunyumba nabhabhusha, “Mwaliga nimulomaki akatungu chilimunjila?” Nibhajibhila.
kulwokubha bhaliga nibhabhambashanya munjila niga agali mkulu.
Eyanjile ansi amwi nabhanafunzi bhaye, naloma nabho, “Labha wonawona oyokenda okubha wokwamba, kabha womalisha niwe mkosi wabhona.
Amugegele omwana namuta agati yebhwe, amuyekele mumabhoko gaye, naika,
Wonawona oyo kamulamila omwana lwaunu mwisina lyani lwaunu, kandamila anye, omunu akangamila anye, atakundamila anyela, noyo antumile.
Yohana namubhwila, “Mwiigisha chamulolele omunu nasosha emisambwa kwalisina lyao nichimuganya, kulwokubha atakuchilubha.”
Nawe Yesu naika, “Mutaja omuganya, kulwokubha ataliwo oyo alikola emilimu misito mwisina lyani naika misango mibhibhi mwisina lyani.
Wonawona oyo ataliinyuma neswe, alikulubhala lweswe.
Wonawona oyo kakuyana echikompe chamanji gokunywa kulwokubha ulina Kristo, Chimali enibhabhwila atakubhusha echibhalo chaye.
Wonawona oyo kabhayabhisha abhatilu bhatu abhanyikilisha anye, yakabheye bhwakisi okubhoywa libhii lyoshela mubhicha nolagashwa munyanja.
Labha okubhoko kwao kukakuyabhisha kuteme. Nibhwakisi okwingila mubhuwanga utali nokubhoko nokwingila mumulilo ulina mabhoko gone. mumulilo “Gunyantasima”.
Awo amafunyo gatakufwa nomulilo gutakusima.
Labha okugulu kwao kukakuyabhisha, kuteme. Nibhwakisi okwingila mubhuwanga uli mulema, nokwingila mumulilo ulina magulu gone.
Awo amafunyo gatakufwa nomulilo gutakusima.
Labha eliso lyao likakuyabhya lishoshemo. Nibhwakisi okwingila mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga ulina liso limwi, nokwingila nameso gabhili nuweshwa mumulilo.
Awo gali amafunyo gatakufwa nomulilo gutakusima.
Kulwokubha bhuli umwi alikolela nomulilo.
Omunyu nigwakisi, labha omunyu gukalema onula oukola kutiki gunulile? mulabha nomunyu mumwyoyo jemwe bhenekili, nokubha nomulembe bhuli umwi.”
Yesu asokelao nagenda mumukoa gwobhuyaudi imbele yomugela gwayorodani, nalikumo lyabhanu nilimulubha bhuyaya. Nabheigisha bhuyaya, lwakutyo akolaga.
Amafarisayo bhejile okumusaka nibhamubhusha, “Nibhwakisi omulume okumusiga omugasi waye?”
Yesu nabhabhwila, “Musa abhalagiliyeki?”
Nibhaika, “Musa achibhwiliye okumwandikila echeti nomubhilimya.”
Kulwokubha emyoyo jemwe jikomee nicho ambhandikiye ichilagilo, Yesu nabhabhwila.
Kubhwambilo bhwomogwa insi, 'Nyamuwanga amogele omulume no mugasi.'
Kulwokubha Omulume kamusiga esemwene na nyilamwene nabha nomugasi waye,
kubhone bhabhili abhabha chinu chimwi; kulwokubha bhatali bhabhili nawe mubhili gumwi.
Echo agwatenye Nyamuwanga, Omunu ataja ochitaganya.”
Bhaliga bhali munyanja, abhanafunzi bhaye nibhamubhusha bhuyaya ligambo elyo.
Nabhabhwila”Wonawona oyokamusiga amugasi waye natwala omugasi owundi, kakola echibhibhi kumwene.
Omugasi akamusiga omulume natwalwa nomulume owundi, kakola echibhibhi.”
Nibhamuletela abhana bhebhwe abhalela abhayane amabhando, tali abhanafunzi nibhabhaganya.
Nawe Yesu ejile akamenya, atakondelesishwe nabhabhwila “Mubhasige abhana abhalela bhaje kwanye, kulwokubha abhanu lwabhanu obhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga nibhwebhwe.
Chimali enibhabhwila, Wonawona oyoatakulamila obhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga lwomwana omulela Chimali atakutula okwingila mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga.
Niwo nabhayeka abhana mumabhoko gaye nabhayana amabhando nabhatelako amabhoko gaye ingulu yebhwe.
Ejile akamba olugendo lwaye munu umwi abhilimile nateja ebhijwi imbele yaye, namubhusha, “Mwiigisha wakisi, Nikole kutiki nibhulole obhukama bhwa kajanende?”
Yesu naika, “Kubhaki oumbilikila wakisi? Ataliwo oyo aliwakisi, Niwe Nyamuwanga wenyele.
Oumenya echilagilo: Utajakwita, utaja kusihana, utaja kwibha, utaika lulimi, utaja kujiga, bhayane echibhalo esomwana na nyokomwana.
Omunu uliya naika, “Mwiigisha, ganu gone nagamenyele nichali mulela.”
Yesu amuloleleye namwenda. Namubhwila “Oulebhya chinu chimwi. Owendibhwa okugusha bhinu bhyone ebhyo ulinabhyo nakubhayana abhataka, oubhona libhando mulwile. Niwouje undubhe.
Nafwa omutima okubhwilwa amagambo ago, nagenda asulumbaye, kulwokubha aliga alimunibhi.
Yesu nalola wone nabhabhwila abhanafunzi bhaye, “Kukomee kumunibhi okwingila mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga!
Abhanafunzi nibhalugushwa namagambo ago. Nawe Yesu nabhabhwila bhuyaya, “Abhana, nikukomee okwingila mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga!
Kwolobhele ingamiya okulabha mwiundu lya insiga, tali omunibhi okwingila mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga.”
Bhalugulime muno nibhaikana, “Niga kakila”
Yesu nabhalola naika, “Kumunu Kukomee, tali kunyamuwanga. kulwokubha Kunyamuwanga gone agatulikana.
Petro nambaokuloma nage, “Lola chasiga bhyone chakulubha.”
Yesu naika, “Chimali enibhabhwila emwe, ataliwo oyo asiga inyumba, nolo muyalawabho, nolo mutabhani wabho, nolo nyilamwene, nolo mwana, nolo esemwene, nolo insambu, nalubha anye naligambo lyani,
Oyo alalema olamya egana muno kwaoli anu kuchalo: inyumba, mulawabho, muyalawabho, nyilamwene, abhana, isambu, kwonyaka, nainsi eyo eija nobhuwanga bhwa kajanende.
Tali abhanfu abhakubhwambilo bhalibha bhomalisha nabho bhalibha bhomalisha bhalibha bhokubhwambilo.
Akatungu bhalimunjila, okuja Yerusalemu, Yesu aliga atangatileyo. Abhanafunzi nibhalugula, nabho bhaliga nibhabhasoka inyuma nibhobhaya. Niwo Yesu nabhasosha kumbali bhaliya ekumi nabhabhili namba okubhwilwa echochija okumubhona munaku jayeyi:
Lola, echigenda Yerusalemu, omwana womunu kakingibhwa kubhakuhani, abhakulu nabhandiki. abhamulamula afwe nabhalimusosha kubha nyamaanaga.
Bhalimugaya, bhalimufubhulila amachwanta, bhalimubhuma najinsimbo, nabhamwita. Nawe kulunaku lwakasatu kasuluka.
Yakobho naYohana, abhana bha Zebedayo, bhejile kwaye nibhaika, “Mwiigisha, echikusabhwa uchikolele chonachona echochilakusabhwa.”
Nabhabhwila omwenda nibhakoleleki?
Nibhaika chikilisishe chibhe bhone mubhukama bhwao, umwi mukubhoko kwolumosi aundi mukulyo.
Tali Yesu nabhabhwila, “Mutakumenya echo omusabhwa.
nabhabhwila Omutula ochinywela echikompe echo nilachinywela nolo okubha mubhubhatijo obhwo nilabhatijibhwa, omubhutula.
Nawe oyokabha mukubhoko kwani kwokulyo aukwolumosi atalianye wososha, tali nibhaliya abho bhasolelwe.
Abhanafunzi abhandi ekumi bhejile bhakongwa ago, nibhamba okubha bhiililwa Yakobho naYohana.
Yesu nabhabhilikila kwaye naika, “Omumenya kutyo abhatangasha bhabhanu bhabhanyamaanga abhabhatangasha, nabhanu bhebhwe abhamenyekane abhabholesha obhutulo bhwebhwe.”
Nawe kutalikisi okubha kutyo kwemwe.
Wonawona oyo alabha mukulu agati yemwe abhatangashe, Wonawona oyo alibha wokwamba kwemwe kabha mukosi wabhona.
Kulwokubha omwana womunu atejile okukolelwa tali okutangasha, nokusosha isangama yaye kubhona.
Nibhaja Yeriko. Akasoka Yeriko nabhanafunzi bhaye nalikumo lyabhanu, Omwana waTimayo, Batimayo, Omuwofu omusabhilishi, eyanjile mumbali yainjila.
Ejile akongwa ni Yesu Munazareti, ambile okuyogana naika, “Yesu, Omwana wa Daudi, nsasila”
Bhanfu bhamuganyishe omuwofu, nibhamubhwila ajibhile. Nawe alilile elaka enene muno, “Mwana wa Daudi, Nsakila.”
Yesu emeleguyu naika bhamulete. nibhamubhilikila omuofu uliya, nibhaika “Imuka Yesu kakubhilikila.”
Nayesa ingubho ingubho yaye, nabhilima muno, naja kuyesu.
Yesu namubhusha naika, “Owenda nikukoleleki?” Omulume uliya omuofu naika “Mwiigisha, enenda nilole.”
Yesu namubhwila, “Genda iimani yao yakwiulisha.” Awo awo amesoso gaye nigalola, namulubhilisha Yesu kunjila.
Akatungu bhejile bhakaja Yerusalemu, nibhalebhelela Besthfage naBethaniya, kwibhanga lye mizeituni, Yesu nabhalagilila abhanafunzi bhabhili,
nabhabhwila, “Mugende munsi eyo ilyayeyi neswe. mkakinga omwo, omwiisanga insikili eyo ichali kulinywa. muibhoye namwiilete kwanye.
Munu Wonawona akabhabhusha, 'Kubhaki omukola kutyo?' mwaike, Bhwana kayenda labha akamala kaisubhya anu.
Bhagendele nokwiisanga insikili ibhoyelwe mulutanga, nibhaigega.
bhaliga bhaliwo abhanu bhemeleguyu aliya nibhabha bhusha, “Kubhaki omusibhula insikili eyo?
nibhabhabhwila lwakutyo Yesu abhabhwiliye, abhanu nibhabhasiga bhagende.
Bhanafunzi bhabhili bhaioetele insikili ku Yesu nibhanja jingubho jebhwe ingulu Yesu alinyeko.
Bhanu bhanfu nibhanja ningubho jebhwe kunjila, abhandi nibhanja amabhabhi agobhatemele okusoka mumalugu.
Abho aliga alinabho nabho bhamulubhilishaga bhambile oyogana, “Hosana! Anamabhando oyokaja mwisina lya Bhwana.
Bhubhone amabhando obhukama obhwobhuja obhwa lata Daudi! Hosana oyo aliingulu.”
Niwo Yesu nengila Yerusalemu naja mukanisa nalola bhulichinu. Akatungu kaliga kagendele, nagenda Bethania amwinabho ekumi nabhabhili.
Olusiku olwo lwalubhiye, akatungu nibhasubha okusoka Bethania. aliga anainjala.
Nalola amabhabhi galiti lya mutini kula, nagendaolola labha alatula okubhonako chonachona ingulu yalyo. Ejile akkingao, Atabhwene chonachona asangile mabhabhiila, kulwokubha yaligaitali nsiku ya mutini.
“Nalibhwila Ataliwo Wonawona oyo alilya litunda okusoka kwao bhuyaya.” Abhanafunzi bhaye nibhongwa.
Bhejile Yerusalemu, omwene nengila mukanisa namaba okubhasosha anja abhagusha nabhagusi bhebhinu mukanisa. najigwisha jimeja jabho bhaliga nibhaingyanya jiyela nebhitebhe bhyabho bhagushaga jinguti.
Atekilishishe Wonawona okugega chonachona mukanisa kwibhyo bhagushaga.
Abheigishishe naika, “itandikilwe, 'inyumba yani ilibhilikilwa nyumba yosabhilwamo bhanubhona?' Tali mwaikola nyumba yebhi bhibhi.
Abhatangasha abhakulu nabhandiki bhongwaga kutyo alomaga, niwo nibhaiga injila yomwita. Nawe bhamubhaile kulwokubha likumo lyabhanu lyalugulile ameigisha gaye.
Akatungu kakegolo kakingaga, nibhaja mujini.
Bhaliga nibhalibhata katondo, nibhalilola liti lyo mutini lyumile nemisi jalyo.
Petro ejukile naika, “Rabi! Lola, liti lyo mutini elyo wafumilisishe lyoma.
Yesu nabhabhwila,”Mulabha naiiman kunyamuwanga.
Mwikilishe enibhabhwila ati oyo alalibhwila libhanga linu, 'Sinduka wenyele, ujokwilasa munyanja, labha kekilisha mumwoyo gwaye echoaika echibhonekana, nikwokutyo Nyamuwanga alakola.
Kulwokubha enibhabhwila: bhulichinu echomusabhwa nokubhusha kwaye, mwikilishe ati omubhona, ebhibha bhyemwe.
Akatungu mukemelegulu nokusabhwa mubhasasile abho mubhayabhiye, Esomwana oyo ali mulwile abhasasile ebhi bhibhi bhyemwe.
“Nawe mukalema okusasila nolo esomwana oyo alimulwile atakubhasasila ebhi bhibhi bhyemwe”
Bhejile Yerusalemu. Yesu aliganalibhata mukanisa, abhatangasha abhakulu, abhandiki nabhakaluka bhejile kwaye.
Nibhamubhwila “Oukola magambo ganu kwobhutulo ki?” “Niga akuyanile obhutulo bhwokukola amagambo ganu?”
Yesu Nabhabhwila, “Enibhabhusha chinu chimwi. Mumbwile anyona enibhabhwila enikola amagambo ganu kwobhutulo ki.
Obhubhatijo bhwa Yohana bhwasokele Mulwile aukubhanu? mumbwile.”
Nibhelomela bhone nibhaika, “labha chikaika, 'bhwasokele Mulwile', kaika, 'kubhwaki mutamwikilishishe?'
Nawe chikaika, bhwasokele kubhanu, bhobhaile abhanu, kulwokubha bhona bhamenyaga Yohana aliga Mukosi wanyamuwanga.
Niwo Nibhamubhwila nibhaika, “Chitakumenya. Niwo Yesu nabhabhwila, “Anyona nitakubhabhwila enikola amagambo ganu kwabhutulo ki.
Niwo Yesu namba okubheigisha kwemifano. Naika, “Omunu ayambile lishamba lyemizabibu, nalisingilisha olugo, nashamba elyobho elyo konjelamo impaye. Nombaka omunala neya nabhatamo abhalimi mwishamba lyemizabibu. neya nabhanolugendo lwakula.
Akatungu kejile okinga amutumile omukosi waye kubhalimi bhemizabibu okulamila okusoka kwebhwe amatunda gemizabibu.
Tali bhamugwatile, nibhamubhuma, Nibhamubhilimya atalina chonachona.
Namulagilisha kwebhwe omukosi oundi, nibhamuutasha mumutwe nibhamukolela amagambo gajinswalo.
Niwo namulagilisha oundi, oyo umwi nibhamwita. bhabhakoleye abhandi bhanfu amagambo lwago, nibha bhabhuma nabhandi okubheta.
Aliga achali namunu umwi muno wokumutuma, mwana mwendwa. Niwe abheye womalisha oyoatumilwe kwebhwe. Naika “Abhamwikilisha omwanawani”
Tali abhalimi nibhelomela bhene kubhene, Unu niwe kanyachinu. muje, chimwite, lishamba elibha lyeswe.
Bhamwingiliye, nibhamwita nokumwesa anja yalishamba lyemizabibu.
Mbe kakola kutiki owalishamba lye mizabibu? Alija nobhabhilimwa abhalimi bhe mizabibu nokubha yana lishamba lye mizabibu abhanu abhandi.
Muchaliga osoma ligambo linu? “libhwii elyo abhombaki bhalilemele, lyamabha libhwii lya kumbali.
Linu lyasokele kubhwana, nanilyolugusha mumeso geswe.”
Bhaigile okumugwata Yesu, Nawe bhobhaile abhanu, kulwokubha bhamenyele ati amagambo ago kaika kabhaikila abhene. Niwo nibhamusiga nibhaja jebhwe.
Niwo nibhabhatuma abhafarisayo namaherodia kumwene bhamubhushe emisango.
Bhejile bhakakinga, nibhamubhwila, “Mwiigisha echimwenya kutyo outegelesha bhulimunu nautakwelesha obhupendeleo kubhanu. Owiigisha injila ya Nyamuwanga muchimali. Chibhwile Nikwakisi okuliya ikodi muserikali nawe pai? echitula okuliya nawe chisige?
Nawe Yesu aliga amenyele insonga yebhwe nabhabhwila, “Kubhaki omundoja? Munane isilingi niilole.”
Nibhaleta imwi ku Yesu, Nabhabhwila, isilingi inu necho chandikilwe anu nichaga? Nibhaika, “Niyaiserikali.”
Yesu Nabhabhwila, “Muyane iserikali ebhinu bhyaye Na Nyamuwanga ebhinu vya Nyamuwanga. “Nibhamulugula.
Niwo Amasadukayo, nibhaika bhutaliwo bhusuluko, Nibhamulubha. Nibhamubhusha, nibhaika,
Mwiigisha, Musa achandikiye ati 'Omukobhe wao akafwa namusiga omugasi waye bhatebhuye nage, Omunu kamugega omugasi womukobhe wabho, nebhula nage abhana.'
Bhaliga bhaliwo bhakobhe mwenda, owokwamba natwala omugasi neya nafwa, bhatebhuye nage.
Owakabhili namugega omwenona nafwa, atasigile mwana. owakasatu ona kutyo.
Nowamwenda nafwa atasigile mwana. Neya omugasi nafwa.
Akatungu kosuluka, bhakasuluka bhuyaya, Alibha mugasi waga? kulwokubha bhone mwenda bhaliga bhalume bhaye.”
Yesu nabhabhwila, kulwokubha bhabha yabhisishe Mutakumenya ligambo na managa ga Nyamuwanga?”
Akatungu kokusuluka okusoka mukabhuli, bhatalitwala notwalwa bhalibha lwa bha malaika bha Mulwile.
Tali, abhafuye abho abhasululwa, mutasomele okusoka muchitabho cha Musa, mumagambo gali poli, kutwo Nyamuwanga aikile namubhwila, 'Anye ni Nyamuwanga wa Abrahamu, Nyamuwanga wa Isaka, na Nyamuwanga wa yakobho?
Omwene atali Nyamuwanga wabhafuye, Tali abho abhesiya. Nichimali mwamulamila.”
Umwi wabhamdiki ejile nategelesha amagambo ago; Nalola ati Yesu abhabhwiliye kisi. Namubhusha “Nichilago ki echakisi kula bhyone?”
Yesu naika “Eyakisi niinu, “Yungwa, Israeli, Bhwana Nyamuwanga weswe, Bhwana niumwi.
Mwende Bhwana Nyamuwanga wao, kwo mwoyo gwao gwone, nomutima gwao gwone, nobhwenge bhwao bhwone, namanaga gao gone.
Echilago chakabhili nichinu 'Mwende jirani wao lwakutyo owiyenda mwenekili.' Chitaliwo chilago chindi chinene lwachinu.”
Omwandiki naika, 'Nikwakisi Mwiigisha! Waika echimali ati Nyamuwanga niumwi, Nati ataliwo owundi lwo mwene.
Okumwenda omwene kumwoyo gwone, kubhwenge bhwone, na managa gone, nokumwenda jirani wao mwenekili, Nikwakisi muno okukila isadaka ya mukanisa.
Akatungu Yesu ejile akalola asosha magambo gakisi, namubhwila, “Awe utali kula Nobhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga.” ejile akamala ataliwo oyo amubhusishe chinu chonachona.
Yesu naika, akatungu aliga neigisha mukanisa, naika, “abhandiki abhaika Kristo nimwana wa Daudi?
Daudi mumagambo gaye kaika, 'Bhwana naika ku Bhwana wani, iyanja mukubhoko kwani kwobhulyo, nibhakole abhakai bhao okubha ansi yamagulu gao.
Daudi mwenekili kamubhilikila Kristo, 'Bhwana' Mbe nimwana wa Daudi kutiki? likumo lyabhanu lamutegeleshishe likondelewe.
Mumeigisha gaye Yesu aikile, “Mulabha bhengeso na bhandiki, abhoabhenda okulibhata najikanju jindela nbhabha kesha mumagusisho,
Nokwiyanja kubitebhe bhyabhakulu munyumba josabhila namusikukuu awo abheyanja abhakulu.
Abhalya jinyumba jabhafwilwa nokusabhwa jisala ndela abhanu bhabhalole. abhanu bhanu bhalilamila ihukumu eyaingulu.
Niwo Yesu neyanja ansi ayeyi nalisandikwa lya jisadaka munda yalikanisa; nalolaga abhanu abho bhasoshaga jisadaka mwisandikwa. abhanu bhanfu abhanibhi bhasosishe sadaka nyanfu.
Niwo mugasi omutaka omufwilwa ejile nasosha silingi ebhili.
Niwo nabhabhilikila abhanafunzi bhaye nokubhabhwila, “Mwikilishe enibhabhwila, omugasi unu omufwilwa asosha chinu chinene kukila bhone abho bhasosishe mwisandikwa lyajisadaka.
Kulwokubha bhone bhasosha okwingana nobhwanfu bhwajiyela jebhwe. Nawe omufwilwa unu, okwingana nobhutaka bhwaye, asosha yela yona oyokumusakila omwene.
Yesu aliga nalibhata nasoka mkanisa, umwi mubhanafunzi bhaye namubhusha, “Mwiigisha, lola amabhwii ganu agalugusha namayumba!”
Namubhwila, oulala amayumba ganu amanfu? litaliwo nolo libhwii limwi elyo lilasigala ingulu yelyejabho elyo litaligwishwa ansi.”
Niwo aliga eyanjile ingulu yalibhanga lye mizeituni inyuma ya ikanisa, Petro, Yakobho, Yohana na Andrea Nibhamubhusha kwebhiwewe,
“Chibhwile, amagambo ganu agabha lii? Niki echimwenyegesho cha magambo ganu obhonekana?”
Yesu ambile okubhabhwila, “Mulabha bhengeso munu Wonawona ataja okubhayabhya.
Bhanfu bhalija kwalisina lyani nibhaika, 'Anye niwe', nabhabhajiga bhanfu.
Mukongwa obhulemo, mutaja kubhaya; amagambo ganu galibhonekana, Tali obhutelo bhuchali.
Insi ilimelegulu nisijana neyejabho, nobhukama bhulisijana nobhwejabho. galibhayo amasingisha chalo nainjala. bhunu nibhwambilo bhwolufu.
Muwe bhengeso. Abhabhasila kumabhalaja, mulibhumwa munyumba josabhila. abhabhemelegushu, mubhusu bhwa bhatangasha nabhakama kwalisina lyani, kuti bhubhambasi bhwebhwe.
Nawe ligambo chitali likinge munsi jona.
Labha bhakabha gwata nokubhasila, mutajakubhaya echo mulaika. Munda yomwanya ogwo, abhabhayana chiya chokwaika; mutaliloma emwe, tali moyo mwela.
Owabho alimubheelesha owabho nibhamwita. Esemwene nomwana waye. abhana bhalibhendelesha bhesemwene nibhabheta.
Bhali bhabhiililwa nabhuli munu kwalisina lyani. Nawe oyo alekomesha mpakakubhutelo, omunu oyo alikila.
Mukalola libhiililwa lyo bhunyamuke limeleguyu aolitakwendibhwa kubha (oyokasoma namwenye) niwo abho bhalimunda ya Yuda bhabhilimile mumabhanga.
Oyo aliingulu yainyumba atatuka ansi, nolokugega chonachona echochilianja,
Noyo alimwishamba atasubha okugega ingubho yaye.
Nawe lulibhabhona abhagasi abhagasi bhajinda nabhanenya munaku ejo!
Musabhe ati gatabhonekana mukatungu kaimbeo.
kulwokubha ilibhao inyanko nyanfu, eyo ichaliga kubhonekana okusoka Nyamuwanga amogee insi, mpakalelo, italiwo, italibhonekana bhuyaya.
Mpakabhwana apunguje jinsiku, gutaliwo mubhili ogwo gulikila, tali kwabho bhasolelwe, abho alibhasola, alipunguja jinsiku.
Akatungu ako munu Wonawona akabhabhwila, lola Yesu alyanu naliya! mutekilisha.
Kulwokubha abha Kristo nabhalagi bholulimi bhalisosha ebhimenyegesho nebhilugusho, koleleki bhabhajige, nabhaliya abhasolwa.
Mulabha bhengeso! Nabhabhwila ganu gone kachali akatungu.
Tali ikalabhao inyanko yajinsiku ejo, lisubha lilibha mwilima, okwesi kutalyaka,
Jinyota jiligwa okusoka mulwile, namanaga ago galimulwile bhaligongwa.
Niwo bhalimulola omwana womunu naja mumele kwa managa manfu nalikusho.
Niwo alilagilisha bhamalaika bhaye nalibhakumanya abhasolwa bhaye okusoka mumbala jone jechalo, okusoka kubhumalisisho bhwechalo nakubhutelo bhwolwile.
Kwamutini mwiigile. lwakutyo litabhi elitula okulagasha nokutako bhwangu amabhabhi gaye, niwo mulimenya olwanda lulyayeyi.
Nkokutyo jili, Mukalola amagambo ganu nigabhonekana, mumenye ati alyayeyi, nomulyango.
Chimali, enibhabhwila, Olwibhulo lunu lutakulabhao kula amagambo ganu gachali obhonekana.
Olwile nainsi jililabhao, tali ligambo lyani litalilabhao kafwile.
Nawe olusiku olwo nakatungu, ataliwo oyakamenya, nolo bhamalaika bha Mulwile nolo Mwana tali Lata.
Mulabha bhengeso, Lola, kulwokubha mutakumenya nikatunguki agabhonekana. “Mulangalila, mulole namulasabhwa”
Nilwakutyo omunu kaja mulugendo: nasiga inyumba yaye, namutamo omwangalisi waye abhe mutangasha wainyumba, bhuli umwi nomulimu gwaye, nokumubhwila omulindi angalile.
Mbe mulangalila! kulwokubha mutakumenya nilii kanyanyumba kasubha ika, amwi nikegolo, amwi ingeta, amwi mulugulu amwi akatondo.
akaja mwanya gwona gwona, atabhasanga mumamile.
Echo enaika nawe enaika nabhulimunu. Mulasabhwa”!
