Yaliga jalabhileo nsiku ebhili okusoka kulusiku lwaipasaka olwemikate ojo jitakutulwamo chifwimbya. abhatangasha abhakulu na abhandiki bhaliga nibhaiga kutyo bhalamugwa Yesu kwolwango lwomita.
Kulwokubha bhaikile, “Katali katungu kanu kaisikukuu, abhanu bhataje bhakasambagana.
Akatungu Yesu aliga ali Bethania munyumba eya Simoni omugenge, bhaliga bhali kumeja, mugasi umwi ejile kwaye ana inchupa eyamafuta amalange ga nardo gelele gayela nyanfu muno, nafundukula inchupa namwitilila ingulu yomutwe gwaye.
bhaliga bhalio abhanu abhandi bhabhiiliwe. Nibhaikana abhene kwabhene nibhaika, “Kubhaki kabhusha amafuta amalange kutyo?
Amafuta amalange ganu gakagusibhwe kukila dinali magana gasatu, nibhabhayana abhataka.” Niwo nibhamuganya.
Niwo Yesu naika, “Mumusige mwenekili. kubhaki omumunyasha? Akola omusango gwakisi kwanye.
Nsiku jone abhataka munabho, nakatungu konakona mukenda omutula okukola agekisi kwebhwe, Nawe mutakubha nanye katungu kona.
Akola echo katula: agusinga omubhili gwani amafuta nichali okufwa.
Chimali enibhabwila, bhuli chalo awo gulisimulwaga Omusango munsi yone, echo akolele omugasi unu chilyaikwa kwomwijuka.
Niwo Yuda Iskariote, umwi wabhaliya ekumi nabhabhili, agendele kubhatangasha abhakulu koleleki abhakabhiji kwebhwe.
Akatungu abhatangasha abhakulu bhejile bhakongwa kutyo, bhakondelewe nibhalagila okumuyana jiyela. Nambakuiga injila yokumkabhiji kwebhwe.
Kulunaku lwokwamba lwe mikate ejo jitana chifwimbya, akatungu bhejile bhakasoshya inyabhalega yaipasaka, abhanafunzi bhaye bhamubhwiliye, “owenda chigendeaki eyo chilalila ebhilyo bhyaipasaka?
Abhatumile abhanafunzi bhaye bhabhili nabhabhwila, “Mugende mujini, omubhugangana nomulume agegele insua, mumulubhe.
Inyumba eyo alengila, mumulubhe namumubhwile kanyanyumba eyo, “Mwiigisha aika, “Chilyaki echumba chabhagenyi awo nilalila ipasaka nabhanafunzi bhani?”
Kabholesha echumba chaingulu echinene chayela nyanfu. mulachikonja nicheswe.”
Abhanafunzi bhasokeleo nibhagenda mujini; nibhasanga bhulichinu lwakutyo aliga abhabhwiliye, nibhakonja ebhilyo bhyaipasaka.
Yejile ikakinga kegolo, ejile nabhaliya ekumi nabhabhili.
nibheyanja lubhebhe kumeja nibhalya, Yesu naika, “chimali enibhabwila, umwi kwimwe oyokalya amwi nanye alinsoka muchiwi.”
Bhona bhasulumbalile umwi kuundi nibhamubhwila, “Chimali atali anye?”
Yesu aikile nabhabwila naika, “Niumwi muekumi nabhabhili kwimwe, umwi oyo oli kakoja litonge mumbakuli amwinanye.
Kulwokubha Omwana wo munu kagenda lwakutyo ligambo elyaika kumwene. Nawe jilimubhona omunu oyo alimwendelesha Omwana wo Munu. Yakabheye bhwakisi omunu lwoyo atakebhuywe.
Awo bhaliga nibhalya, Yesu agegele omukate, nagubhaliki, agubhutula. Nabhayana naika “Mugege. Gunu nimubhili gwani.”
Agegele echikompe, nasima, nabhayana, bhone nibhachinywela.
Abhabhwiliye “Inu ninsagama yani eyechilagano, insagama eyo eitika kubhanfu.
Chimali enibhabhwila, nitalisubhila okuywa litwasho lyo muzabibu mpaka olusiku luliya olwoniliywa bhuyaya mubhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga.”
Bhejile bhakama okwimba amembo, bhagendele anja mumabhanga gemizeituni.
Yesu nabhabhwila, “Emwe bhona mulibha kumbali kwalisina lyani, kulwokubha yandikilwe, Nilimubhuma Omulefi najinyabhalega nijisalambana.
Nawe nikamala okusuluka, omusanga imbele yemwe Galilaya.
Petro namubhwila “Nolo bhona bhakakusiga, anye nitakukusiga.”
Yesu nabhabwila, echimali enikubhwila, ingeta inu, ing'okolomi ichali okokolima kabhili, ousanga wandemele kasatu.”
Nawe petro naika, “Nilifwa nawe, nitakukusiga.” Wona bhasoshisye echilagano chilya chilya.
Bhejile awo patogagwa Gethsemane, niwo Yesu nabhabwila abhanafunzi bhaye, “Mwiyanje anu akatungu nisabhwa.”
Abhagegele Petro, Yakobo, na Yohana nomwene, namba okusulumbala nonyaka muno.
Nabhabwila, “Omutima gwani gusulumbaye muno nolufu. Musigale anu musabhwe.”
Yesu agendele imbele katilu, nateja ebhijwi, nasabhwa, yakabheye bhwakisi omwanya gunu gwakansokeleko.
Aikile,”Aba, Lata, Amagambo gone kwawe agatulikana. Nsosishao echikompe chinu. Nawe kutali kwelyenda lyani, tali kulyenda lyao.”
Asubhile nabhasanga bhamamile, namubhwila Petro, “Simon, mumamile? mutatulile okusabhwa nolo esaa limwi?
mulasabhwa koleleki mutaja mukengila mubhi bhibhi. Chimali omwoyo nibhando, nawe omubhili nimufuye.”
Agengele okusabhwatena, naika amagambo galya galya.
Ejiletena nabhasanga bhamamile, kulwokubwa ameso gebhwe galiga galimasito bhatamenyele haike chiya.
Ejile kulwakasatu nabhabhwila, “Muchali mumamile no woya? Yeya! Akatungu kakinga. Lola! Omwana wo munu abhamusila mumabhoko gabhanu bhebhi bhibhi.
Mwimuke, chigende. Lola, oyo kangusha alyayeyi.”
Omwanya ogwo aliga achaloma, Yuda, umwi wabhaliya ekumi nabhabhili, nakinga, nalikumo lyanfu lya bhatangasha abhakulu, abhandiki nabhakaluka bhe bhitemelo nama bhumilo.
akatungu ako oyoaliga abhasokele muchiwi abhayanile echimenyegesho, naika, oyonilamubusu niwe omwene. Mumu gwate namumusile ansi yobhwangalisi.
Akatungu Yuda ejile akakinga, agendende chimwi mpaka ku Yesu naika, “Mwiigisha!” namubusu.
Niwo nibhamuta ansi yobhwangalisi nibhamugwata.
Nawe umwi kwebhwe oyoaliga emeleguyu nage asolotoye echitemelo chaye namubhuma omukosi wa kuhani omukulu namutema okutwi.
Yesu nabhabhwila, “Mwaja okungwata nebhilwanilo kuti nilimwifi?
Kenu bhulisiku naliga nilinemwe nibheigisha mukanisa, mutangwatile. Nawe linu lyakolekana ligambo likinge kubhutelo.
Nabhaliya bhona abhobhaliga bhalina Yesu bhamusigile nibhabhilima.
Musigaji umwi amulubhile, oyoaliga afwaye isukala eyoaliga eswikiye imusingilisishe; nawe bhamugwatile
Abhatesukile naisiga isuka aliya nabhilima tuyu.
Bhamulibhasishe Yesu okuja ku kuhani omukulu. niwo bheyanjile nage amwi nabha kuhani abhakulu bhone, abhakaluka, nabhandiki.
Petro ona amulubhilishaga Yesu alikula, naja kwiuwa ewa kuhani omukulu. Neyanja amwi nabhalindi, abhobhaliga bhalyayeyi nomulilo nibhabhila bhabhote imbita.
Omwanya ogwo bhakuhani abhakulu bhone nalibhalaja lyone bhaliga nibhaiga obhubhambasi ku Yesu bhamwite. Nawe bhatabhubhwene.
Kulwokubha bhanu bhanfu bhaletele obhubhambasi bhwolulimi ku mwene, tali obhubhambasi bhwebhwe bhutasusene.
Abhandi bhemelegeyu nibhaleta obhumbambasi bhwolulimi ku mwene; nibhaika,
“Chamunguye naika, Enilinyamula likanisa linu elyo lyakonjelwe namabhoko, na mumwanya gwansiku esatu enumbaka elindi elyo litakumbakwa namabhoko.”
Nawe nolo obhubhambasi bhwebhwe bhutasusene.
Kuhani omukulu emeleguyu agati yebhwe namubhusha Yesu, “utakusubhya chonachona?” Abhanu bhanu abhakubhambalila chinuki kwawe?”
Nawe ajibhiye ataikile chonachona. Niwo kuhani omukulu namubhusha, “Nawe kristo, omwana wo mubhalikwa?
Yesu naika, “Nanye omwene. Ulimulola omwana wo munu eyanjile mukubhoko kwobhulyo kwamanaga naja namele gamulwile.”
Kuhani omukulu nabhiililwa nesa ingubho yaye naika, “chichali chichenda abhabhambasi?”
Mwongwa ikufulu. Obhulamusi bhwemwe nibhuya?” bhone bhamulamuye lwomunuyo endwaga afwe.
Abhandi bhambile akumufubhulila amachwanta nibhamuswikila obhusu nibhamubhuma nibhamubhwila, “bhalikisha!” Bhaafisa bhamugegele nibhamubhuma.
Akatungu Petro aliga achali ansi yaliuwa, mukosi umwi omugasi wa kuhani omukulu ejile kwaye.
Amulolele petro awoaliga emeleguyu nabhila omulilo, namulola namwililako. niwo naika, “Aweona waliga ulina Omunazaleti, Yesu”.
Nawe alemele naika, “Nitakumenya chonachona echo owaika!” Niwo nasokawo nagenda anja. Naing'oko nikokolima.
Nawe omukosi wechigasi uliya, amulolele namba okubha bhwilwa bhuyaya bhaliya abhobhaliga bhemeleguyu aliya, “Omunu unu niumwi nabhaliya!”
Nawe alemele bhusibhusi. mwanya mutilu abho bhaliga bhemeleguyu aliya bhaliga nibhamubhwila Petro, “Nawe awe uliumwi webhwe, kulwokubha aweona uli Mugalilaya.”
Nawe ambile okwitula mwenekili ansi yalifumilisho nolema, “Nitakumumenya omunu unu oyomwaika.”
Niwo ing'okolomi nikokolima lwakabhili. Niwo Petro nechuka emisango ejo Yesu aliga amubhwiliye: “ing'oko ichali kukokolima lwakabhili, oundema kasatu.” Niwo nagwa ansi nalila.
Mulugulu katondo abhakulu bhamakuhani bhabhonene amwi nabhakaluka nabhandiki nalibhalaja lyone lya bhakaluka. Niwo nibhamubhoya Yesu nibhamusila ewa Pilato. Pilato namubhusha, “awe ulimkama wabhayahudi?”
“Naika, “Awe waika kutyo.”
Abhakulu bha makuhani nibhelesha obhubhambasi bhwanfu ku Yesu.
Pilato namubhusha bhuyaya, “Utakwaika chonachona? Utakulola kutyo abhakubhambalila ku misango myanfu?
Nawe Yesu atamusubhishe Pilato, nalugula muno.
Kulwakutyo mu mwanya gwaisikukuu abhegulilaga omubhoywa umwi, bhasabhile omubhoywa umwi.
Bhaliga bhaliwo abhakai mwigeleza, abho bhaliga bhabhoyelwe kwebhikayo bhyokwita. Aliga aliwo munu umwi nabhilikilwa Baraba.
Likumo lyabhanu lyejile ku Pilato, nibhamusabhwa akole lwakutyo akolele inyuma eyo.
Pilato nabhabhwila naika, “Omwenda nibhegulile Omukama wabhayaudi?”
Kulwokubha amenyele bhalina olwiso abhakulu bhamakuhani bhamugwatile Yesu nibhamuleta kwaye.
Nawe abhakulu bha makuhani bhabhwiliye abhanu bhayogane kwo bhulaka ati bhamwigulile Baraba nawe omwene uli.
Pilato nabhabhwila bhuyaya naika, “Nikolechiya Mkama wa Bhayahudi?
Nibhayogana bhuyaya, “Mumubhambe”
Pilato naika, “Akola musangoki mubhibhi? Niwo bhagendeleye okuyogana muno “Mumubhambe.”
Pilato endele okubhakondelesha abhanu, namwigulila Baraba. Namubhuma Yesu emijeledi niwo nibhamusosha ajobhambwa.
Abhalwani nibhamusila munkambi bhekumanyishe amwi abhalwani.
Nibhamuswikila Yesu ikanju yaizambalawe, nibhakonja ingofila ya mawa nibhamufwafya.
Nibhamba okumugaya nibhaika, Omukama wa Bhayahudi!”
Nibhamubhuma mumutwe nomuanzi nibhamufubhulila amachwanta. Nibhateja ebhijwi imbele yaye kwalisima.
Bhejile bhakamala okumugaya, nibhamufula ikanju iliya yaizambalawe nibhamufwafya jingubho jaye, nibhamusosha anja okuja okumubhamba.
Nibhamusinyilisha omunu okumusakila, oyo engilaga mujini nasoka mumashamba. Abhilikilwaga Simoni Mkirene (esemwene Isikanda na Rufo); nibhamusinyilisha okuyeka omusalabha gwa Yesu.
Abhalwani nibhamusila Yesu awo kabhilikilwa Goligota (isonga yendeo ni, kulwotosi lwo mutwe).
Nibhamuyana impaye eyo itobhelemo na imanemane, tali atainyweye.
Nibhamubhamba nibhagabhana jingubho jaye, nibhajibhumila jikula okulamula echipande echoalagega bhuli mulwani.
Mumwanya gwa saa esatu katondo awo bhamubhambile.
Nibhatula ingulu yaye olubau olwo lwandikilwe “Omukama wa Bhayahudi.”
Bhamubhambile amwi nabhakai bhabhili, umwi mulubhala lwaye lwokulyo oundi mukumosi kwaye.
“Naligambo nilikingila elyo lyaikilwe”
Abho bhalabhaoga bhamufumaga, nibhasingisha emitwe jebhwe nibhaika, “Aah! nawe owokulifumya likanisa nokulyumbaka nsiku esatu,
Isakila mwenekili utuke ansi usoke kumusalabha!”
Musonga iliya iliya abhakulu wa makuhani bhamugaile nibhaikaga, amwi nabhandiki nibhaika, “Abhasakiye abhandi, nawe atakutula okwisakila mwenekili.
Kristo Omukama wa Israel, tuka ansi oli usoke kumusalabha, niwo chilole nokwikilisha. Nabho bhabhambilwe amwinage bhamugaile.
Yejile ikakinga saa sita, omwilima niguja ingulu yainsi yona adi saa tisa.
Mumwanya gwa saa tisa, Yesu alilile kwalilaka enene, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” ilinaisonga “Nyamuwanga wani, Nyamuwanga wani, kubhaki wansiga?”
Abho bhaliga bhemeleguyu bhejile bhakongwa nibhaika, “Lola, kamubhilikila Eliya.”
Munu umwi nabhilima, nenika isiponji musiki naitunga kwiti lyo muanzi, namuyana anywe. Munu umwi naika, “Siga chilole labha Eliya alaja okumutusha ansi.”
Niwo Yesu nalila kwalilaka muno nafwa.
Lipazia lya Ikanisa niligabhanyika kabhili okusoka ingulu okuja emwalo.
Afisa umwi oyoaliga emeleguyu namulolela Yesu, ejile akalola nafwa kutyo, naika, “Chimali omunu unu aliga alimwana wa Nyamuwanga.”
Bhaliga bhaliwo abhagasi nibhalola bhalikula. Abhobhaliga bhaliwo ni Mariamu Magdalena, Mariamu (nyilamwene Yakobo omutoto wa Yose), na Salome.
Akatungu ali Galilaya bhamulubhile nibhamukolela. Nabhagasi abhandi abhanfu bhagendaga nage mpaka Yerusalemu.
Yejile ikabha kegolo, kulwokubha lwaliga lulilusiku lwamaandaliyo, olusiku ichali kwingila isabhao,
Yusufu wa Arimathaya ejile aliya. Aliga alimukosi walibhalaja oyo akusiibhwaga omunu oyoabhwendaga Obhukama bhwa Nyamuwanga. Kwo bhuigi nagenda ewa Pilato, nasabhwa omubhili gwa Yesu.
Pilato nalugushwa ati Yesu afuye; namubhilikila afisa uliya namubhusha labha Yesu afuye.
Ejile akabhanechimali okusoka ku afisa ati afwa, namwikilisisha Yusufu okugugega omubhili.
Yusufu aliga agulile lisanda. Namusosha Yesu okusoka mumusalabha, namusemba nalisanda, namusika mukabhuli eyoyasimbilwe agati yalibhwii. Niwo nailingisha libhwii kumulyango gwaikabhuli.
Mariamu Magdalena na nyilamwene Yose bhalolele awo bhamusikile Yesu.
Akatungu isabhato yejile ikawa, Mariamu Magdalena na Mariamu nyilamwene Yakobo, na Salome, bhagulile amafuta gakisi, bhaje bhagusinge amafuta omubhili gwa Yesu ilibhagusike.
Mulugulu katondo olusiku lwokwamba lwobhwoyo, bhagendele kukabhuli mumwanyogwo lisubha elisokayo.
Nibhalomaga abhene, “Niga alasilingisha libhwii achisakile eswe chingile mukabhuli?”
Mumwanyogwo bhejile bhakalola, bhamulolele alisosisheo libhwii, lyaliga lilinene muno.
Nibhengila mukabhuli nibhamulola omusigaji afwaye ikanju imwela, eyanjile kulubhala lwokulyo, na nibhalugushwa.
Nabhabhwila “Msiogope. Omumuiga Yesu, wa Nazareti, oyo bhamubhambile. Asuluka! Ataliwo anu. Mulole aliya bhaliga bhamumamishe.
Mugende, mujobhabhwila abhanafunzi bhaye na Petro ati omumusanga akingile Galilaya. Eyo mulimulola, lwakutwo aliga abhabhwiliye.”
Nibhagenda nibhabhilima kusoka kukabhuli; bhayalaye nibhalugushwa. Bhataikile chonachona kmutu wonawona kulwokubha bhobhaile bhona.
Mulugulu kulusiku lwokwamba lwobhwoyo, ijile akasuluka, namubhonekanila Mariamu Magdalena, okusoka kumwene amusosisheko misambwa mwenda.
Agendele nokubhabhwila bhaliya abho bhaliga bhaliamwinage, omwanyogwo bhaliga bhasulumbaye nibhalila amasiga.
Bhonguye ati nimuwanga abhonekana, nawe bhatamwikilisishe.
mumwanya mufwii, nabhonekana andi kubhanu abhandi bhabhili, mumwanyogwo bhalibhataga nibhasoka muchalo.
Bhagendele nibhabhwila abhanafunzi abhandi abhobhasigaye. nawe bhatabhe kilisishe.
Yesu mumwanya gundi nabhonekana kubhaliya kuminamoja bhaliga bheyanjile kumeja, nabhakemea okulema okwikilisha kwebhwe nobhukomeye bhwe myoyo, kulwokubha bhatabhekilisishe abho bhamulolele ejile akasuluka okusoka mukabhuli.
Nabhabhwila, “Mugende munsi wone, nokulasha omusango kubhanu bhona.
Wonawona oyoalekilisha nobhatijibhwa kachunguka muntambala, oyo atakwikilisha alibha muntambala.
Ebhimenyegesho bhinu bhililubhana nabhona abhekilisha. Kwisina lyani bhalisosha emisambwa. bhalyaika mukabhila inyaya.
Bhaligwata injoka mumabhoko gebhwe, nolo bhakanywa chinu chonachona chokwita chitalibheta. Bhalita amabhoko kubhalwaye, bhaliulila.
Ejile Bwana akamala okuloma nabho, nagegibhwa ingulu mulwile na eyanjile mukubhoko kwo bhulyo kwa Nyamuwanga.
Abhanafunzi nibhagenda nokulasha wona, akatungu ako Bwana akolaga emilimu nabho nokwikilisha ligambo lyaye ebhijejekanyo bhabhonekanaga kwebhwe.
Abhanu bafu bhekomesishe okujitonda kisi emisango jinu jakumiye agati yeswe.
Lwakutyo eswe chayabhwilwe na bhanu bhajilolele na ameso kwambila kubhwambilo bhali bhakosi bho Omusango gwa Nyamuanga.
Kulwejo anye ona, nejile namala okukengela kisi obhwambilo bhwe emisango jona- nalola ati nikisi nikwandikile kubhwitondi bhwajo-Teofilo owechibhalo.
Koleleki utule okumenya echimali che emisango jinu weigisibhwe.
Munsiku ja Herode omukama wa Yudea, aliga alio omugabisi atogwaga Zakaria, owamulubho lwo obhugabhisi bhwa Abiya; omugasi waye Elizabeti aliga asokole muluganda lwa Haruni.
Abho bhone bhaliga bhali bhalengelesi imbele ya Nyamuanga bhagwatiliye ebhilagilo byona ebhyo Omukama na jindamu jaye.
Nawe bhaliga bhatana mwana, kulwokubha Elizabethi aliga alimugumba, na bhaliga bhakokoye muno.
Kakingile akatungu ko olubho lwa Zakaria okubha imbele ya Nyamuanga nakolaga emilimu jobhugabhisi,
Mbe nibhamusola okwingana lwa kutyo bhasolwaga mumilimu jo obugabhisi, agende mwiyekalu okututa omuchumulilo.
Katungu nibhatuta omuchumulilo elikofyanya lyaliga lilianja nilisabhwa.
Mbe Malaika wo Omukama amufulumukiyeko nemelegulu mukubhoko kwe ebhulyo okwe ebhigabhilo bhokututila.
Ejile Zakaria amulola natinyuka nabhamo nobhubha.
Nawe malaika namubhwila ati, “Wasiga kubhaya Zakaria, kulwokubha lisabhwa lyao lyongwibhwa. Omugasi wao Elijabeti kaja okwibhulila omwana we echilume. Risina lyaye umutoge Yoana.
Ulikondelwa nokusandabha, na bhanfu bhalikondelelwa ukwibhulwa kwaye.
Kulwokubha alibha mukulu imbele ya meso go Omukama. Atalinywa omulamba gwa majabhibhu amwi echinu chinu echitamisha, na alijusibhwa Mwoyo Mweru kusokelela munda ya nyilamwene.
Alubhasubhya bhanu bhafu bha Isiraeli kumukama Nyamuanga webhwe
Alitangata imbele yo obhusu bhwa Lata Bhugenyi kulwo mwoyo na mumanaga ga Eliya. Alikola kutyo koleleki asubye emitima ja abhebhusi kubhana, koleleki bhanyantongwa bhalame mubhwengeso bhwa abhalengelesi. Alikola kutyo okubhemalilisha bhanu bhelabhilwe okusolwa ingulu yaye.”
Zakaria nabhwila malaika ati, “Omusango gunu enigumenya kutiki? Kulwokubha anye nakokoye ke emyaka jo omugasi wani ona jabheye myafu muno.”
Malaika nasubhya namubhwila ati, “Anye nanye Gabhulyeli, unu nimeleguyu imbele ya Nyamuanga. Nitumilwe okuja nikubhwile omusango gunu ogwekisi.
Mbe lola oubha mujibhi, utakwaika kukingila kulusiku olwo jinu jilikumila. Kulwokubha walemele okwikilisha emisango jani ejojilikumila mukatungu akene.
Mbe abhanu bhaliga bhamulindiliye zakaria. Nibhalugula okulola namala omwanya mulela ali mwiyekalu.
Nawe ejile auluka atatule kwaika nabho. Nibhamenya ati aliga alolele chiroro mwiyekaru.
Nijibha ati ejile amala emilimu jo obhugabhisi nemuka okusubha ika owaye.
Ejile Zakaria amala okusubha ika okusoka kumilimu jaye eja muyekalu, omugasi waye nagega inda. Mbe namala mesi gatanu obhutasoka ika owaye. Naika ati,
“Linu nilyo Lata Bhugenyi amankolelea ejile ansima koleleki ansosheko jinswalo imbele ya abhanu.”
Inda ya Elijabheti yejile yakingya mesi mukaga, Nyamuanga atumile malaika Gabhulieli okugenda mumusi gwa Galilaya gunu ogutogwa Najareti,
ku muyalajuma unu asandwaga obhuko no mulume natogwa Yusufu. Omumula oyo aliga wamuluganda lwa Daudi, na lisina lyo omuyalajuma aliga natogwa Mariamu.
Ejile amukingako naika ati, “Uno omu! embe, unu Uyabhilwe libhando enene! Omukama ali amwi nawe.”
Nawe emisango ja malaika nijimusobhela nalema okumenya obhukesha obhwokulugusha bhunu bhuna nsongaki ku mwene.
Malaika namubhwila ati “Utobhaya, Mariamu, obha wabhwene ribhando ku Nyamuanga.
Rora ougega inda Munda yao no owibhula omwana na lisina ryae oumutoga Yesu. omwene
alibha mukuru alitogwa omwana wa unu ali inguru muno Lata Bhugenyi Nya Daudi esemwene
Alikama oruganda lwa Yakobo kajanende no bhukama bhwaye bhutaliwao.
Mariamu nabhusya malaika jiribha kutiki okubha nitana murume.
Malaika namubhira “moyo mweru alikwijila inguru yao, namanaga unu aliinguru muno Anja inguru yao. ku nokubha omwana unu kebhulwa alitongwa omwana wa Nyamuanga
Lola, omuili wao Elijabheti ali na inda yo mwana mu bhulame bhae obhwo bhukaluk. Kunu ni kwesi kwa sita kwa inda yae, unu aliga natogwa mugumba.
Kulwokubha litalio linu elimusinga Nyamuanga.”
Maliamu naikati, Lola, anye ndi mukosi we chigasi wa Nyamuanga. Siga jibhe kutyo aikile kwanye emisango jao.”Neya malaika namusiga.
Nio kunsiku ejo Mariamu nagenda bhwangu mu chalo chebhima, mu musi mu nsi ya Yudea.
Agendele nengila munyumba ya Jakalia namukesha Elijabheti.
Oli yabhonekene ati Elijabheti ejile inkesha ya Maliamu, omwana munda yae nejunga, na Elijabheti nejushwa no mwoyo mwelu.
Naikila ingulu kwo bhulaka bhunene,”una libhando agati ya bhagasi bhona, no mwana unu ali munda yao ona abhonekewe.
Jabhakutiki kwanye ati, nyila wa Latabhugenyi jimwiile aje kwanye?
Kulwokubha lola, anu nongwo obhulaka bhwo kukeshyanya kwao, omwana munda yani nejunga ku lwokusandabha.
Na abhonekeweomugasi oyo unu ekilisishe ati jakabhonekene jinu jaikilwe jili ja chimali jinu abhwiliwe okusoka ku Latabhugenyi.”
Maliamu naikati, omwoyo gwani ogumukuya Latabhugenyi,
No mwoyo gwani gukondelewemu Nyamuanga omukisha wani.
Kulwokubha amalola kutyo ali mwololoomukosi wae owechigasi. Lola, okwambila woli jinyibhulo jona ejija okumbilikila owamabhando.
Kulwokubha omwene owobhutulo amakola amgambo manene kwanye, na lisina lyae ni lyelu.
Nechigongo chae chilio okusoka maimbo na maimbo ku bhanu bhanu abhamwikilisha.
Olesishe amanaga kwo kubhoko kwae, anyalambuye bhanu bhekushaga ingulu yo bhwiganilisha bhwe mioyo jebhwe.
Abhatelemusishe ansi abhana bha bhakama okusoka kubhitebhe bhyebhwe ebhyobhukama no kubhakusha bhanu bhaliga bhagailwe.
Abhegusishe bhanu bhaliga bhana omweko gwe bhinu bhyekisi, tali abhanibhi abhabhilimishe bhatali na chinu.
Asosishe obhusakisi ku Israel omukosi wae, koleleki okwichuka okwolesha echigongo
(lwakutyo aikile ku bhalata bheswe) ku Abrahamu no lwibhulo lwae kajanende.”
Maliamu ekae na Elijabheti kwa mwanya gwa mesi gasatu kutya nio nasubha ika ewae.
Woli omwanya gwaliga gweile ogwa Elijabheti okwibhula omwana wae na nebhula omwana we chilume.
Abhekashanya bhae na bhaili bhae bhonguhywe kutyo Latabhugenyi amwikisishe echigongo kumwene, nibhakondelelwa amwi nage.
Woli jasokene ku lusiku lwa nane ati bhejile okumtenda omwana. Jaliga jibheile okumtoga lisina lyae,“Jakaliya,”kwo kulubha lisina lye esemwene,
Tali nyila wae nasubhya naikati,”Payi; kabhilikilwa Yowana.”
Nibhamubwilati, atalio na umwi amwi mubhaili bhao unu kabhilikilwa lisinaelyo.”
Nibhamukolela echijejekanyo esemwene wae okususanyisha omwene aliga nenda atogwe niga.
Esemwene nenda olubao lwo kwandikila, na nandikati,”Lisina lyae ni Yowana.”Bhona nibhalugusibhwa nelyo.
Aonao omunwa gwae nigwiguka no lulimi lwae nilusulumuka. Naloma nakumukusha Nyamuanga.
Nibhobhaya bhona bhanu bhaliga bhekae ayeyi nabho. Emisango ejo nijiswila muchalo chona echa mabhanga ga Yudeya.
Bhona bhanu bhagonguhye nibhagabhika mumitima jebhwe, nibhaika ati, “Omwana unu ni wakutiki?” Kulwokubha okubhoko kwa Nyamuanga kuliamwi nage.
Esemwene wae Jakaliya ejusibhwe no Mwoyo Mwelu nasosha obhulagi, naikati, Asimwe
Latabhugenyi, Nyamuanga wa Isilaeli, kulwokubha amasakila na amafulubhendela omwelulo gwa bhanu bhae.
Amachinamusisha liyembe elyomwelulo mu nyumba yo mukosi wae Daudi, okusoka mubhamwi bho luganda lwo mukosi wae Daudi,
Lwakutyo aikile kwo munwa gwa bhalagi bhae bhanu bhaliga bhalio ku mwanya gwa kala.
Kaja ochikisha okusoka kubhasoko bheswe no kusoka mumabhoko gabhanu bhachiyatile.
Alikola kutya okwolesha echigongo kubhalata, nokwichuka lilagano lyae lyo bhwelu,
no mulayi gunu aikile ku lata weswe Aburamu.
Alaiye okwolesha ati jakatulikene okumukolela Omwene atali na bhubuha, chisanga chamalile okuchungulwa okusoka mumabhoko ga bhasoko bheswe.
Mubhwelu no bhulengelesi lmbele yaye munsiku jeswe jona.
Yee, aona mwana, oubhilikilwa mulagi wa Unu ali ingulu muno, kulwokubha ouja okugenda mubhusu bhwa Latabhugenyi koleleki okumuchumila injila, okubhamenyesha abhanu kulwokuja kwae,
Okubhamenyesha abhanu bhae ati, bhalichungulwa kwo kwiswalililwa ebhibhibhi bhyebhwe.
Linu libhonekene kulwainsonga ye chigongo cha Nyamuanga weswe, kulwainsonga ati lisubha okusoka ingulu lilichijila,
Okumulikila bhanu bhanu bhekae muchisute na mwilengesi lyo lufu. Kakola kutyo okutangasha amagulu geswe mu njila yo mulembe.”
Woli, omwana oyo nakula nabha namanaga ge chinyamwoyo na ekae mwibhala kukinga olusiku lwo kubhonekana kwae ku Isilaeli.
Woli ku nsiku ejo, yabhonekene ati Kaisali Agusito asosishe obhulaka naikati bhugegibhwe obhukumi bhwa bhanu bhona munsi.
Bhunu bhwaliga bhuli bhubhasi bhwo kwamba bhunu bhakolekene omwanya gunu Kilenio ali mukama wa Siliya.
Kulwejo bhuli munu nagenda mumusi gwabho okubhalwa obhukumi.
Yusufu ona nasoka mumusi gwa Najaleti eyo Galilaya nasafili Yudeya mu musi gwa Beteleemu, gunu gwaliga nigumenyekana ati musi gwa Daudi, kulwokubha asokele mu luganda lwa Daudi.
Agendeleyo okwiyandika amwi na Maliyamu, unu aliga ali no bhuko nage naliga nibhenda obhona omwana.
Oli jabhonekene ati, bhachali eyo omwanya gwo kwibhula nigukinga.
Nebhula omwana we chilume, omwibhulwa wae owokwamba, namufwafya emyenda ataja kubhona mbeo omwana. Niwo namuta muchigoli echokulisishamo jintyanyi, kulwokubha bhatabhwene bhwanya mu nyumba ja bhagenyi.
Mulubhala olwo, bhaliga bhalio abhalefi bhanu bhaliga bhekae mumashamba nibhalinda amaijo ga jinyabhalega jebhwe mungeta.
Aonao, Malaika wa Latabhugenyi nabhabhonekela, na likusho lya Latabhugenyi ndinyenyegela okubheinda, nibhabha no bhubha muno.
“Niwo malaika nabhabhwilati,”Mutaja kubhaya, kulwokubha enibhaletela emisango jo bhwana jinu ejija okuleta bhukondelewe bhunene ku bhanu bhona.
Lelo Omuchungusi ebhulwa ingulu yemwe mumusi gwa Daudi! omwene niwe Kilisto Latabhugenyi!
Chinu nicho echibhalikisho chinu omuja oyanwa, omuja okumusanga omwana abhoelwe emyenda na amamile mu chigoli cho kulebhela jintyanyi.”
Aonao nilibhao eijo enene elya mulwile nibha amwi na malaika oyo nibhamukusha Nyamuanga, nibhaikati,
“Likusho libhe ku Nyamuanga unu ali ingulu muno, no mulembe gubhe muchalo ku bhanu bhona bhanu kakondelelwa nabho.”
Bhejile bhamalaika bhamala okugenda mulwile, abhalefi nibhaikana abhene kwa bhene, Chigende woli eliya Betelehemu, chijolola chinu chabhonekana, chinu Latabhugenyi achimenyesha.”
Nibhanguya okuja eliya, na nibhamusanga Maliamu na Yusufu, na nibhamulola omwana amamile muchigoli echokulisishamo jintyanyi.
Bhejile bhalola kutyo, nibhabhwila abhanu chinu bhaliga bhabhwiliwe ingulu yo mwana.
Bhona bhonguhye emisango ejo nibhalugula chinu chaikilwe na bhalefi.
Tali Maliyamu nagendelela okwiganilisha kujona jinu aligaonguhye, nagabhika mumwoyo gwae.
Abhalefi nibhasubha nibhamukusha no kumukuya Nyamuanga ku lwa bhuli chinu chinu bhonguhye no kulola, lwakutyo jaiga jaikilwe kubhene.
Lwejile okukinga olusiku lwa nane yaliga guli mwanya gwo kumutenda omwana, nibhamubhilikila Yesu, lisina linu ayanibhwe na malaika oyo achali na kujila nda,
Jejile jikalabhao jinsiku jo kusomoka, okulubhana na bhilagilo bhya Musa, Yusufu na Maliyamu nibhamusila mwi yekalu eliya Yelusalemi okumta imbele ya Latabhugenyi.
Lwakutyo jandikilwe mu bhilagilo bhya Latabhugenyi,”Bhuli mulume unu kamba okwibhulwa katogwa unu asosibhwe ku Latabhugenyi.”
Abhenene ona bhejile okusosha echogo okulubhana na chinu chaikilwe mu bhilagilo bhya Latabhugenyi,”Njibha ebhili amwi bhana bhabhili bha jinguti.”
Lola, aliga alio munu umwi mu Yelusalemu unu abhilikilwaga lisina lyae Simiyoni. omunu unu aliga alimulengelesi na namulamyaga Nyamuanga. Omwene aliga nalinda okulola omusimbagilisha wa Isilaeli, no mwoyo mwelu aliga ali ingulu yae.
Aliga amalile okuswelulibhwa no mwoyo mwelu ati atakufwa achali kumulola Kilisto wa Latabhugenyi.
Lusiku lumwi ejile munda ya iyekalu, natangasibhwa no Mwoyo Mwelu. Anu abhebhusi nibhamuleta omwana, Yesu, okumukolela ganu galiga geile okulubhana ne bhilagilo,
Niwo Simiyoni namulamila mumabhoko gae, na namukuya Nyamuanga naikati,
“Woli numwikilishe omukosi wao agende kwo mulembe Latabhugenyi, okulubhana na ligambo lyao.
Kulwokubha ameso gani galola omwelulo gwao,
Gunu ogubhonekana mumeso gabhanu bhona.
Omwene ni bhwelu bhwo obhuswelulo ku bhanu bha Maanga na likushyo kubhanu bha Isilaeli.”
Esemwene na Nyilamwene nibhalugushwa na magambo ganu galomwaga ingulu yae.
Niwo Simiyoni nabhasabhwila amabhando na naika ku nyila mwene Maliyamu ati,”Tegelesha kwo bhwenge! Omwana unu kaja kubha njuno yo kubhula no kukila kwa bhanu bhamfu mu Isilaeli na nichibhalikisho chinu bhanu bhamfu abhaja okuchilema.
Nawe ni panga linu elisoma mumwoyo gwao omwene, koleleki obhwiganilisha bhwe mioyo ja bhamfu jibhonekane.”
Omulagi omugasi unu atogwaga Ana ona aliga alimo mwi yekalu. Omwene aliga ali muyala wa Fanueli okusoka muluganda lwa Asheli. Aliga ali ne miyaka myamfu muno. Ekae no mulume wae miyaka saba bhatwalene,
Nio nafwilwa omulume nekala miyaka makumi munana nena. Omwene atasoka mwiyekalu na aliga nagendelela okumulamya Nyamuanga amwi no kusibha no kusabha, mungeta na mumwisi.
Nakumwanya ogwo, ejile anu bhaliga bhali namba okumusima Nyamuanga. Alomele ingulu yo mwana kubhuli munu unu aliga nalinda omwelulo gwa Yelusalemi.
Bhejile bhamala bhuli chinu jinu jaliga jiile okukolwa okulubhana na ebhilagilo bhya Latabhugenyi, nibhasubha Galilaya, mumusi gwabho, Najaleti.
Omwana akulile, na nabha namanaga, nabha no bhwengeso, ne chigongo cha Nyamuanga chaliga chili ingulu yae.
Abhebhusi bhae bhuli mwaka bhagendaga Yelusalemu ingulu yo lusiku lukulu olwa ipasaka.
Ejile abha ne miyaka ekumi ne bhili, bhagendele lindi lwa kutyo jintugwa jebhwe jaliga jili ingulu yo lusiku lukulu.
Bhejile okusigala nsiku jona ingulu yo lusiku lukulu, nibhamba okusubha mumisi jebhwe. Tali omusigaji Yesu asigae inyuma Muyelusalemu na abhebhusi bhae bhatamenyaga ogwo.
Bhetogelagati alimo mwiijo linu bhaliga nibhalibhata nalyo, kulwejo nibhalibhata lugendo lwa lusiku lumwi. Niwo nibhamba okumuyenja mubhaili na mubhasani bhebhwe.
Bhejile bhasingwa okumubhona, bhasubhile Yelusalemu nibhamba okumuyenja omwo.
Nibhonekana ati bhejile bhamala nsiku esatu, nibhamubhona mwi yekalu, enyanjile agati ya bheigisha, nabhategelesha no kubhabhusha amabhusho.
Bhona bhanu bhamunguhye bhalugulile obhwengeso bhwae na masubhyo gae.
Bhejile bhamubhona, nibhalugula. Nyila mwene namubhwilati,”Mwana wani, kulwaki wachikola kutya? Tegelesha, esomwana nanye chaliga nichikuyenja kwo kwitimata muno.”
Nabhabhwila ati,”Kulwaki aliga nimunyenja? Mtamenyagati jinyiile okubhamo mu nyumba ya Lata wani?
Tali bhatamenyele chinu aliga naikilila ku magambo ago.
Niwo nagenda amwi nabho okukinga ika Najaleti na aliga ali mwikeyi kubhene. Nyila mwene abhikile amagambo ago mumwoyo gwae.
Tali Yesu agendelee okukula mu bhwengeso no bhukulu, nagendelela okwendwa na Nyamuanga na bhanu.
Woli, mumwaka gwa kumi na tano ogwokukama bhwa Kaisali Tibelia, omwanya ogwo Pontiyo Pilato aliga ali mukama wa Uyaudi, Helode aliga ali mukulu wo mukoa gwa Galilaya, na Filipo mumulawabho aligaali mukulu wo mukowa Ituleya na Tlakoniti, na Lisania aliga ali mukulu wo mukoa gwa Abilene,
Omwanya ogwomugabhisi mukulu owa Anasi na Kayafa, Ligambo lya Nyamuanga lyamwijie Yowana mwana wa Jakaliya, mwibhala.
Nalibhata mumukowa gwona okwiinda Yolodani, nalasha obhubhatijwa bhwo kuta kulwokusasibhwa ebhibhibhi
Kutyo jandikilwe muchitabho magambo ga Isaya omulagi,”Obhulaka bhwo munu unu kalagilisha mwibhala,”Muichume injla ya Latabhugenyi, mukole injila yae inu imile.
Bhuli kolongo elijusibhwa, bhuli bhanga ne bhibhanga ebhinyalambulwa, jinjila jinu jikotele ejigololwa, na jinjila jinu jilina magunguli jilinyalambulilwa.
Bhanu bhona bhali bhulola obhwelulo bhwa Nyamuanga.”
Kulwejo, Yowana nabhwila elikofyanya enene elyabhanu bhanu bhajaga okubhatijwa nage,”Emwe olwibhulo lwa injoka yo bhusungu, niga unu amabhakabhusha okubhilima lisungu linu elija?
Mwibhule amatwasho ganu agagendana no kuta, na mutaja kwaika munda yemwe,”Chinage Ibulaimu unu ali lata weswe; kulwokubha enibhabhwila ati, Nyamuanga katula okumubhonela abhana okusoka ku mabhuyi ganu.
Nawoli inshoka iteweyo kumisi ja mati. Kulwejo, bhuli ti linu litakwibhula matwasho ga kisi, elitemwa no kweswa mumulilo.
Nibheya abhanu bha mwiijo nibhamubhusha nibhaikati,”Woli jichiile chikoleki?”
Abhasubhishe naikati,”labha omunu ali na nkanju ebhili jimwiile asoshe nkanju imwi ku undi unu atanayo silisili, na unu ali nebhilyo ona nakole kutyo.”
Nibheya amwi ya bhatobhesha bhushulu nibhaja okubhatijwa, na nibhamubhwila ati,”Mwiigisha, jichiile chikole kutiki?
Nabhabhwilati, Musige okumanya jiyela kukila kutyo omwendibhwa okukumanya.”
Na amwi ya bhasilikale ona nibhamubhusha nibhaikati,”Kaoli eswe kutiki? Echendibhwa chikole kutiki?”Nabhabhwilati, Mutaja kugega jiyelaku munu wonawona kwa managa, mutaja kumubheelesha munu wonawona kwo lubheyi. mwihye ne miyelo jemwe”
Woli, kulwokubha abhanu bhaliga bhano bhwila bhwo kumulinda Kilisto unu alija, bhuli munu aliga neganilisha mumwoyo gwae ingulu ya Yowana labha niwe Kilisto.
Yowana nasubhya kwo kubhabhwila bhona ati,”Anye enibhabhatija kwa manji, tali alio umwi unu kaja unu ali na managa kukila anye, na anye niteile kusulumula jingoe je bhilato bhyae. Kabhabhatija emwa kwo mwoyo mwelu na kwomulilo.
Lisungulilo lyae lili mumabhoko gae koleleki achumechume kisi owokusungulila ingano no kuikumanya muchitala chae. Tali kasingalisha ingunyu kwo mulilo gunu gutakusima.
Kwo kubhatongela agandi mamfu ona, alasishe emisango jo bhwana kubhanu,
Yowana amuganyishe ona Helode omukulu wo mukowa kwo kutwala Helodiya, omugasi wo mumula wabho na kwobhunyamuke bhwamfu bhunu Helode aliga nakola.
Tali eile Helode akolele obhunyamuke obhundi bhubhibhi muno. Namubhoya Yowana mwibhoelo.
Njiya njisokanati, omwanya gunu abhanu bhona bhaliga nibhabhatijwa na Yowana, Yesu ona abhatijishwe. Omwanya ogwo asabhilwe, olwile nilwiguka.
Omwoyo Mwelu natuka ingulu yae kulwolususo lwa lilengesi lya inguti, omwanya ogwo obhulaka nibhuja okusoka mulwile nibhwaikati,”Awe ulimwana wani mwendwa. Enikondelwa muno na nawe”
Oli Yesu omwene, ejile amba okufundisha, aliga ali ne myaka makumi gasatu. Aliga ali mwana (lwakutyo aliga nibheganilisha) wa Yusufu, omwana wa Eli,
omwana wa Mathati, omwana wa Lawi, omwana wa Meliki, omwana wa Yana, omwana wa Yusufu,
Omwana wa Matasiya, omwana wa Amosi, omwana wa Nahumu, omwana wa Esili, omwana wa Nagayi,
Omwana wa Maati, omwana wa Matasiya, omwana wa Semeini, omwana wa Yusufu, omwana wa Yuda,
Omwana wa Yoanani, omwana wa Resa, omwana wa Zelubabeli, omwana wa Sheatieli, omwana wa Neli,
Omwana wa Meliki, omwana wa Adi, omwana wa Kosamu, omwana wa Elimadamu, omwana wa Eli,
Omwana wa Yoshuwa, omwana wa Eliezeli, omwana wa Yolimu, omwana wa Matasi, omwana wa Lawi,
Omwana wa Simeoni, omwana wa Yuda, omwana wa Yusufu, omwana wa Yonamu, omwana wa Eliyakimu,
Omwana wa Meleya, omwana wa Mena, omwana wa Matasa, omwana wa Nathani, omwana wa Daudi,
Omwana wa Yese, omwana wa Obedi, omwana wa Boazi, omwana wa Salimoni, omwana wa Nashoni,
Omwana wa Abinadabu, omwana wa Alamu, omwana wa Hesiloni, omwana wa Pelesi, omwana wa Yuda,
omwana wa Yakobo, omwana wa Isaka, omwana wa Iblaimu, omwana wa Tela, omwana wa Naholi,
Omwana wa Seluig, omwana wa Lagau, omwana wa Pelegi, omwana wa Ebeli, omwana wa Sala,
Omwana wa Kenani, omwana wa Alufakisadi, omwana wa Shemu, omwana wa Nuhu, omwana wa Lameki,
Omwana wa Metusela, omwana wa Henoko, omwana wa Yaledi, omwana wa Mahalalei, omwana wa Kenani,
Omwana wa Enoshi, omwana wa Seti, omwana wa Adamu, omwana wa Nyamuanga.
Neya, Yesu ejuye Omwoyo Mwelu, nasubha okusoka mumugela gwa Yelodani, atangasibhwe no Mwoyo okuja mwibhala.
Kwa nsiku makumi gana, neyo nalegejibhwa na shetani. Omwanya ogwo atalyaga chinu chonachona, no bhutelo onguhye injala.
Shetani namubhwila ati,”Labha uli mwana wa Nyamuanga, libhwile libhuyi linu gubhe mukate.”
Yesu nasubhya naikati,”Jandikilwe, omunu atakulama kwe mikate jenyele.”
Neya Shetani namutangasha okuja kuchinsonge che chima, namwolesha obhuka bhwona bhwe chalo kwo mwanya mufuyi.
Shetani namubhwilati,”Enikuyana obhutulo obhwokukama amwi na likusho lyabho. Enitula okukola kutyo kulwokubha niyanibhwe bhyona nibhikame, na enitula okumuyana wonawona unu enenda.
Kulwejo, ukanyifukamila no kundamya, ebhinu bhyona bhinu ebhibha bhyawo.”
Tali Yesu asubhishe namubhwilati,”Yandikilwe, Nibhusibhusi umulamye Latabhugenyi Nyamuanga wao, na nibhusibhusi umukolele omwene ela.”
Amalile Shetani namutangasha Yesu okukinga Yelusalemu namuta ingulu chimwi eya liyekalu namubhwilati,”Labha uli mwana wa Nyamuanga nulagale ansi okusokanu.
Kulwokubha yandikilwe,”Kabhalagilila bha malaika bhae bhakulamile no kukulinda,
na abhakwimusha ingulu mumabhoko gebhwe koleleki utaja kuutasha amagulu gao ingulu ya mabhuyi”
Yesu nasubhya namubhwilati,“Jaiikilwe,”utamulegeja Latabhugenyi Nyamuanga wao.”
Shetani ejile amala okumulegeja Yesu, nagenda jae namusiga kukinga mwanya gundi.
Neya Yesu nasubha Galilaya kwa managa go Mwoyo, na jinkuma jae nijiswila muchalo chona chinu aliga bhasijene nacho chona.
Eiigisishe mu mekofyanyisho gebhwe, na bhuli munu amukuyishe
Lusiku lumwi agendele Najaleti, omusi gunu ebhuliwemo nokukulilamo. Lwakutyo yaliga ili ntugwa yae nengila mulikofyanyisho olusiku lwa isabhato, emeleguyu no kusoma amaandiko.
Ayanibhwe echitabho cho mulagi Isaya, kulwejo, nafumbula echitabho naiga anu kandikilwe,
Omwoyo gwa Latabhugenyi guli ingulu yani, kulwokubha anyitilie amfuta okusimula emisango jo bhwana ku bhataka. Antumile okulasha okusulumulwa kwa bhanu bhabhoelwe, nokukola bhanu bhatakulola bhabhone okulola lindi. Okubhokola bhanu abhaijmibhwa bhasige ojimibhwa,
Okulashaomwaka gunu Latabhugenyi kolesha obhwekisi bhwae.”
Namala nafumbika echitabho, namusubhisha omutangasha we likofyanyisho, nenyanja ansi. Ameso gabhanu bhona bhanu bhaliga bhali mulikofyanyisho nibhamulola omwene.
Namba okuloma nabho naikati, Lelo elyandiko linu lyakumila mumatwi gemwe.”
Bhuli munu aliya amenyele chinu Yesu aliga naika, na bhamfu amwi yebhwe bhalugusibhwe na magambo go bhwengeso ganu gasokaga mukanwa kae. Bhaliga nibhaikati”unu atali mwana wa Yusufu, jitali kutyo?”
Yesu nabhabhwilati,”chimali omuja okwaika olugani lunu kwanye ati, Omuwosha, ikisha awe omwene. Chonachona chonguhye nukola Kapelinaumu, nuchikole anu muchijiji chao.”
Nalindi naikati,”chimali enibhabhwila emwe ati, atalio mulagi unu abhamwikilisha muchalo chae.”
Tali enibhabhwila emwe echimli ati bhaliga bhalio abhagasi bhamfu bhanu bhaliga bhafwilile na bhalume mu Isilaeli omwanya gwa Eliya, omwanya gunu olwile lwafungilwe ngubha kugwa payi kwo mwanya gwa miyaka esatu na nusu, anu yabheewo injala nyafu muno mu chalo chona.
Tali Eliya atatumilwe ku umwi wabho, tali ku kuumwi unu aliga ali Seleputa ayeyi no musi gwa Sidoni.
Nalindi bhaliga bhalio abhagenge bhamfu mu Isilaeli mu mwanya gwao mulagi Elisha, tali atabheeo hata umwi unu eulisibhwe tali Naamani omunu wa Siliya.
Abhanu bhona munda ye likofyanyisho nibhejula na lisungu bhejile bhwongwa ejo jona.
Bhemeleguyu nibhamuulusha anja yo musi, nibhamtangasha okukinga kubhenenelo bhe chima cho musigunu gwombakilwe ingulu yae, koleleki bhamwese ansi.
Tali alabhileo agati yebhwe naja jae.
Neya natebhela Kapelenaumu, mumusi gwa Galilaya. Isabhato imwi aliga neigisha abhanu Munda ya lisomelo.
Nibhalugula kulwameigisho gae, kulwokubha eigisishe ku lwo bhutulo.
Olusiku olwo Munda ye likofyanyisho, aligaalio omunu wa musabwa mubhibhi, alilile kwo bhulaka bhwa ingulu,”
Chili naki nawe, Yes wa Najaleti? waja okuchisimagisha? Enimenya awe nawega! Awe nawe omwelu wa Nyamuanga!”
Yesu nagonya omusabwa nagubhwilati,”Jibhila Jibhila na umusokemo omunu unu!”Omusabwa ogwo nigumubha ansi agati yebhwe, gwamusokeleko bila kumukolela bhusasi bhwonabhwona.
Abhanu bhona nibhalugula, nibhagendelela okuloma omusango ogwo bhuli munu no wejabho. Nibhaika,”ni magamboki ganu?”Kalagilila amasabwa kwo bhuinga na manage nigabhasokako.”
Kulwejo, jinkuma ja Yesu nijiswila bhuli mbala okwiinda omukowa ogwo.
Neya Yesu nasokamo mumusi omwo nengila munyumba ya Simoni. Oli, nyabhuko war Simoni aliga Ali nomuswija mwamfu, nibhamulembeleja ingulu yae.
Kulwejo, Yesu namufogelela, nagonya omuswija ogwo na nigumusokako. Awo nawo nemelegulu namba okubhafulubhendela.
Lisubha lyejile lyagwa, Abhanu nibhamulembeleja Yesu bhuli munu unu abhaga no mulwae wa malwala ga bhuli mbaga. Nabhatako amabhoko gae ingulu yebhwe na nabhaosha bhona.
Amasambwa gona gabhasokeleko bhamfu nigasekana nigaikati,”Awe nawe omwana wa Nyamuanga!”Yesu nagonya amasabwa na atagekilisishe gaike, kulwokubha gamenyele ati omwene niwe Kilisto.
Bhwejile obhwile bhwela, naja mulubhala lunu atabhaoga munu. Amekofyanya ga bhanu bhaliga nibhamulembeleja na nibhaja anualigali. Nibhenda okumwingilila atajakugenda Kula nabho.
Nawe nabhabhwila ati,”Nibhusibhusi nilashe emisango jo bhwana ejobhukama bhwa Nyamuanga mumisi ejindi myamfu, kulwokubha inu niyo injuno inu nitumilwe Anu.”
Neya nagendelesha okulasha Munda ya amekofyanyisho mu bhuyaudi Yona.
Mbe jabhonekene omwanya gunu abhanu bhamwikumanyisheko Yesu nibhategelesha omusango gwa Nyamuanga, aliga emeleguhyu kunchechekela yo mwalo gwa Genesaleti.
Alolele mato gabhili gesele jinanga mulubhaju lwo mwalo. Abhategi bhaliga bhasokelemo nabhaliga nibhafula emitego jebhwe.
nengila nengila mubhwato bhumwi, inu yaliga ili ya Simoni namusabhwa aisile mubhusibha katyali. Neya neigisha okusokelela mubhwato omwo.
Naloma, namubhwila Simoni ati,” Sila obhato okukinga ebhusibha na utege emitego jao koleleki with jinswi.
“Simoni nasubhya naikati, Latabhugenyi, chakolele emilimu ngeta Yona, chichali kubhona chonachona, Tali kwo musango gwao, enijitega emitego.
Bhejile bhakola kutyo bhetile nswi nyafu muno na emitego jebhwe nijamba okutemuka.
Kulwejo nibhalagilisha abhejabho mubhwato obhundi bhaje okubhasakila. Bhejile nibhejusha amato gebhwe gonna, amato nigalebhelela okwika.
Tali Simoni Petelo, ejile alola kutyo, aguye mumagulu ga Yesu naikati,”Soka kwanye, kulwokubha any nili munu we bhibhibhi Latabhugenyi.”
Kulwokubha alugusibhwe, nabhanu bhaliga bhalio amwi nage, kubhwiti bhwa jinswi jinu bhaliga bhetile.
Linu lyabhatee amwi Yakobo na Yohana abhana bha Jebhedayo, bhanu bhaliga bhamwi na Simoni. Na Yesu namubhwila Simoni ati, Utajakubhaya, kulwokubha kwambila oli no kugendelela ouja okubha mutegi wa bhanu.”
Bhejile bhaleta amato gebhwe kuchalo, bhasigile bhuli chinu nibhamulubha omwene.
Jasokene kutya anu aliga ali mumusi amwi mwijo, omunu umwi aliga ejuye ebhigenge aliga alimo omwo. Omwanya gunu amulolele Yesu, aguhye nafukama obhusu bhwae ansi nasabhwa, naikati,”Latabhugenyi, ukabha nuwenda, outula okumwosha.
“ Neya Yesu nagolola okubhoko kwae namukunyako, naikati,”Enenda. Nuwole.”Omwanya ogwogwo obhugenge nibhumuwako.
“Amulagilie ataja kubhwila munu wonawona, tali amubhwilie,”Genda jao, ujokwiyolesha ku bhagabhisi na usoshye echiyanwa cho kuosibhwa kwao, chinu Musa alagilie, bhubhwe bhubhambasi kubhene.”
Tali jinkuma ingulu yae nijiswila alela nao, na bhanu bhamfu nibhaja okumtegelesha neigisha no kwiulisha amalwala gebhwe.
Tali bhuli katungu esumbaga wenyele no kusabhwa.
Jasokene lusiku lumwi lunu aliga neigisha, bhaliga bhalio Amafalisayo na bhalimu bhwa jishelia bhenyanjile ao bhejile okusoka mubhijiji bhyamfu bhatasokele mumukoa gwa Galilaya na Yudeya, no kusokelela mumusi gwa Yelusalemi. Amanaga ga Latabhugenyi galiga gali amwi nage okwiulisha
Abhanu abhandi bhejile, bhagegele omunu unu aliga afuhye omubhili, nibhaenjelesha injila yokumwingisha munda koleleki bhamumamye imbele ya Yesu.
Bhatabhwene njila yo kumwingisha munda kulwokubha abhanu bhaliga bhali bhamfu, kulwejo nibhalinya kuluswi lwa inyumba nibhamutelemusha okulabhila mubhigae, ingulu omukeka gwae agati ya bhanu, imbele chimwi ya Yesu.
Nalola elikilisha lyebhwe, Yesu naikati,”Musani, ebhibhibhi bhyao wasasilwa.”
Abhandiki na Mafalisayo nibhamba okubhusha elyo, nibhaikati,”Unu niga unu kaika ejokufuma? Niga unu katula okusasila ebhibhibhi tali ni Nyamuanga wenyele?”
Tali Yesu, aliga amenyele chinu bheganilishaga, abhasubhishe naikati,”Kulwaki omubhushanya linu mumiyo jemwe?
Niki chinu chili bhwangu okwaikati,'Ebhibhibhi bhya bhyasasilwa' angu okwaikati imelegulu ulibhate?
Tali mumenye ati Omwana wa Adamu ali no bhutulo muchalo obhwokusasila ebhibhibhi, Enikubhwila awe, Imuka, gega omukeka gwao ugende ika ewao.”
Omwanya ogwogwo nemuka imbele yebhwe nagega omukeka gwae gunu aliga amamiye. Neya nasubha ikewae namukusha Nyamuanga.
Bhuli munu alugusibhwe na nibhamukuya Nyamuanga. Bhejuhye no bhubha, nibhaikati,”Chalola ganu galiga kulugusha lelo.”
Gejile galabhao magagambo ago, Yesu asokeleyo namulola omutobhesha wo bhushulu unu atogwaga Lawi enyanjile anu bhatobhesishaga likodi. Namubhwilati,”Ndubha”
Kulwejo Lawi nemuka namulubha, nasiga bhuli chinu inyuma.
Neya Lawi nakola ikewae obhugenyi bhunene ingulu ya Yesu. Bhaliga bhalio abhatobhesha bho bhushulu bhamfu eyo na bhanu bhamfu bhanu bhaliga bhenyanjile kumeja nibhalya amwi nabho.
Tali Amafalisayo na bhandiki bhebhwe bhaliga nibhabhafwimbila abheigisibhwa, nibhaikati,”Kulwaki omulya no kunywa na bhatobhesha bho bhushulu na bhanu bhwe ebhibhibhi?”
Yesu nabhasubhyati, “Abhanu bhanu bhali bhaanga bhatakwenda mulagusi, nibhanwila abhalwala nibho abhenda omulagusi.
Nitejile okubhabhilikila abhalengelesi bhabhone okuta, tali abhebhibhi bhabhone okuta.”
Nibhamubhwilati, “Abheigisibhwa bha Yowana mala kamfu abhasibha no kusabhwa, na abheigisibhwa bha Bhafalisayo bhona abhakola kutyo, Tali abheeigisibhwa bhao abhalya no kunywa.”
Yesu nabhabhwilati, “Eitulikana omunu wonawona akabhakola bhanu bhajiye mubhulegesi bhwo Mutwasi okusibha Omutwasi achalio nabhwo?
Tali jinsiku ejija anu Omutwasi alasokao agati yebhwe, niwo kunsiku ejo abhasibha.”
Neya Yesu naloma nabho kwe bhijejekanyo.”Atalio unu katemula ingubho inyaya natula kungubho ya kala. Na akakola kutyo, katemula ingubho inyaya, nechibhutu echiyaya okusoka ku ngubho inyaya chiteyile okuta kungubho ya kala.
Nakulwejo atalio munu unu katao idivai inyaya mubhunu ebhikokolo. Na akakola kutyo, idivayi inyaya eifumula echinu echo, na idivayi niitika, nebhinu nibhinyamuka.
Tali idivayi inyaya nibhusibhusi bhaitule mubhinu bhyekisi.
Na atalio munu anywee idivayi ya kala, unu atakwenda inyaya, kwainsonga kaikati,”Eyakala ni kis
Oli yasokene ku lusiku lwa isabhato ati Yesu na bheigisibhwa bhae alabhile mwi bhwi linu lyaliga lilimo obhulo nibhamba okulya eminani, nibhagakubhila mumabhoko gebhwe nibhalya obhulo.
Tali agati ya Mafalisayo nibhaikati,”Kulwaki omukola echinu chinu chitakwendibhwa okukolwa kulusiku lwa isabhato”?
Yesu, nabhasubhya, naikati, “Chaliga kusoma chinu Daudi anu aliga ali nainjala, omwene amwi na bhalume bhanu bhaliga bhaliamwi?
Agendele mu nyumba ya Nyamuanga, nagega emikate emyelu no kulya ejindi, no kuyana abhanu abhandi bhanu bhaliga bhanage nibhalya, nolokutyo jaliga jili jo kulibhwa na bhagabhisi.”
Neya nabhabhwila,”Omwana wa Adamu ni Latabhugenyi wa Isabhato.”
Jabhonekene ku lusiku lwa Sabhato eindi agendele mulikofyanyisho neigisha abhanu eyo. Aliga alio omunu umwi unu okubhoko kwae okwebhulyo kwaliga kufuye ganzi.
Abhandiki na Mafalisayo bhaliga nibhamulola kwo kumwitegelesha labha kaja okumuosha ku lusiku lwa Isabhato, koleleki bhabhone injuno yo kumusitaka kwa likosa elyo.
Tali amenyele chinu bhaliga nibheganilisha na naika kuunu aliga afuye okubhoko,”Imuka, imelegulu agati ya bhuli munu,”Kulwejo omunu oyo nemuka nemelegulu awo.
Yesu naika kwebhwe ati,”Enibhabhusha emwe, ni jakisi kulusiku lwa Isabhato okukola ja kisi au okukola obhujabhi, okukisha obhuanga angu okugasingalisha?” Nabhalola bhona namubhwila omunu oyo,
“Golola okubhoko kwao.”Nakola kutyo, no kubhoko kwae nikwiulila.
Tali nibhejulwa na lisungu, nibhaikana abhene kwa bhene nichiya chinu chiile bhakole kwa Yesu.
Jabhonekene ati ajiye mwibhanga okusabha. Abheeyo ngeta Yona namusabhaga Nyamuanga.
Yejile yakinga katondo, nabhilikila abheigisibhwa bhae kumwene, na nabhasola akumi na bhabhili agati yebhwe, bhanu atogele “ntumwa”
Amasina ga jintumwa galiga Simoni (unu abhilikilwaga Petelo) na Andelea amumula wabho, Yakobho, Yohana, Filipo, Balitolomayo,
Matayo, Tomaso, na Yakobho omwana wa Alufayo, Simoni, unu atogelwe Zelote,
Yuda omwana wa Yakobho na Yuda Isikaliyote, unu abhee muli wa iniku.
Neya Yesu natebhela nabho okusoka mwibhanga nemelegulu kulutanga. Nechiyo Cha abheigisibhwa bhae bhaliga eyo, amwi na bhanu bhanu bhamfu okusoka Bhuyaudi na Yelusalemi, nokusoka kumbalama ya Till na Sidoni.
Bhejile okumtegelesha no kwiulisibhwa amalwae gebhwe. Abhanu bhaliga nibhanyasibhwa na masabwa amabhibhi bhona bheulisibhwe.
Bhuli umwi mulikofyanyisho alegejaga okumukunyako kulwokubha amanaga go kuwosha aliga njisoka Munda yae na abheulisishe bhona.
Neya nabhasola abheigisibhwa bhae, naikati, Muna libhando abho muli bhataka, kulwokubha obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga ni bhwemwe.
Muna libhando bhanu Muna injala woli, kulwokubha omuja okwigusibhwa. Muna libhando bhanu omulila woli, kulwokubha omuja okuseka.
Muna libhando emwe bhanu abhanu abhaja okubhalema no kubhasolola no kubhabheelesha emwe ati mulibhajabhi, kulwainjuno yo Mwana wa Adamu.
Mukondelelwe, kunsiku ejo nimwijungajunga kwo bhukondelewe, kulwokubha chimali omubhona omuyelo munene mulwile, kulwokubha bhesemwene bhabhakolee kutyo abhalagi.
Tali jilibhabhona bhanu muli bhanibhi! kulwokubha mwamalile okubhona okusimbagilisibhwa kwemwe. Jilibhabhona bhanu mwigutile woli! kulwokubha omuja olumwa injala.
Jilibhabhona bhanu omuseka woli! kulwokubha omuja okulila chililo chinene.
Jilibhabhona emwe, mulikuibhwa na bhanu bhona! Kulwokubha bhesemwene bhebhwe bhabhakolee kutyo abhalagi bho lubheyi kutyo kutyo.
Tali enaika nemwe bhanu omuntegelesha, mubhende abhasoko bhemwe nokubhakolela jakisi bhanu bhabhasokele.
Mubhayane amabhando bhanu abhabhafumilisha emwe na mubhasabhilwe bhanu abhabhajimya.
Kuunu kakubhuma litama limwi, muindulile nelyakabhili. Nomunu akakutesha omwambalo gwao utamuganya na inkanju.
Muyane bhuli unu kakusabhwa. Labha omunu akakutesha echinu chili chao, utamusabhwa akusubhishe.
Lwakutyo omwenda abhanu bhabhakolee, emwona mubhakolele kutyokutyo.
Labha mukenda abhanu bhanu abhabhendala, ogwo ni muyeloki kwemwe? Kulwokubha hata abhebhibhi ona abhenda bhanu abhabhendala.
Nalabha mukabhakolela agekisi, ogwo nimuyeloki kwimwe? Kulwokubha abhebhibhi bhona abhakola kutyo kutyo.
Nalabha mukakopesha ebhinu kubhanu bhanu omwiikanya ati abhabhasubhisha, ogwo nimuyeloki kwemwe? Nolo abhebhibhi bhona abhabhakopesha abhebhibhibhi, na abheikanya okulamila obhukumi obhwo obhwo Lindi.
Tali mubhende abhasoko bhemwe na mubhakolele ja kisi. Mubhakopeshe na mutaja kubhaya ingulu yo okusubhisibhwa, no muyelo gwemwe ogubha munene. Omubha bhana bha Unu ali ingulu, kulwokubha omwene ni wakisi kubhanu bhatali na some nabhajabhi.
Mubhe nechigongo, Lwakutyo Lata wemwe ali wechigongo.
Mutalamula, kuti emwe mutalilamulwa. Mutalifumilisha, emwona mutalifumilisibhwa. Musasilega abhandi, emwona mulisasilwa.
Mubhayane abhandi, emwona omuyanibhwa. Obhwamfu bhwo bhufula bhunu bhwigatiwe, nokugelelela no kwitika echitika kubhijwi bhyemwe. Kulwokubha indengo yonayona inu omulengelamo, indengo eyo eyo ona mulilengelwamo”.
Neya nabhabhwila echijejekanyo ona. “Angu omunu unu alimuofu katula okumtangasha omuofu oundi? Labha akolele kutyo, bhona bhakatubhiye mulyobho, angu bhatakatubhiye?
Omwiigisibhwa atakubha mukulu kukila omwiigisha wae, tali bhuli munu akamala okwiigisibhwa kwo bhulengelesi kabha lwo mwiigisha wae.
Kulwaki woli oulola akakongokela kanu kali muliso lyo mumula wanyu, na liti linu lilimuliso lyawo utalilola?
Outula atiki okumubhwila omula wanyu,'Wasu, enisabha nikusoshemo akakongokela kanu kali muliso lyao,'nawe awe utakulola liti linu lilimuliso lyao awe omwene? Mubheyi awe! Yamba okusoshamo liti muliso lyao omwene, niwo oulola kisi akakongokela kanu kali muliso lyo mumula wanyu.
Kulwokubha litalio eti lyakisi linu elitwasha matwasho mabhibhi, nalitalio liti libhibhi linu elibhula matwasho ga kisi.
Kulwokubha bhuliti elimenyekana ku lwa matwasho galyo. kulwokubha abhanu bhatakutongola jitini okusoka kumawa, na bhatakutongola jijabhibhu okusoka kumasongama.
Omunu wo bhwana kasosha mwibhikilo lyae lyo mwoyo jinu jili jo bhwana, no munu omunyamuke mu chibhikilo chae cho bhunyamuke bhwo mwoyo gwae gwo bhunyamuke ogusosha jinu jili jo bhunyamuke. Kulwokubha omunwa gwae ogwaika ganu gejuhye mumwoyo gwae.
Kulwaki omumbilikila, 'Latabhugenyi, Latabhugenyi, 'na mutagakola ganu enaika?
Bhuli munu unu kaja kwanye nokungwa emisango jani no kujikolela emilimu, enibholesha kutyo kasusa.
Kasusana no munu unu ombakile inyumba yae, unu asimbile muno ansi, nombaka omusingi gwa inyumba kulutale lukomee. Anu induluma yejile, emigela ja manji njiibhuma inyumba, nawe katatulile kuisingisha, kulwokubha yaliga yumbakilwe kisi.
Tali wona wona unu onguhye emisango jani nalema okujikola, kasusana no munu unu ombakile inyumba yae ingulu yo musenyi itabha na musingi, omugela gwejile gwalabhao kwa managa, inyumba iliya nifuma ninyamuka bhunene.
Ejile Yesu amala bhuli chinu chinu aliga naika kubhanu bhanu bhaliga nibhamtegelesha, nengila Kapelenaumu.
Omugaya umwi owa akida, unu aliga ali wa chibhalo kumwene, aliga ali mwasibhwa muno na aliga nalebhelela okufwa.
Tali aliga onguhye ingulu ya Yesu, Akida oyo namulagilila omukulu wa bhayaudi, okumusabhwa aje amukishe omugaya wae ataja kufwa.
Bhejile bhakinga ayeyi na Yesu bhamulembelejishe muno nibhaikati,”jimwiile okukola kutyo ingulu yae,
Kulwokubha kalyenda liyanga lyeswe, na niwe ombakile elikofyanyisho ingulu yeswe.”
Yesu nagendelela no lugendo lwae amwi nabho. nawe achali kugenda kula na inyumba, omukulu umwi nabhatuma abhasani bhae okuloma nage.”Latabhugenyi, utenyasha omwene kulwokubha anye niteile awe okuja ewani.
Kulwokubha sanga niteganilisishe anye ela omwene jitanyiile okuja kwawe, nawe yaika omusango ela omugaya wani keulila.
Anyona ni munu unu nitulilweko na ninobhuinga na nina abhasilikale emwalo yani. Enaika kuunu “Genda”na kagenda, na kuundi,“Ija”ona naja, na kumukosi wani 'Kola chinu,'no mwene kakola”
Yesu ejile ongwa ago nalugula, nabhaindukila elikofyanya bhanu bhaliga nibhamulubha naikati.”Enibhabhwila ati, ata Muisilaeli nichali kubhona omunu welikilisha kama linu.
Mbeya bhanu bhaliga bhatumilwe nibhasubha ika nibhamusanga omukosi ali muanga.
Gwejile gwalabhao omwanya, yabhonekene ati Yesu aliga nalibhata okuja mumusi gunu gwatogwaga Naini. Abheigisibwa bhae nibhagenda amwi nage nibhalubhanaga na bhanu bhamfu.
Ejile akalebhelela no bhwingililo bho musi lola, omunu unu aliga afuye aliga abhatuhye, na nimwana wa agali ku nyila mwene. unu aliga afwiliwe no mulume, bhanu bhamfu bho kusoka mumusi bhaliga bhali amwi nage,
Ejile amulola, Latabhugenyi namufogelela kwe chigongo chinene muno ingulu yae namubhwila ati,”siga kulila.”
Neya nelila imbele nalikunyako lisandikwa linu lyaliga lilimo omubhili gwo mufuye, nabhanu bhaliga bhabhatuye nibhemelegulu naikati,”Musigaji naikati imuka”
Omufuye nemuka nenyanja ansi namba okuloma. Neya Yesu namusubhya kunyilamwene.
Nibhabha no bhubha bhona. nibhagendelela okumukusha Nyamuanga nibhaikati “Omulagi omukulu emusibhwa okusoka mwishwe” na “Nyamuanga abhalola abhanu bhae”
Ne misango jo bhwana eja Yesu nijiswila Yudeya yona na kwemikoa jinu jaliga jiliayeyi.
Abheigisibhwa bha Yowana nibhaamubhwila emisango ejo jona.
Nio Yowana nabhabhilikila abhabhilil okusoka mubheigisibhwa bhae nabhalagilila ku Latabhugenyi okwaikati “Awe nawe unu kaja, tali alio oundi chimulindilile? Bhejile bhakinga ayeyi na Yesu bhnu nibhaikati,”Yowana omubhatija achilagilila kwawe naikati,'Awe nawe unu kaja
angu alio oundi chimutegelele?”
Kumwanya ogwo abheulisishe bhamfu okusoka mumalwala na munyako, okusoka kumasabwa amabhibhi, na kubhanu bhaliga bhatakulola abhayanile okulola.
Yesu nasubhya kubhenene naikati. Mukamala okugenda enu musokele mulamumenyesha Yowana chinu mwalola no kungwa. Abhaofu abhabhona okulolalindi, abhalema abhalibhata, abhebhigenge abhaosibhwa, na bhasibhe bha matwi abhongwa, abhafuye abhasululwa nibhabha bhaanga lindi, abhataka abhabhwilwa emisango jo bhwana.
No munu unu atakunyikilisha ku lwe bhikolwa bhyani ana libhando”
Abhanu bhaliga bhatumilwe na Yowana bhejile osubhayo enu bhaliga bhasokele, Yesu namba okwaika na amekofyanyisho ingulu ya Yowana,”Mwajiye anja okulola ki, lisekeyanda nilisingisibhwa no muyaga?
Tali mwagendele kulolaki, omunu unu aliga afwae kisi? lola abhanu bhaliya bhanu abhafwala ebhifwalo bhye chikama no kwikala obhulame bhwo lumula bhali kumwanya gwe chikama.
Nawe omuja anja okulola ki, Omulagi? Chimali, enaika nemwe muno okukila omulagi.
Unu niwe andikiwe,”Lola anye enituma intumwa yani imbele ya meso gemwe, unu kachuma injila yani,
Enaika kwemwe ati, amwi ya bhanu bhebhuhye no mugasi, atalio unu ali mukulu kama Yowana, nawe omunu unu atali wa bhusibhusi unu kaja okwikala na Nyamuanga anu ali omwene, kabha mukulu okukila Yowana.”
Abhanu bhona bhejile bhongwa ago amwi na bhatobhesha bho bhushulu, nibhalasha ati Nyamuanga ni mulengelesi. Bhaliga bhalio bhanu bhaliga bhabhatijiswe no bhubhatijwa bhwa Yowana.
Nawe amafalisayo nabhabhuya bha jishelia je chiyaudi, bhanu bhaliga bhatabhatijiswe nage nibhalema obhulengelesi bhwa Nyamuanga kwo kwenda kwebhwe.
Enitula okubhasusanisha naki abhanu bho lwibhulo lwa woli? Bhali kutiki?
Abhasusana na bhana bhanu bhenyaga kulubhala lwa lisoko, bhanu bhenyanjile no kubhilikilana oumwi no oundi nibhaikati,'Chabhuma ifilimbi ingulu yemwe, na mutabhina. chalila mutalila.'
Yowana omubhatija ejile atalyaga mukate na atanywaga divayi, na nimwaika “Ana lisabwa.
Omwana wo Munu ejile nalya no kunywa na nimwaikati,”Mulole ni mwifi na nimutamiji, ni musani wa abhatobhesha bho bhushulu na abhebhibhi!
Nawe obhwengeso bhumenyekene ku bhalengelesi ku bhana bhae bhona.”
Oumwi wa mafalisayo amusabhwile Yesu agende okulya amwi nage. Ejile Yesu engila munyumba ya falisayo, eekekele ku meja koleleki alye.
Lola aliga alio mugasi umwi mumusi omwo unu aliga ali nebhibhibhi. Nechukati aliga ekae ewa Falisayo, naleta inchupa ya mafuta amalange.
Nemelegulu inyuma yae ayeyi na magulu gae enu nalila. Lindi namba okugelelesha amasiga kumagulu gae, nokukubhula kwa jimfwili ja kumutwe gwae, nanyunya amagulu gae nogasin
Na falisayo uliya aliga amukalibhisishe Yesu ejile alola kutiyo, neganilisha omwene naikati, “Labha omunu unu akabhee ali mulagi, akamenyele ati unu niga na nimugasi wa lususoki unu kamukunyako, kutyo ali we bhibhibhi.
Yesu nasubhya naikati,”Simoni nina echinu cho kukubhwila. “Naikati” Chaikela mwiigisha!”
Yesu naikati “Bhaliga bhalio bhatongwa bhabhili bhanu bhaliga nibhatogwa no munu umwi. Oumwi aliga tatongwa dinali magana gatanu no wa kabhili aliga natogwa dinali amusini.
Anu bhailiga bhatana cha kulipa nabhasasila bhona. Woli niga unu kamwenda muno?
Simoni namusubhya naikati,”Eniganilishati unu asasiwe ebhanja enene. “Yesu namubhila ati, “Walamula kwo bhwengeso.”
poopYesu naindukila omugasi naika kusimoni ati, “Oumulola omugasi unu. Nengila munyumba yao. Utanana manji ingulu ya magulu gani, nawe unu, kwa masiga gae, ajajishe amagulu gani nogakubhula kwa jimfwili jae.
Utanyunya, nawe omwene, ningiye munu achali kusiga kunyunya amagulu gani.
Utambambaga amagulu gani kwa mafuta, nawe agabhambagile amagulu gani kwa mafuta amalange.
Ku lwo musango gunu, enikubhwilati aliga ali nebhibhibhi bhyamfu eswalililwa bhyona, na lindi endele muno. Nawe unu keswalililwa katilu, kenda katilwila.”
Neya namubhwila omugasi,”Ebhibhibhi bhyao bhyeswalililwa.”
Bhanu bhaliga bhenyanjile amwi nage ku meja nibhamba okuloma abhene kwa bhene, “Unu niga okukinga okwiswalilila ebhibhibhi?
Na Yesu namubhila omugasi, “Elikilisha lyawo lyakukisha. Nugende kwo mulembe”
Gwejile gwalabhao mwanya mufuyi Yesu namba okugenda mumisi emitoto ne misi minene, nasimula no kulasha emisango jo bhwana jo bhukama bhwa Nyamuanga na bhaliya ekumi na bhabhili bhagendaga amwi nage.
kutyo kutyo bhagasi bhalebhe bhanu bhaliga bhaosibhwe okusoka ku masambwa amabhibhi na malwae gabhuli mbaga. Aliga ali Maliyamu unu atogwaga Magedalena unu aliga asosibhweko amasabwa saba.
Yowana omugasi wa Kuza na omukulu wa Helode, Susana, na bhagasi abhandibhamfu, bhanu bhasosishe ebhinu bhyebhwe kwainjuno yebhwe abhene.
Bhejile abhanu bhamfu bhakekumanya amwi, bhalimo na bhanu bhajaga kumwene okusoka mumisi jabhuli mbaga, alomele nabho kwebhijejekanyo.
Omuyambi agendele okubhibha jimbibho, anu aliga nayamba, jimbibho ejindi nijigwa kumbali ya injila nijilibhatwa emwalo ya magulu, na jinyonyi ja mulutumba nijijilya.
Jimbibho ejindi nijigwa ingulu ya mayalu ganu gali kulutale na jejile jamela nijamba ofuka nijiotoka kulwokubha aliga gutalio munyililo.
Jimbibho ejindi nijigwa mumati na mumawa, amati ago agamawa nigakula amwi na jimbibho ejo niga jinyiga.
Nawe jimbibho ejindi jaguye mumayalu ga kisi nijibhula amatwasho kukila egana.”Yesu ejile amala okwaika amagambo ago, alomele kwo bhulaka bhunene naikati,”Wona wona unu ali na matwi no gwe.”
Lindi abheigisibhwa bhae nibhamubhusha ingulu ye chijejekanyo echo,
Yesu nabhabhila ati,”Muyanibhwe okumenya imbisike yo bhukama bhwa Nyamuanga, tali abhanu abhandi abheeigisibhwa ku lwebhijejekanyo ela, koleleki bhakalola bhatajakulola na bhakongwa bhatajakusombokelwa.'
Na inu niyo insonga ye chijejekanyo chinu. Imbibhoni nigambo lya Nyamuanga.
Jimbibho jinu jaguye ayeyi na kunjila nibho bhanu bhanu abhongwa omusango, omusoko shetani nalisoshamo mumioyo jebhwe, koleleki bhasige okwikilisha nokuchungulwa.
Jinu jaguye kulutale ni bhanu bhanu abhongwa omusango nokugulamila kwo kusandabha nawe bhatali na misi jonajona, abhekilisha kwo mwanya mufuyi, no mwanya gwokulegejibhwa nibhagwa.
Na jimbibho jinu jaguye mumawa ni bhanu bhanu abhongwa omusango, nawe bhakagendelela okukula nibhaingililwa nokufulubhendela obhunibhi no bhukonde bhwo bhulame na bhatakwibhula matwasho.
Nawe jimbibho jinu jaguye mumayalu gakisi nibhanu bhanu, bhali nobhikeyi ne mioyo jakisi, bhakongwa omusango abhaligwatilila na abhebhula amatwasho go kwikomesha.
Woli anu, atalio nolo umwi, unu kakongesha itala naifundikila naimbakuli au naita mubhutalaasi. Nalema okuita kungango koleleki bhuli unu kengila abhone okuilola.
Kulwokubha chitalio chinu chiliseleka nichilema okumenyekana, au chonachona chinu chili cha mumbisike chinu chitali bhonekana kubwelu.
Kulwejo nubhe mwengeso anu ulabhaga nutegelesha. Kulwokubha unu ali nacho, kongesibhwa lindi, nawe unu atanacho nolo kanu alinako akatilu kona akagegibhwa.”
Eile nyilamwene Yesu na bhamula bhabho nibhaja kumwene bhatamulebhelee kulwokubha lyaliga lilio eijo enene lya bhanu.
Nibhamubhwila,”Nyokomwana na bhamula bhanyu bhalianja abhakwenda.
Nawe Yesu, nabhasubhya naikati,”Mayi wani na bhamula bhasu ni bhanu abhongwa omusango gwa Nyamuanga no kugwimako.”
Munaku ejo Yesu na bheigisibhwa bhae nibhalinya mubhwato, nabhabhwila ati, “Chambuke chigende ku ngego ya kabhili yo mwalo.” Nibhachumachuma obhwato bhwebhwe.
Nawe bhejile bhamba okwimuka, Yesu namama naongela, nomuyaga mwamfu ogwe chiule, obhwato bhwebhwe nibhwijula amanji bhaliga bhali munyanko nene muno.
Bheile abheigisibhwa bhae nibhamwimusha, nibhaikati,”Latabhugenyi mkulu! Latabhugenyi mkulu! chiliayeyi okufwa!”Nemuka nagonya omuyaga na makonjo ga manji nigafungama na ndibha etole.
Lindi nabhabhwila ati,”Elikilisha lyemwe liliaki?”Nibhobhaya, Nibhatanga'ngala, nibhaikana bhuli munu no wejabho,”Unu niga, unu kagonya omuyaga na manji nigafung'ama?”
Nibhakinga mumusi gwa Gelasini inu ili inyuma yo musi gwa Galilaya.
Yesu ejile atuka nataja kuchalo, omunu umwi okusoka mujini, nabhugangana nage, no munu unu aliga ali na masabhwa. kwo mwanya mulela aliga atakufwala ngubho, na aliga atakwikala munyumba, tali aliga nekala enu bhasikaga abhafuye.
Ejile amulola Yesu nalila kwo bhulaka, nagwa ansi imbele yae. kwo bhulaka bhunene naikati, Nakoleleki anye kwawe, Yesu omwana wa Nyamuanga unu ali ingulu? Enikulembeleja, utaja kunyasha anye”
Yesu nalagilila amasabwa ago amabhibhi gamusokeko omunu oyo, kulwokubha mwanya mwamfu aliga asalile. Nolwo kutyo aliga abhoelwe ne minyololo no kutulwa ansi yo bhangalisi, abhutulaga nokulibhasibhwa okukinga mwibhala.
Yesu namubhusha ati,”Lisina lyao nawega?”nasubhya naikati,“Legioni”Kulwokubha amasabwa mamfu gengiye kumwene.
Njigendelela okumulembeleja utachilagilila okuja mulyobho.
Liijo lya jingulubhe lyaliga ndilebhwa ingulu ya libhanga, nibhamulembeleja abhabhile bhengile mu ngulubhe. Nabhekilisisha bhakole kutyo.
Kulwejo amasabwa ago nigamusokako omunu oyo nigengila mungulubhe, na liijo nilibhilimila kuchima nibhagwilila mumanji nibhafwila omwo.
Abhanu bhanu bhaliga nibhalebha jingulubhe ejo bhejile bhalola chinu chabhao, nibhabhilima na nibhajaokwaika mumusi na mumisi jinu jaliga jibheindileko.
Abhanu bhejile bhakongwa ago nibhaja okulola jinu jabhonekana, na nibhaja ku Yesu nibhamulola omunu amasabhwa galiga gamusokeleko. aliga afwae kisi na ali no bhwenge bhwa kisi, enyanjile kumagulu ga Yesu, nibhobhaya.
Niwo oumwi webhwe unu alolele chinu chabhonekene namba okubhabhwila abhandi kutyo omunu oyo unu aliga natangasibhwa na masabhwa kutyo eulisibhwa.
Abhanu bhona abhomukowa gwa Wagelasi na bhanu bhaliga bhasijene nibhamusabhwa Yesu abhasokeko kulwokubha bhaliga bhali no bhubha bhamfu. Nengila mubhwato nasubhayo.
Omunu unu asosibhweko emisabhwa namulembeleja Yesu agende nage, nawe Yesu namubhwila agende no kwaikati,
“Subha mumusi gwao na ubhale gona ganu Nyamuanga akukolela”. Omunu oyo nagenda, nalasha mumusi gwona ganu Yesu amukolela omwene,
Yesu nasubha, abhanu bhamfu nibhamulamila, kulwokubha bhona bhaliga bhamutegelee.
Lola naja munu umwi unu atogwaga Yailo ni umwi wa bhatangasha mulikofyanyisho. Yailo nagwa mumagulu ga Yesu namwilembeleja agende ika ewae.
Kulwokubha aliga ali no mwana muyala umwila, unu aliga ali ne miyaka kumi ne bhili, ali mumwanya gwo kufwa. Anu aliga nagenda, bhanu bhamfu nibhamuiganya omwene.
Omugasi unu aululaga insagama kwe miyaka ekumi ne bhili aliga alio awo amalile jiela jae kubhafumu, nawe atalio na umwi unu aliga amuosishe.
Naja inyuma ya Yesu nakunyako kwipindo lyo mwenda gwae, aonao okusoka insagama kwae nikutemekela.
Yesu naikati, Niga unu ankunyako?”Bhejile bhalema bhona, Petelo naikati, Latabhugenyi, abhanu ni bhamfu munu bhanu abhakukula no kukuiganya.”
Nawe Yesu naikati,”Omunu umwi ankunyako, okubha namenya amanaga gansokamo.”
Omugasi ejile alolati atakutula kuseleka chinu akola, namba okuyalala, nagwa ansi imbele ya Yesu nabhwila abhanu bhona chinu chakola amukunyeko na kutyo eulisibhwa aonao.
Neya naika nage ati,”Muyala, elikilisha lyao lyakola ubhe muanga. Genda no mulembe.”
Mbe anu aliga achaika, omunu umwi naja okusoka munyumba yo mutangasha we likofyanyisho, naikati,”Omuyansha wao afuye. Siga okumunyasha omwiigisha.”
Nawe Yesu ejile ongwa kutyo, namusubhya naikati,”Utaja kubhaya. Ikilishala, nakakila.”
Mbe bhejile bhengila munyumba eyo, atekilisishe munu undi okwingila nage, tali Petelo, Yowana na Yakobho, esemwene omwana na nyila mwene.
Ao abhanu bhona bhaliga nibhalila kwo bhulaka, nawe naikati,”Musige okusekana, achali kufwa, nawe amamilela.”.
Nawe nibhamuseka kwo kumugaya, okubha bhaliga bhamenyele ati afuye.
Nawe omwene, namugwata omuyala okubhoko, nabhilikila kwo bhulaka, naika ati,”Mwana imuka”
Omwoyo gwae nigusubhamo, nemuka omwanya ogwo ogwo, Nabhalagilila ati, ayabhwe echinu cho kulya abhone okulya.
Abhebhusi bhae nibhalugula, nawe nabhabhwila bhasiga kubhwila munu kutyo jabha.
Nabhabhilikila amwi abheigisibhwa bhaye ekumi na bhahili, nabhayana obhutulo no bhuinga ingulu ya amasambwa gona nokuosha amalwaye.
Nabhatuma wagende okulasha obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga nokuosha abhalwaye.
Nabhabhwila ati, “mwasiga okugega chonachona mulugendolwemwe nolwo insimbo, nolwo omufuko, nolwo omukate, nolwo jimpilya, mwasiga nolwo okugega jinkanju ebhili.
Omusi gwonagwona gunu mwakengilemo, mwikalao kukingila mwakasokeo ao.
Bhanu bhatalibhalamila, mkasokamo mumusi ogwo, mukunkumule oluteli okusoka kumagulu gemwe mukole kutyo ingulu yo obhubhambasi bhwemwe ingulu yebhwe.”
Nibhasokao nibhagenda okulabha mubhijiji, nibhalashaga omusango gwekisi nokuosha abhanu bhuli lubhala
Mbe omukama Herode aliga nongwa ganu galiga nigakolekana nanyasibhwa muno, kulwokubha abhandi bhaikaga ati Yoana Omubhatija asurukile okusoka mubhafuye,
abhandi ati Elia ejile, na abhandi ati oumwi mubhalagi bha kala asurukile lindi okusoka mubhafu.
Herode naika ati, “nachinjile Yoana, Nawe si niga unu enungwa amagambo gaye? Mbe Yoana nalondaga injila eyokumulola Yesu.
Bhejile bhasubha bhanu bhaliga bhatumilwe, nibhamubhwila bhuli chinu echo bakolele. Nabhagega bhona, nibhagenda mumusi gunu gwatogwaga Betisaida.
Nawe liijo nilyungwa ati asokao nibhamulubha, nabhakumilila, na naloma nabho ingulu yo obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga, naosha bhanu bhaliga nibhakena okuosibhwa.
Lisubha niliwako, na Jintumwa ekumi ne bhili nibhamujako nibhamubhwila ati, “Nyalambula liijo bhagende mubhijiji bhyayei na mumusi bhaje okufung'ama nokulonda ebhilyo, kulwokubha anu chili ni chalo cha ibala.”
Nawe nabhabhwila ati, “Mubhayane ebhilyo bhalye.” Nibhaika ati, “Chitali nabhyo tali bhilio bhibhala bhitanu ebhye mikate na nswi ebhili, nawe chakajiye okugula ebhilyo bhyaliijo lya abhanu bhanu.”
Mbe bhaliga bhalio ao abhalume bhiumbi bhitanu. Nabhwila abheigisibhwa bhaye, “mubheyanje ansi mkole jingobho ja bhanu makumi gatanu tanu.”
Kulwejo nibhakola kutyo, abhanu nibheyanja ansi.
Mbe nagega emikate etanu na jinswi ebhili nalola ingulu, nasima, najibhutulanya bhibhala, nabhayana abheigisibhwa bhaye koleleki bhaligabhile liijo.
Nibhalya bhona nibheguta, nibhakofya ebhibhala bhyo obhusigala nibhejusha ebhibho ekumi na bhibhili.
Mbe nijibha kutiya, Yesu aliga nasabha ebhisile ali na abheigisibhwa bhaye, nabhabhusha naika ati, “abhanu abhaika ati anye nanyega?”
Nibhasubhya, nibhaika ati, “Yoana Omubhatija, Nawe abhandi abhaika ni Eliya, abhandi abhaika ni umwi was abhalagi we emyaka ja kala amasubha okusuruka.”
Nabhabhwila ati, “Nawe emwe omwaika ati nanye uya?” Petro nasubhya naika ati,
“Nawe Kristo okusoka ku Nyamuanga.” Nawe Yesu nabhaonya, nabhelesha ati bhasiga kubhwila munu wonawona ingulu yo omusango ogwo.
Naika kutya, “Omwana wa Adamu ni bhusibhusi anyale na amagambo mafu nokubhulwa okwendwa na bhakaruka na abhagabhisi abhakulu na abhandiki, na abhamwita, na kasuruka olunaku lwa akasatu”
Nabhabhwila ati, “Omunu wonawona akenda okundubha, ni bhusibhusi eleme omwene, ayeke omusalabha gwaye bhuli siku, andubhe.
Wonawona unu kalegeja okuchungula obhulame bhwaye alibhubhusha, Nawe unu kabhusha obhulame kulwa injuno ya libhona lyani, alibhuchungula.
Omwana munu alibhona chinuki, alibha akabhona echalo chona, Nawe akabhusha amo akabhona i-asara yo mwoyo gwaye?
Wonawona unu alinyiswalilila any ne emisango jani, Omwana was Adamu ao alibha mwikusho lyaye alimwiswalilila omunuyo na likusho lya Lata na bhamalaika abhatakatifu(abhelu).
Nawe enibhabhwila echimali, bhalio abhandi bhemeleguyu anu bhataliloja lufu okukinga bhabhulole obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga.”
Jejile jalabhao nsiku munana amalile okwaika emisango ejo, nagega Petro, Yoana na Yakobo. Nibhalinya muchima okusabhwa.
Nao aliga achali mwisabhwa, olususo lwo ubhusu bhwaye niluinduka, na jingubho jaye nijibha jimwela no okubhalangilya.
Lola, bhaliga bhalio bhalume bhabhili nibhalomaga nage! Aliga ali Musa na Eliya,
bhabhonekene bhali mwikusho. Ni bhalomelela ingulu yo okusokao kwaye, omusango gunu aliga alebhelee okukumisha ali Yerusalemu.
Petro na abhejabho bhaliga bhaongee muno. Nawe bhejile bhasisimuka, nibhalola likusho laye na bhalume bhabhili bhanu bhaliga bhemeleguyu nage.
Bhejile bhasigana na Yesu, Petro namubhwila ati, “Lata Bhugenyi, jakabhee jakisi eswe chikale anu na jichiile chumbake anu jinyumba ja bhanu bhasatu. Chumbake eyao imwi, eindi ili ya Musa, na eindi ili ya Eliya.” Nawe aikaga emisango ejo ohhutamenya.
Ao aliga achaika kutyo, nilija elile nilibhafundikila; nibhobhaya kulwokubha bhaliga bhajongewe ne elile.
Obhulaka nibhusoka mulile nibhwaika ati, “Unu niwe Omwana wani Omusolwa. Mbe nimumutegeleshe.
“Obhulaka bhwejile bhwajibhila, Yesu nasigala enyele. Nibhajibhila, na munsiku ejo bhatabhwiliye munu wonawona kumisango jonajona jinu bhalolele.
Bwire bhucheye, bhejile bhasoka muchima, liijo lya abhanu nilibhugangana nage.
Lola, omumula umwi okusoka mwiijo nalila kwo bhulaka, naika ati, “Mwiigisha enikusabhwa undolele omwana wani kubha niwe nilinagela enyele.
Mbe oulola kagwatibhwa amasambwa, nayogana, lugendo agamuyana okugwa lilaru nokusoka lifilo mukanwa. Agamutatila kwa inyako, nigamusigila obhwashe bhusito.
Nilabhasabhileko abheigisibhwa bhao bhagagonye Nawe bhatatulile.”
Yesu nasubhya naika ati, “Emwe olwibhulo lunu lutakwikilisha na lunu lutasikene ne echimali, enikala nemwe nokubhagegela ganu agabhatama okukingila katunguki? Nufogeshe omwana wao anu.”
Nolwo akatungu kanu omusigaji oyo aliga naja lisambwa nilimugwisha ansi kwo okumunyongotola. Nawe Yesu naligonya lisambwa elyo, namwiulisha namusubhisha esemwene
Abhanu bhona nibhalugula obhukulu bhwaye Nyamuanga. Nawe ao bhaliga bhachalugula gona ago Yesu akolele, nabhwila abheigisibhwa bhaye ati,
“Mutule mukutwi emisango jinu enenda obhabhwila olyanu: Omwana wo Omunu kaja okutulwa mumabhoko ga abhanu.”
Nawe bhatasombokewe insonga ye misango ejo, gaselekelwe mumeso gebhwe, koleleki bhasiga okugasombokelwa.
Mbe okubhula okungwana nikwibhuka agati yebhwe ingulu yobhukulu, ati niga unu kajokubha mukulu okukila bhona.
Nawe Yesu ejile amenya chinu bhaliga nibhabhushanya, nagega Omwana mulela, namwimelegushu mulubhafu lwaye.
Mbe nio nabhabhwila ati, “Wonawona unu kakumilila omwana omulela lwa unu kwisina lyani, kabha andamiye anye ona; na unu kankumilila any kabha akumiliye unu antumile anye. Kulwokubha unu ali mtoto agati yemwe bhona oyo niwe omukulu kukila bhona.”
Yoana nasubhya naika ati, “Mukama, chalolele omunu nagonya amasambwa mwisina lyao nichimujibhila kulwokubha atakulibhata amwi neswe.”
Nawe Yesu nabhabhwila ati, “Musige okumujibhila, kulwokubha unu atatasikene nemwe niwejanyu.”
Jinsiku jejile jafogela ayei ejo omwene okugegwa okuja mulwire, nalolelela okuja Yerusalemu.
Natuma abhanu bhelabhe imbele yaye, mbe nibhagenda nibhengila muchijiji cha Abhasamaria koleleki bhamwilabhile obhwiyanjo.
Nawe abhanu bhendeyo bhatamulamiye, kulwokubha aliga nalolelela okuja Yerusalemu.
Abheigisibhwa bhaye, Yakobo na Yoana bhejile bhalola elyokutyo, nibhaika ati, “Lata Bugenyi owenda chilagilishe omulilo gutuke ansi okusoka mulwire gubhasingalishe?”
Nawe nabhekebhukila nokubhaganya.
Nibhamala nibhagenda muchijiji echindi.
Ao bhaliga bhali munjila yebhwe nibhagenda, omunu umwi namubhwila ati, “Enikulubhilila onaona eyo ouja.”
Yesu namubhwila ati, “jinyamubhwe jina amobho, jinyonyi ja mulutumba jina amasuli, nawe Omwana wa Adamu atana wa wakumamya omutwe gwaye.”
Achalao nabhwila omunu undi ati, “Niundubhe.” Nawe omwenene naika ati, “Lata Bhugenyi, nunane omwanya okwamba nigende nijosika lata.”
Nawe Yesu namubhwila ati, “Nusige abhafuye bhasike abhafu bhabho, nawe awe nugende ulashe obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga bhuli mbala.”
Omunu undi ona naika ati, “Enikulubhilila, Mukama, nawe nana omwanya okwamba nilage abha ika owani.”
Nawe Yesu namubhwila ati, “atalio unu katao okubhoko kwaye alime namala nalola inyuma oyo ateile mubhukama bhwa Nyamuanga.”
Gejile galabhao amagambo ago, Lata Bhugenyi nasola ebheigisibhwa abhandi makumi musanju, nabhatuma bhabhili bhili bhelabhe okukinga bhuli musi na bhuli chalo echo aliga neikanya okujamo.
Nabhabhwila ati, “ebhyokugeswa ni bhafu, nawe abhakosi bhemilimu ni bhatoto. Mbe kulwejo musabhe Omukama wa wobhugesi koleleki atume bhwangu abhakosi bhemilimu mulugeso lwaye.
Mugende mumisi. Mbe mwimenye, nabhatuma lwa jinama agati ye emisege ja ibara.
Mwasiga okugega omufuko gwa jiela, nolwo emikoba eja bhanu abhaja lugendo, nolwo bhilato, mwasiga nokukesha wonawona munjila.
Mukengila munyumba yonayona, echokwamba mwaike kutya, 'Omulembe gubhemo munyumba munu.'
Akasanga alimo omunu womulembe munyumba eyo, omulembe gweme ogusigala ingulu yaye, nawe akasanga atalimo, omulembe ogusubha kwimwe.
Mwikale munyumba eyo, mulye no kunywa bhihu abhabhaletela, kulwokubha omukosi we emilimu kabhonaga omuyelo. Mwasiga okufuruka mukaja nyumba indi.
Mukengila mumusi na bhakabhalamila, mulye chonachona chinu abhaleta imbele yemwe.
Muoshe abhalwaye bhanu bhali mumusi ogwo. Mubhabhwile ati, 'Obhukama bhwa mulwire bhwafogee ayeyi nemwe.'
Nawe mumusi gwona gwona gunu mwakengilemo bhasige okubhalamila, musokemo muje anja kunjila nimwaika ati,
'Nolwo oluteli lo omusi gunu lunu lugwatiliye kumaguru geswe chalukubhula lubhe ingulu yemwe! Nawe mulagumenya gunu, Obhukama bhwa Nyamuanga bhwafogee yeyi.'
Enibhabhwila kutiya olunaku lwa indamu lulibha lwokwikomesha muno ku Sodoma kusiga omusi ogwo.
Kolazini jakubhona, Betisaida jakubhona! Ka labha emilimu mikulu jinu jakolekana ewao chisanga jikolekene Tiro na Sidoni, bhakasigile ebhibhi bhwangu muno, bhakafwaye jingubho jamagunila na lifu.
Nawe kulibhao okwikomesha muno ku musi gwa Tiro na Sidoni kulunaku olwa indamu kusiga emwe.
Awe Kaperanaumu, owiganilishati bhalikutula ingulu okukinga mulwire? Pai, outelembushwa emwalo okukinga nyombe.
Oyo alibhategelesha emwe kantegelesha anye, na wonawona unu alibhalema emwe kalema anye, na wonawona oyo kandema anye kalema unu antumile anye.”
Bhaliya makumi musanju bhasubhile kwobhukondelelwa muno, nibhaika ati, “Mukama nolwo amasambwa ona agachungwa mwisina lyao.”
Yesu nabhabhwila ati, Nalolele shetani nagw aokusoka mulwire lwo olukubha.
Mbe mulole, nabhayana obhuyinga bhwo kutaja jinjoka na jinge, na amanaga gonna agomusoko, na chitalio chona chona na kwa njila yonaona chinu chilibhanyamula.
Nolwo kutiyo mwasiga kukondelewa kwo omusango gumwi ila gunu, nawe mukondelelwe muno kulwokwandikwa kwanamasina gemwe mulwire.”
Omwanya ogwo, nakondelelwa muno mu Mwoyo Mwelu, naika ati, “Enikukuya awe, Lata, Omukama wo olwire ne echalo, kulwokubha waselekele emisango jinu kubhanu bhobhwengeso no obhwenge, nugasulula kubhanu bhateigisibhwe, lwa abhana abhalela. Nikwo kutyo, Lata, kulwokubha jakukondeye mumeso gao.”
“Bhuli chinu niyabhilwe na Lata wani, na atalio unu kamenya ati Omwana niga, tali ni Lata, na atalio unu kamenya ati Lata niga, tali ni Omwana, na wonawona unu Omwana kekumbulila okwisulula kumwene.”
Nabhaindukila abheigisibhwa nabhabhwila bhali kasugumbaju, “Bhana libhando bhanu abhalola ganu ago omulola emwe.
Enibhabhwila emwe kutya, abhalagi bhafu na abhakama bhesigombelaga okulola ganu omulola, nawe bhatagabhwene no okungwa ganu omungwa.”
Mbe lola, omwiigisha umwi owebhilagilo ebhye Chiyaudi emeleguyu namusaka Yesu naika ati, “Mwiigisha, nikole chinuki koleleki nilye omwandu gwo bhuanga bhwa akajanende?”
Yesu namubhwila ati, “Jandikilwe kutiki mubhilagilo? Ousomaga kutiki?”
Namusubhya naika ati, “Yendaga Omukama Nyamuanga wao kwo moyo gwao gwona, kwomutima gwao gwona, kwa amanaga gao gona na kwo bhwenge bhwao bhwona na wende omwikashanya wao lwakutyo owienda awe omwene.”
Yesu naika ati, “Wasubhya kisi. Mbe nukole kutyo ouja okulama.”
Nawe omwiigisha nenda okwibhalila obhulengelesi omwenekili, namubhwila Yesu ati, “Ko mwikashanya wani niga?”
Yesu nasubhya naika ati, “Omunu umwi aliga nolomoka okusoka Yerusalemu najaga Yeriko. Mbe nagwa mumabhoko agabhasakusi, nibhamusakula ebhinu bhaye bhyona nibhamubhuma nokumusigao alikuti afuye.
Kutiki ebhando, omugabhisi umwi aliganolomoka kunjila eyo, ejile amulola netulila kumbali.
Omulawi ona nakola kutyo, ejile akakinga ao namulola, ona netulila kumbali.
Nawe omusamaria umwi unu aliga naja lugendo lwaye, nalabha ao aliga omuuta. Ejile amulola nasilwa nechigongo.
Namufogelako namusemba obhuuta bhwaye, namusiga amafuta na idivai kumubhili gwaye. Amulinyishe ingulu ya intyanyi yaye, namusila munyumba ya abhagenyi nokumulwasha.
Bwire bhucheye nagega jiyela dinari ebhili, nayana kanya nyumba ya abhagenyi namubhwila ati, 'Numulwashe na chona chona chinu chileyongesha echowakakolele, nakaje okukulia nakasubhe.'
Mbe ni uya mubhanu abho ukeganilisha, unu aliga ali mwikashanya wa unu agwiliye mumabhoko ga abhasakusi?”
Omwiigisha nasubhya ati, “Ni unu elesishe echigongo kumuuta.” Mbe Yesu namubhwila ati, “Genda aona ukole kutyo.”
Mbe ao bhaliga bhachagenda mulugendo, nibhakinga muchijiji chimwi, no omugasi umwi natogwa Marita namukumililanika ewaye.
Omugasi oyo aliga ali namuyala wabho natogwaga Mariamu, unu aliga eyanjile mumagulu go Omukama nokutegelesha omusango gwaye.
Nawe Marita nagega milimu myafu ejo kufulubhenda okuteka ebhilyo. Nagenda ku Yesu nokwaika ati, “Lata Bhugenyi, awe utakusasila oulola muyalawasu ansigila obhufulubhendi nenyele? Kulwejo numubhwile ansakile.”
Nawe Lata Bhugenyi namusubhya namubhwila ati, “Marita, Marita, ounyakilila magambo mafu,
nawe liliwo egambo limwi la elya insonga. Mariamu asola linu likondele, na litakuja kumusokako.”
Akatungu kamwi Yesu aliga nasabhwa, oumwi wa abheigisibhwa bhaye namubhwila ati, “Lata Bhugenyi nuchiigishe okusabhwa lwakutyo Yoana eigisishe abheigisibhwa bhaye.”
Yesu nabhabhwila, Mukabha nimusabhwa, mwaike, “Lata, Lisina lyao likusibhwe. Obhukama bhwa bhuje.
Uchiyane ebhilyo bhyeswe ebhya bhuli lunaku.
Uchisasile obhunyamuke bhweswe, lwakutyo eswe ona echisasila bhona bhanu abhachiyabhila. Waisiga okuchisindika chikaga mumasakwa.”
Yesu nabhabhwila ati, “Niga kwimwe oyo ali no omusani, namujako ingeta, namubhwila, 'musani nuunsakile emikate esatu.
